\input{intro}
\section*{Jeremiah (Parallel) — LXX order}
\ChapterHeading{1}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{1:1}{The word of God which came to Jeremias the son of Chelcias, of the priests, who dwelt in Anathoth in the land of Benjamin:}{1:1}{The words of Jeremiah the son of Hilkiah, one of the priests who were in Anathoth in the land of Benjamin.}
\VersePair{1:2}{accordingly as the word of God came to him in the days of Josias son of Amos king of Juda, in the thirteenth year of his reign.}{1:2}{Yahweh’s word came to him in the days of Josiah the son of Amon, king of Judah, in the thirteenth year of his reign. \footnote{1:2: “Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.}}
\VersePair{1:3}{And it was in the days of Joakim son of Josias king of Juda, until the eleventh year of Sedekias king of Juda, even until the captivity of Jerusalem in the fifth month.}{1:3}{It came also in the days of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, king of Judah, to the end of the eleventh year of Zedekiah, the son of Josiah, king of Judah, to the carrying away of Jerusalem captive in the fifth month.}
\VersePair{1:4}{And the word of the Lord came to him, saying,}{1:4}{Now Yahweh’s word came to me, saying,}
\VersePair{1:5}{Before I formed thee in the belly, I knew thee; and before thou camest forth from the womb, I sanctified thee; I appointed thee a prophet to the nations.}{1:5}{{\raggedright “Before I formed you in the womb, I knew you. \poemline{2}{Before you were born, I sanctified you.}\poemline{2}{I have appointed you a prophet to the nations.”}}}
\VersePair{1:6}{And I said, O Lord, thou that art supreme Lord, behold, I know not how to speak, for I am a child.}{1:6}{Then I said, “Ah, Lord Yahweh! Behold, I don’t know how to speak; for I am a child.” \footnote{1:6: The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”} \footnote{1:6: “Behold”, from “\texthebrew{הִנֵּה}”, means look at, take notice, observe, see, or gaze at. It is often used as an interjection.}}
\VersePair{1:7}{And the Lord said to me, Say not, I am a child: for thou shalt go to all to whomsoever I shall send thee, and according to all the words that I shall command thee, thou shalt speak.}{1:7}{But Yahweh said to me, “Don’t say, ‘I am a child;’ for you must go to whomever I send you, and you must say whatever I command you.}
\VersePair{1:8}{Be not afraid before them: for I am with thee to deliver thee, saith the Lord.}{1:8}{Don’t be afraid because of them, for I am with you to rescue you,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{1:9}{And the Lord stretched forth his hand to me, and touched my mouth: and the Lord said to me, Behold, I have put my words into thy mouth.}{1:9}{Then Yahweh stretched out his hand and touched my mouth. Then Yahweh said to me, “Behold, I have put my words in your mouth.}
\VersePair{1:10}{Behold, I have appointed thee this day over nations and over kingdoms, to root out, and to pull down, and to destroy, and to rebuild, and to plant.}{1:10}{Behold, I have today set you over the nations and over the kingdoms, to uproot and to tear down, to destroy and to overthrow, to build and to plant.”}
\VersePair{1:11}{And the word of the Lord came to me, saying, What seest thou? And I said, A rod of an almond tree.}{1:11}{Moreover Yahweh’s word came to me, saying, “Jeremiah, what do you see?” I said, “I see a branch of an almond tree.”}
\VersePair{1:12}{And the Lord said to me, Thou hast well seen: for I have watched over my words to perform them.}{1:12}{Then Yahweh said to me, “You have seen well; for I watch over my word to perform it.”}
\VersePair{1:13}{And the word of the Lord came to me a second time, saying, What seest thou? And I said, A caldron on the fire; and the face of it is toward the north.}{1:13}{Yahweh’s word came to me the second time, saying, “What do you see?” I said, “I see a boiling cauldron; and it is tipping away from the north.”}
\VersePair{1:14}{And the Lord said to me, From the north shall flame forth evils upon all the inhabitants of the land.}{1:14}{Then Yahweh said to me, “Out of the north, evil will break out on all the inhabitants of the land.}
\VersePair{1:15}{For, behold, I call together all the kingdoms of the earth from the north, saith the Lord; and they shall come, and shall set each one his throne at the entrance of the gates of Jerusalem, and against all the walls round about her, and against all the cities of Juda.}{1:15}{{\raggedright For behold, I will call all the families of the kingdoms of the north,” says Yahweh. \poemline{1}{“They will come, and they will each set his throne at the entrance of the gates of Jerusalem,}\poemline{2}{and against all its walls all around, and against all the cities of Judah.}}}
\VersePair{1:16}{And I will speak to them in judgment, concerning all their iniquity, forasmuch as they have forsaken me, and sacrificed to strange gods, and worshipped the works of their own hands.}{1:16}{{\raggedright I will utter my judgments against them concerning all their wickedness, \poemline{2}{in that they have forsaken me,}\poemline{2}{and have burned incense to other gods,}\poemline{2}{and worshiped the works of their own hands.}}}
\VersePair{1:17}{And do thou gird up thy loins, and stand up, and speak all the words that I shall command thee: be not afraid of their face, neither be thou alarmed before them; for I am with thee to deliver thee, saith the Lord.}{1:17}{“You therefore put your belt on your waist, arise, and say to them all that I command you. Don’t be dismayed at them, lest I dismay you before them.}
\VersePair{1:18}{Behold, I have made thee this day as a strong city, and as a brazen wall, strong against all the kings of Juda, and the princes thereof, and the people of the land.}{1:18}{For behold, I have made you today a fortified city, an iron pillar, and bronze walls against the whole land— against the kings of Judah, against its princes, against its priests, and against the people of the land.}
\VersePair{1:19}{And they shall fight against thee; but they shall by no means prevail against thee; because I am with thee, to deliver thee, saith the Lord.}{1:19}{They will fight against you, but they will not prevail against you; for I am with you ”, says Yahweh, “to rescue you.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{2}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{2:2}{And he said, Thus saith the Lord, I remember the kindness of thy youth, and the love of thine espousals, in following the Holy One of Israel, saith the Lord.}{2:1-2:2}{{\raggedright Yahweh’s word came to me, saying, “Go and proclaim in the ears of Jerusalem, saying, ‘Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“I remember for you the kindness of your youth,}\poemline{2}{your love as a bride,}\poemline{1}{how you went after me in the wilderness,}\poemline{2}{in a land that was not sown.}}}
\VersePair{2:3}{Israel was the holy people to the Lord, and the first-fruits of his increase: all that devoured him shall offend; evils shall come upon them, saith the Lord.}{2:3}{{\raggedright Israel was holiness to Yahweh, \poemline{2}{the first fruits of his increase.}\poemline{1}{All who devour him will be held guilty.}\poemline{2}{Evil will come on them,”’ says Yahweh.”}}}
\VersePair{2:4}{Hear the word of the Lord, O house of Jacob, and every family of the house of Israel.}{2:4}{Hear Yahweh’s word, O house of Jacob, and all the families of the house of Israel!}
\VersePair{2:5}{Thus saith the Lord, What trespass have your fathers found in me, that they have revolted far from me, and gone after vanities, and become vain?}{2:5}{{\raggedright Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“What unrighteousness have your fathers found in me,}\poemline{2}{that they have gone far from me,}\poemline{1}{and have walked after worthless vanity,}\poemline{2}{and have become worthless?}}}
\VersePair{2:6}{And they said not, Where is the Lord, who brought us up out of the land of Egypt, who guided us in the wilderness, in an untried and trackless land, in a land which no man at all went through, and no man dwelt there?}{2:6}{{\raggedright They didn’t say, ‘Where is Yahweh who brought us up out of the land of Egypt, \poemline{2}{who led us through the wilderness,}\poemline{2}{through a land of deserts and of pits,}\poemline{2}{through a land of drought and of the shadow of death,}\poemline{2}{through a land that no one passed through,}\poemline{2}{and where no man lived?’}}}
\VersePair{2:7}{And I brought you to Carmel, that ye should eat the fruits thereof, and the good thereof; and ye went in, and defiled my land, and made mine heritage an abomination.}{2:7}{{\raggedright I brought you into a plentiful land \poemline{2}{to eat its fruit and its goodness;}\poemline{1}{but when you entered, you defiled my land,}\poemline{2}{and made my heritage an abomination.}}}
\VersePair{2:8}{The priests said not, Where is the Lord? and they that held by the law knew me not: the shepherds also sinned against me, and the prophets prophesied by Baal, and went after that which profited not.}{2:8}{{\raggedright The priests didn’t say, ‘Where is Yahweh?’ \poemline{2}{and those who handle the law didn’t know me.}\poemline{1}{The rulers also transgressed against me,}\poemline{2}{and the prophets prophesied by Baal}\poemline{2}{and followed things that do not profit.}}}
\VersePair{2:9}{Therefore I will yet plead with you, and will plead with your children's children.}{2:9}{{\raggedright “Therefore I will yet contend with you,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“and I will contend with your children’s children.}}}
\VersePair{2:10}{For go to the isles of the Chettians, and see; and send to Kedar, and observe accurately, and see if such things have been done;}{2:10}{{\raggedright For pass over to the islands of Kittim, and see. \poemline{2}{Send to Kedar, and consider diligently,}\poemline{2}{and see if there has been such a thing.}}}
\VersePair{2:11}{if the nations will change their gods, though they are not gods: but my people have changed their glory, for that from which they shall not be profited.}{2:11}{{\raggedright Has a nation changed its gods, \poemline{2}{which really are no gods?}\poemline{2}{But my people have changed their glory for that which doesn’t profit.}}}
\VersePair{2:12}{The heaven is amazed at this, and is very exceedingly horror-struck, saith the Lord.}{2:12}{{\raggedright “Be astonished, you heavens, at this \poemline{2}{and be horribly afraid.}\poemline{2}{Be very desolate,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{2:13}{For my people has committed two faults, and evil ones: they have forsaken me, the fountain of water of life, and hewn out for themselves broken cisterns, which will not be able to hold water.}{2:13}{{\raggedright “For my people have committed two evils: \poemline{2}{they have forsaken me, the spring of living waters,}\poemline{2}{and cut out cisterns for themselves: broken cisterns that can’t hold water.}}}
\VersePair{2:14}{Is Israel a servant, or a home-born slave? why has he become a spoil?}{2:14}{{\raggedright Is Israel a slave? \poemline{2}{Is he born into slavery?}\poemline{2}{Why has he become a captive?}}}
\VersePair{2:15}{The lions roared upon him, and uttered their voice, which have made his land a wilderness: and his cities are broken down, that they should not be inhabited.}{2:15}{{\raggedright The young lions have roared at him and raised their voices. \poemline{2}{They have made his land waste.}\poemline{2}{His cities are burned up, without inhabitant.}}}
\VersePair{2:16}{Also the children of Memphis and Taphnas have known thee, and mocked thee.}{2:16}{The children also of Memphis and Tahpanhes have broken the crown of your head.}
\VersePair{2:17}{Has not thy forsaking me brought these things upon thee? saith the Lord thy God.}{2:17}{{\raggedright “Haven’t you brought this on yourself, \poemline{2}{in that you have forsaken Yahweh your God, when he led you by the way? \footnote{2:17: The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “\texthebrew{אֱלֹהִ֑ים}” (Elohim).}}}}
\VersePair{2:18}{And now what hast thou to do with the way of Egypt, to drink the water of Geon? and what hast thou to do with the way of the Assyrians, to drink the water of rivers?}{2:18}{{\raggedright Now what do you gain by going to Egypt, to drink the waters of the Shihor? \poemline{2}{Or why do you go on the way to Assyria, to drink the waters of the River? \footnote{2:18: i.e., the Euphrates River}}}}
\VersePair{2:19}{Thine apostasy shall correct thee, and thy wickedness shall reprove thee: know then, and see, that thy forsaking me has been bitter to thee, saith the Lord thy God; and I have taken no pleasure in thee, saith the Lord thy God.}{2:19}{{\raggedright “Your own wickedness will correct you, \poemline{2}{and your backsliding will rebuke you.}\poemline{1}{Know therefore and see that it is an evil and bitter thing,}\poemline{2}{that you have forsaken Yahweh your God,}\poemline{2}{and that my fear is not in you,” says the Lord, Yahweh of Armies.}}}
\VersePair{2:20}{For of old thou hast broken thy yoke, and plucked asunder thy bands; and thou hast said, I will not serve thee, but will go upon every high hill, and under every shady tree, there will I indulge in my fornication.}{2:20}{{\raggedright “For long ago I broke off your yoke, \poemline{2}{and burst your bonds.}\poemline{1}{You said, ‘I will not serve;’}\poemline{2}{for on every high hill and under every green tree you bowed yourself,}\poemline{2}{playing the prostitute.}}}
\VersePair{2:21}{Yet I planted thee a fruitful vine, entirely of the right sort: how art thou a strange vine turned to bitterness!}{2:21}{{\raggedright Yet I had planted you a noble vine, \poemline{2}{a pure and faithful seed.}\poemline{2}{How then have you turned into the degenerate branches of a foreign vine to me?}}}
\VersePair{2:22}{Though thou shouldest wash thyself with nitre, and multiply to thyself soap, still thou art stained by thine iniquities before me, saith the Lord.}{2:22}{{\raggedright For though you wash yourself with lye, \poemline{2}{and use much soap,}\poemline{2}{yet your iniquity is marked before me,” says the Lord Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{2:23}{How wilt thou say, I am not polluted, and have not gone after Baal? behold thy ways in the burial-ground, and know what thou hast done: her voice has howled in the evening:}{2:23}{{\raggedright “How can you say, ‘I am not defiled. \poemline{2}{I have not gone after the Baals ’?}\poemline{1}{See your way in the valley.}\poemline{2}{Know what you have done.}\poemline{1}{You are a swift dromedary traversing her ways,}}}
\VersePair{2:24}{she has extended her ways over the waters of the desert; she was hurried along by the lusts of her soul; she is given up to them, who will turn her back? none that seek her shall be weary; at the time of her humiliation they shall find her.}{2:24}{{\raggedright a wild donkey used to the wilderness, that sniffs the wind in her craving. \poemline{2}{When she is in heat, who can turn her away?}\poemline{2}{All those who seek her will not weary themselves. In her month, they will find her.}}}
\VersePair{2:25}{Withdraw thy foot from a rough way, and thy throat from thirst: but she said, I will strengthen myself: for she loved strangers, and went after them.}{2:25}{{\raggedright “Keep your feet from being bare, \poemline{2}{and your throat from thirst.}\poemline{1}{But you said, ‘It is in vain.}\poemline{2}{No, for I have loved strangers,}\poemline{2}{and I will go after them.’}}}
\VersePair{2:26}{As is the shame of a thief when he is caught, so shall the children of Israel be ashamed; they, and their kings, and their princes, and their priests, and their prophets.}{2:26}{{\raggedright As the thief is ashamed when he is found, \poemline{2}{so the house of Israel is ashamed —}\poemline{2}{they, their kings, their princes, their priests, and their prophets,}}}
\VersePair{2:27}{They said to a stock, Thou art my father; and to a stone, Thou hast begotten me: and they have turned their backs to me, and not their faces: yet in the time of their afflictions they will say, Arise, and save us.}{2:27}{{\raggedright who tell wood, ‘You are my father,’ \poemline{2}{and a stone, ‘You have given birth to me,’}\poemline{1}{for they have turned their back to me,}\poemline{2}{and not their face,}\poemline{2}{but in the time of their trouble they will say, ‘Arise, and save us!’}}}
\VersePair{2:28}{And where are thy gods, which thou madest for thyself? will they arise and save in the time of thine affliction? for according to the number of thy cities were thy gods, O Juda; and according to the number of the streets of Jerusalem they sacrificed to Baal.}{2:28}{{\raggedright “But where are your gods that you have made for yourselves? \poemline{2}{Let them arise, if they can save you in the time of your trouble,}\poemline{2}{for you have as many gods as you have towns, O Judah.}}}
\VersePair{2:29}{Wherefore do ye speak unto me? ye all have been ungodly, and ye all have transgressed against me, saith the Lord.}{2:29}{{\raggedright “Why will you contend with me? \poemline{2}{You all have transgressed against me,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{2:30}{In vain have I smitten your children; ye have not received correction: a sword has devoured your prophets as a destroying lion; yet ye feared not.}{2:30}{{\raggedright “I have struck your children in vain. \poemline{2}{They received no correction.}\poemline{1}{Your own sword has devoured your prophets,}\poemline{2}{like a destroying lion.}}}
\VersePair{2:31}{Hear ye the word of the Lord: thus saith the Lord, Have I been a wilderness or a dry land to Israel? wherefore has my people said, We will not be ruled over, and will not come to thee any more?}{2:31}{{\raggedright Generation, consider Yahweh’s word. \poemline{2}{Have I been a wilderness to Israel?}\poemline{2}{Or a land of thick darkness?}\poemline{1}{Why do my people say, ‘We have broken loose.}\poemline{2}{We will come to you no more ’?}}}
\VersePair{2:32}{Will a bride forget her ornaments, or a virgin her girdle? but my people has forgotten me days without number.}{2:32}{{\raggedright “Can a virgin forget her ornaments, \poemline{2}{or a bride her attire?}\poemline{2}{Yet my people have forgotten me for days without number.}}}
\VersePair{2:33}{What fair device wilt thou yet employ in thy ways, so as to seek love? it shall not be so; moreover thou hast done wickedly in corrupting thy ways;}{2:33}{{\raggedright How well you prepare your way to seek love! \poemline{2}{Therefore you have even taught the wicked women your ways.}}}
\VersePair{2:34}{and in thine hands has been found the blood of innocent souls; I have not found them in holes, but on every oak.}{2:34}{{\raggedright Also the blood of the souls of the innocent poor is found in your skirts. \poemline{2}{You didn’t find them breaking in,}\poemline{2}{but it is because of all these things.}}}
\VersePair{2:35}{Yet thou saidst, I am innocent: only let his wrath be turned away from me. Behold, I will plead with thee, whereas thou sayest, I have not sinned.}{2:35}{{\raggedright “Yet you said, ‘I am innocent. \poemline{2}{Surely his anger has turned away from me.’}\poemline{1}{“Behold, I will judge you,}\poemline{2}{because you say, ‘I have not sinned.’}}}
\VersePair{2:36}{For thou hast been so exceedingly contemptuous as to repeat thy ways; but thou shalt be ashamed of Egypt, as thou wast ashamed of Assur.}{2:36}{{\raggedright Why do you go about so much to change your ways? \poemline{2}{You will be ashamed of Egypt also,}\poemline{2}{as you were ashamed of Assyria.}}}
\VersePair{2:37}{For thou shalt go forth thence also with thine hands upon thine head; for the Lord has rejected thine hope, and thou shalt not prosper in it.}{2:37}{{\raggedright You will also leave that place with your hands on your head; \poemline{2}{for Yahweh has rejected those in whom you trust,}\poemline{2}{and you won’t prosper with them.}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{3}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{3:1}{If a man put away his wife, and she depart from him, and become another man's, shall she return to him any more at all? shall not that woman be utterly defiled? yet thou hast gone a-whoring with many shepherds, and hast returned to me, saith the Lord.}{3:1}{“They say, ‘If a man puts away his wife, and she goes from him, and becomes another man’s, should he return to her again?’ Wouldn’t that land be greatly polluted? But you have played the prostitute with many lovers; yet return again to me,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{3:2}{Lift up thine eyes to look straight forward, and see where thou hast not been utterly defiled. Thou hast sat for them by the wayside as a deserted crow, and hast defiled the land with thy fornications and thy wickedness.}{3:2}{“Lift up your eyes to the bare heights, and see! Where have you not been lain with? You have sat waiting for them by the road, as an Arabian in the wilderness. You have polluted the land with your prostitution and with your wickedness.}
\VersePair{3:3}{And thou didst retain many shepherds for a stumbling-block to thyself: thou hadst a whore's face, thou didst become shameless toward all.}{3:3}{Therefore the showers have been withheld and there has been no latter rain; yet you have had a prostitute’s forehead and you refused to be ashamed.}
\VersePair{3:4}{Hast thou not called me as it were a home, and the father and guide of thy virgin-time?}{3:4}{Will you not from this time cry to me, ‘My Father, you are the guide of my youth!’?}
\VersePair{3:5}{Will God's anger continue for ever, or be preserved to the end? Behold, thou hast spoken and done these bad things, and hadst power to do them.}{3:5}{“‘Will he retain his anger forever? Will he keep it to the end?’ Behold, you have spoken and have done evil things, and have had your way.”}
\VersePair{3:6}{And the Lord said to me in the days of Josias the king, Hast thou seen what things the house of Israel has done to me? they have gone on every high mountain, and under every shady tree, and have committed fornication there.}{3:6}{Moreover, Yahweh said to me in the days of Josiah the king, “Have you seen that which backsliding Israel has done? She has gone up on every high mountain and under every green tree, and has played the prostitute there.}
\VersePair{3:7}{And I said after she had committed all these acts of fornication, Turn again to me. Yet she returned not. And faithless Juda saw her faithlessness.}{3:7}{I said after she had done all these things, ‘She will return to me;’ but she didn’t return, and her treacherous sister Judah saw it.}
\VersePair{3:8}{And I saw that (for all the sins of which she was convicted, wherein the house of Israel committed adultery, and I put her away, and gave into her hands a bill of divorcement,) yet faithless Juda feared not, but went and herself also committed fornication.}{3:8}{I saw when, for this very cause, that backsliding Israel had committed adultery, I had put her away and given her a certificate of divorce, yet treacherous Judah, her sister, had no fear, but she also went and played the prostitute.}
\VersePair{3:9}{And her fornication was nothing accounted of; and she committed adultery with wood and stone.}{3:9}{Because she took her prostitution lightly, the land was polluted, and she committed adultery with stones and with wood.}
\VersePair{3:10}{And for all these things faithless Juda turned not to me with all her heart, but falsely.}{3:10}{Yet for all this her treacherous sister, Judah, has not returned to me with her whole heart, but only in pretense,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{3:11}{And the Lord said to me, Israel has justified himself more than faithless Juda.}{3:11}{Yahweh said to me, “Backsliding Israel has shown herself more righteous than treacherous Judah.}
\VersePair{3:12}{Go and read these words toward the north, and thou shalt say, Return to me, O house of Israel, saith the Lord; and I will not set my face against you: for I am merciful, saith the Lord, and I will not be angry with you for ever.}{3:12}{Go, and proclaim these words toward the north, and say, ‘Return, you backsliding Israel,’ says Yahweh; ‘I will not look in anger on you, for I am merciful,’ says Yahweh. ‘I will not keep anger forever.}
\VersePair{3:13}{Nevertheless, know thine iniquity, that thou hast sinned against the Lord thy God, and hast scattered thy ways to strangers under every shady tree, but thou didst not hearken to my voice, saith the Lord.}{3:13}{Only acknowledge your iniquity, that you have transgressed against Yahweh your God, and have scattered your ways to the strangers under every green tree, and you have not obeyed my voice,’” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{3:14}{Turn, ye children that have revolted, saith the Lord; for I will rule over you: and I will take you one of a city, and two of a family, and I will bring you in to Sion:}{3:14}{“Return, backsliding children,” says Yahweh, “for I am a husband to you. I will take one of you from a city, and two from a family, and I will bring you to Zion.}
\VersePair{3:15}{and I will give you shepherds after my heart, and they shall certainly tend you with knowledge.}{3:15}{I will give you shepherds according to my heart, who will feed you with knowledge and understanding.}
\VersePair{3:16}{And it shall come to pass that when ye are multiplied and increased upon the land, saith the Lord, in those days they shall say no more, The ark of the covenant of the Holy One of Israel: it shall not come to mind; it shall not be named; neither shall it be visited; nor shall this be done any more.}{3:16}{It will come to pass, when you are multiplied and increased in the land in those days,” says Yahweh, “they will no longer say, ‘the ark of Yahweh’s covenant!’ It will not come to mind. They won’t remember it. They won’t miss it, nor will another be made.}
\VersePair{3:17}{In those days and at that time they shall call Jerusalem the throne of the Lord; and all the nations shall be gathered to it: and they shall not walk any more after the imaginations of their evil heart.}{3:17}{At that time they will call Jerusalem ‘Yahweh’s Throne;’ and all the nations will be gathered to it, to Yahweh’s name, to Jerusalem. They will no longer walk after the stubbornness of their evil heart.}
\VersePair{3:18}{In those days the house of Juda shall come together to the house of Israel, and they shall come, together, from the land of the north, and from all the countries, to the land, which I caused their fathers to inherit.}{3:18}{In those days the house of Judah will walk with the house of Israel, and they will come together out of the land of the north to the land that I gave for an inheritance to your fathers.}
\VersePair{3:19}{And I said, So be it, Lord, for thou saidst, I will set thee among children, and will give thee a choice land, the inheritance of the Almighty God of the Gentiles: and I said, Ye shall call me Father; and ye shall not turn away from me.}{3:19}{“But I said, ‘How I desire to put you among the children, and give you a pleasant land, a goodly heritage of the armies of the nations!’ and I said, ‘You shall call me “My Father ”, and shall not turn away from following me.’}
\VersePair{3:20}{But as a wife acts treacherously against her husband, so has the house of Israel dealt treacherously against me, saith the Lord.}{3:20}{“Surely as a wife treacherously departs from her husband, so you have dealt treacherously with me, house of Israel,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{3:21}{A voice from the lips was heard, even of weeping and supplication of the children of Israel: for they have dealt unrighteously in their ways, they have forgotten God their Holy One.}{3:21}{A voice is heard on the bare heights, the weeping and the petitions of the children of Israel; because they have perverted their way, they have forgotten Yahweh their God.}
\VersePair{3:22}{Turn, ye children that are given to turning, and I will heal your bruises. Behold, we will be thy servants; for thou art the Lord our God.}{3:22}{Return, you backsliding children, and I will heal your backsliding. “Behold, we have come to you; for you are Yahweh our God.}
\VersePair{3:23}{Truly the hills and the strength of the mountains were a lying refuge: but by the Lord our God is the salvation of Israel.}{3:23}{Truly help from the hills, the tumult on the mountains, is in vain. Truly the salvation of Israel is in Yahweh our God.}
\VersePair{3:24}{But shame has consumed the labours of our fathers from our youth; their sheep and their calves, and their sons and their daughters.}{3:24}{But the shameful thing has devoured the labor of our fathers from our youth, their flocks and their herds, their sons and their daughters.}
\VersePair{3:25}{We have lain down in our shame, and our disgrace has covered us: because we and our fathers have sinned before our God, from our youth until this day; and we have not hearkened to the voice of the Lord our God.}{3:25}{Let us lie down in our shame, and let our confusion cover us; for we have sinned against Yahweh our God, we and our fathers, from our youth even to this day. We have not obeyed Yahweh our God’s voice.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{4}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{4:1}{If Israel will return to me, saith the Lord, he shall return: and if he will remove his abominations out of his mouth, and fear before me, and swear,}{4:1}{“If you will return, Israel,” says Yahweh, “if you will return to me, and if you will put away your abominations out of my sight; then you will not be removed;}
\VersePair{4:2}{The Lord lives, with truth, in judgment and righteousness, then shall nations bless by him, and by him they shall praise God in Jerusalem.}{4:2}{and you will swear, ‘As Yahweh lives,’ in truth, in justice, and in righteousness. The nations will bless themselves in him, and they will glory in him.”}
\VersePair{4:3}{For thus saith the Lord to the men of Juda, and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem, Break up fresh ground for yourselves, and sow not among thorns.}{4:3}{For Yahweh says to the men of Judah and to Jerusalem, “Break up your fallow ground, and don’t sow among thorns.}
\VersePair{4:4}{Circumcise yourselves to your God, and circumcise your hardness of heart, ye men of Juda, and inhabitants of Jerusalem: lest my wrath go forth as fire, and burn, and there be none to quench it, because of the evil of your devices.}{4:4}{Circumcise yourselves to Yahweh, and take away the foreskins of your heart, you men of Judah and inhabitants of Jerusalem; lest my wrath go out like fire, and burn so that no one can quench it, because of the evil of your doings.}
\VersePair{4:5}{Declare ye in Juda, and let it be heard in Jerusalem: say ye, Sound the trumpet in the land; cry ye aloud: say ye, Gather yourselves together, and let us enter into the fortified cities.}{4:5}{Declare in Judah, and publish in Jerusalem; and say, ‘Blow the trumpet in the land!’ Cry aloud and say, ‘Assemble yourselves! Let’s go into the fortified cities!’}
\VersePair{4:6}{Gather up your wares and flee to Sion: hasten, stay not: for I will bring evils from the north, and great destruction.}{4:6}{Set up a standard toward Zion. Flee for safety! Don’t wait; for I will bring evil from the north, and a great destruction.”}
\VersePair{4:7}{The lion is gone up from his lair, he has roused himself to the destruction of the nations, and has gone forth out of his place, to make the land desolate; and the cities shall be destroyed, so as to be without inhabitant.}{4:7}{A lion has gone up from his thicket, and a destroyer of nations. He is on his way. He has gone out from his place, to make your land desolate, that your cities be laid waste, without inhabitant.}
\VersePair{4:8}{For these things gird yourselves with sackclothes, and lament, and howl: for the anger of the Lord is not turned away from you.}{4:8}{For this, clothe yourself with sackcloth, lament and wail; for the fierce anger of Yahweh hasn’t turned back from us.}
\VersePair{4:9}{And it shall come to pass in that day, saith the Lord, that the heart of the king shall perish, and the heart of the princes; and the priests shall be amazed, and the prophets shall wonder.}{4:9}{“It will happen at that day,” says Yahweh, “that the heart of the king will perish, along with the heart of the princes. The priests will be astonished, and the prophets will wonder.”}
\VersePair{4:10}{And I said, O sovereign Lord, verily thou hast greatly deceived this people and Jerusalem, saying, There shall be peace; whereas behold, the sword has reached even to their soul.}{4:10}{Then I said, “Ah, Lord Yahweh! Surely you have greatly deceived this people and Jerusalem, saying, ‘You will have peace;’ whereas the sword reaches to the heart.”}
\VersePair{4:11}{At that time they shall say to this people and to Jerusalem, There is a spirit of error in the wilderness: the way of the daughter of my people is not to purity, nor to holiness.}{4:11}{At that time it will be said to this people and to Jerusalem, “A hot wind blows from the bare heights in the wilderness toward the daughter of my people, not to winnow, nor to cleanse.}
\VersePair{4:12}{But a spirit of full vengeance shall come upon me; and now I declare my judgments against them.}{4:12}{A full wind from these will come for me. Now I will also utter judgments against them.”}
\VersePair{4:13}{Behold, he shall come up as a cloud, and his chariots as a tempest: his horses are swifter than eagles. Woe unto us! for we are in misery.}{4:13}{Behold, he will come up as clouds, and his chariots will be as the whirlwind. His horses are swifter than eagles. Woe to us! For we are ruined.}
\VersePair{4:14}{Cleanse thine heart from wickedness, O Jerusalem, that thou mayest be saved: how long will thy grievous thoughts be within thee?}{4:14}{Jerusalem, wash your heart from wickedness, that you may be saved. How long will your evil thoughts lodge within you?}
\VersePair{4:15}{For a voice of one publishing from Dan shall come, and trouble out of mount Ephraim shall be heard of.}{4:15}{For a voice declares from Dan, and publishes evil from the hills of Ephraim:}
\VersePair{4:16}{Remind ye the nations; behold, they are come: proclaim it in Jerusalem, that bands are approaching from a land afar off, and have uttered their voice against the cities of Juda.}{4:16}{“Tell the nations, behold, publish against Jerusalem, ‘Watchers come from a far country, and raise their voice against the cities of Judah.}
\VersePair{4:17}{As keepers of a field, they have surrounded her; because thou, saith the Lord, hast neglected me.}{4:17}{As keepers of a field, they are against her all around, because she has been rebellious against me,’” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{4:18}{Thy ways and thy devices have brought these things upon thee; this is thy wickedness, for it is bitter, for it has reached to thy heart.}{4:18}{“Your way and your doings have brought these things to you. This is your wickedness, for it is bitter, for it reaches to your heart.”}
\VersePair{4:19}{I am pained in my bowels, my bowels, and the sensitive powers of my heart; my soul is in great commotion, my heart is torn: I will not be silent, for my soul has heard the sound of a trumpet, the cry of war, and of distress: it calls on destruction;}{4:19}{My anguish, my anguish! I am pained at my very heart! My heart trembles within me. I can’t hold my peace, because you have heard, O my soul, the sound of the trumpet, the alarm of war.}
\VersePair{4:20}{for all the land is distressed: suddenly my tabernacle is distressed, my curtains have been rent asunder.}{4:20}{Destruction on destruction is decreed, for the whole land is laid waste. Suddenly my tents are destroyed, and my curtains gone in a moment.}
\VersePair{4:21}{How long shall I see fugitives, and hear the sound of the trumpet?}{4:21}{How long will I see the standard and hear the sound of the trumpet?}
\VersePair{4:22}{For the princes of my people have not known me, they are foolish and unwise children: they are wise to do evil, but how to do good they have not known.}{4:22}{“For my people are foolish. They don’t know me. They are foolish children, and they have no understanding. They are skillful in doing evil, but they don’t know how to do good.”}
\VersePair{4:23}{I looked upon the earth, and, behold, it was not; and to the sky, and there was no light in it.}{4:23}{I saw the earth and, behold, it was waste and void, and the heavens, and they had no light.}
\VersePair{4:24}{I beheld the mountains, and they trembled, and I saw all the hills in commotion.}{4:24}{I saw the mountains, and behold, they trembled, and all the hills moved back and forth.}
\VersePair{4:25}{I looked, and, behold, there was no man, and all the birds of the sky were scared.}{4:25}{I saw, and behold, there was no man, and all the birds of the sky had fled.}
\VersePair{4:26}{I saw, and, behold, Carmel was desert, and all the cities were burnt with fire at the presence of the Lord, and at the presence of his fierce anger they were utterly destroyed.}{4:26}{I saw, and behold, the fruitful field was a wilderness, and all its cities were broken down at the presence of Yahweh, before his fierce anger.}
\VersePair{4:27}{Thus saith the Lord, The whole land shall be desolate; but I will not make a full end.}{4:27}{For Yahweh says, “The whole land will be a desolation; yet I will not make a full end.}
\VersePair{4:28}{For these things let the earth mourn, and let the sky be dark above: for I have spoken, and I will not repent; I have purposed, and I will not turn back from it.}{4:28}{For this the earth will mourn, and the heavens above be black, because I have spoken it. I have planned it, and I have not repented, neither will I turn back from it.”}
\VersePair{4:29}{The whole land has recoiled from the noise of the horseman and the bent bow; they have gone into the caves, and have hidden themselves in the groves, and have gone up upon the rocks: every city was abandoned, no man dwelt in them.}{4:29}{Every city flees for the noise of the horsemen and archers. They go into the thickets and climb up on the rocks. Every city is forsaken, and not a man dwells therein.}
\VersePair{4:30}{And what wilt thou do? Though thou clothe thyself with scarlet, and adorn thyself with golden ornaments; though thou adorn thine eyes with stibium, thy beauty will be in vain: thy lovers have rejected thee, they seek thy life.}{4:30}{You, when you are made desolate, what will you do? Though you clothe yourself with scarlet, though you deck yourself with ornaments of gold, though you enlarge your eyes with makeup, you make yourself beautiful in vain. Your lovers despise you. They seek your life.}
\VersePair{4:31}{For I have heard thy groaning as the voice of a woman in travail, as of her that brings forth her first child; the voice of the daughter of Zion shall fail through weakness, and she shall lose the strength of her hands, saying, Woe is me! for my soul faints because of the slain.}{4:31}{For I have heard a voice as of a woman in travail, the anguish as of her who gives birth to her first child, the voice of the daughter of Zion, who gasps for breath, who spreads her hands, saying, “Woe is me now! For my soul faints before the murderers.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{5}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{5:1}{Run ye about in the streets of Jerusalem, and see, and know, and seek in her broad places, if ye can find one, if there is any one that does judgment, and seeks faithfulness; and I will pardon them, saith the Lord.}{5:1}{“Run back and forth through the streets of Jerusalem, and see now, and know, and seek in its wide places, if you can find a man, if there is anyone who does justly, who seeks truth, then I will pardon her.}
\VersePair{5:2}{The Lord lives, they say; do they not therefore swear falsely?}{5:2}{Though they say, ‘As Yahweh lives,’ surely they swear falsely.”}
\VersePair{5:3}{O Lord, thine eyes are upon faithfulness: thou hast scourged them, but they have not grieved; thou hast consumed them; but they would not receive correction: they have made their faces harder than a rock; and they would not return.}{5:3}{O Yahweh, don’t your eyes look on truth? You have stricken them, but they were not grieved. You have consumed them, but they have refused to receive correction. They have made their faces harder than a rock. They have refused to return.}
\VersePair{5:4}{Then I said, It may be they are poor; for they are weak, for they know not the way of the Lord, or the judgment of God.}{5:4}{Then I said, “Surely these are poor. They are foolish; for they don’t know Yahweh’s way, nor the law of their God.}
\VersePair{5:5}{I will go to the rich men, and will speak to them; for they have known the way of the Lord, and the judgment of God: but, behold, with one consent they have broken the yoke, they have burst the bonds.}{5:5}{I will go to the great men and will speak to them, for they know the way of Yahweh, and the law of their God.” But these with one accord have broken the yoke, and burst the bonds.}
\VersePair{5:6}{Therefore has a lion out of the forest smitten them, and a wolf has destroyed them even to their houses, and a leopard has watched against their cities: all that go forth from them shall be hunted: for they have multiplied their ungodliness, they have strengthened themselves in their revoltings.}{5:6}{Therefore a lion out of the forest will kill them. A wolf of the evenings will destroy them. A leopard will watch against their cities. Everyone who goes out there will be torn in pieces, because their transgressions are many and their backsliding has increased.}
\VersePair{5:7}{In what way shall I forgive thee for these things? Thy sons have forsaken me, and sworn by them that are no gods: and I fed them to the full, and they committed adultery, and lodged in harlots'houses.}{5:7}{“How can I pardon you? Your children have forsaken me, and sworn by what are no gods. When I had fed them to the full, they committed adultery, and assembled themselves in troops at the prostitutes’houses.}
\VersePair{5:8}{They became as wanton horses: they neighed each one after his neighbour's wife.}{5:8}{They were as fed horses roaming at large. Everyone neighed after his neighbor’s wife.}
\VersePair{5:9}{Shall I not visit for these things? saith the Lord: and shall not my soul be avenged on such a nation as this.}{5:9}{Shouldn’t I punish them for these things?” says Yahweh. “Shouldn’t my soul be avenged on such a nation as this?}
\VersePair{5:10}{Go up upon her battlements, and break them down; but make not a full end: leave her buttresses; for they are the Lord's.}{5:10}{“Go up on her walls, and destroy, but don’t make a full end. Take away her branches, for they are not Yahweh’s.}
\VersePair{5:11}{For the house of Israel have indeed dealt treacherously against me, saith the Lord: the house of Juda also}{5:11}{For the house of Israel and the house of Judah have dealt very treacherously against me,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{5:12}{have lied to their Lord, and they have said, These things are not so; no evils shall come upon us; and we shall not see sword or famine.}{5:12}{They have denied Yahweh, and said, “It is not he. Evil won’t come on us. We won’t see sword or famine.}
\VersePair{5:13}{Our prophets became wind, and the word of the Lord was not in them.}{5:13}{The prophets will become wind, and the word is not in them. Thus it will be done to them.”}
\VersePair{5:14}{Therefore thus saith the Lord Almighty, Because ye have spoken this word, behold, I have made my words in thy mouth fire, and this people wood, and it shall devour them.}{5:14}{Therefore Yahweh, the God of Armies says, “Because you speak this word, behold, I will make my words in your mouth fire, and this people wood, and it will devour them.}
\VersePair{5:15}{Behold, I will bring upon you a nation from far, O house of Israel, saith the Lord; a nation the sound of whose language one shall not understand.}{5:15}{Behold, I will bring a nation on you from far away, house of Israel,” says Yahweh. “It is a mighty nation. It is an ancient nation, a nation whose language you don’t know and don’t understand what they say.}
\VersePair{5:16}{They are all mighty men:}{5:16}{Their quiver is an open tomb. They are all mighty men.}
\VersePair{5:17}{and they shall devour your harvest, and your bread; and shall devour your sons, and your daughters; and they shall devour your sheep, and your calves, and devour your vineyards, and your fig-plantations, and your olive yards: and they shall utterly destroy your strong cities, wherein ye trusted, with the sword.}{5:17}{They will eat up your harvest and your bread, which your sons and your daughters should eat. They will eat up your flocks and your herds. They will eat up your vines and your fig trees. They will beat down your fortified cities in which you trust with the sword.}
\VersePair{5:18}{And it shall come to pass in those days, saith the Lord thy God, that I will not utterly destroy you.}{5:18}{“But even in those days,” says Yahweh, “I will not make a full end of you.}
\VersePair{5:19}{And it shall come to pass, when ye shall say, Wherefore has the Lord our God done all these things to us? that thou shalt say to them, Because ye served strange gods in your land, so shall ye serve strangers in a land that is not yours.}{5:19}{It will happen when you say, ‘Why has Yahweh our God done all these things to us?’ Then you shall say to them, ‘Just as you have forsaken me and served foreign gods in your land, so you will serve strangers in a land that is not yours.’}
\VersePair{5:20}{Proclaim these things to the house of Jacob, and let them be heard in the house of Juda.}{5:20}{“Declare this in the house of Jacob, and publish it in Judah, saying,}
\VersePair{5:21}{Hear ye now these things, O foolish and senseless people; who have eyes, and see not; and have ears, and hear not:}{5:21}{‘Hear this now, foolish people without understanding, who have eyes, and don’t see, who have ears, and don’t hear:}
\VersePair{5:22}{will ye not be afraid of me? saith the Lord; and will ye not fear before me, who have set the sand for a bound to the sea, as a perpetual ordinance, and it shall not pass it: yea, it shall rage, but not prevail; and its waves shall roar, but not pass over it.}{5:22}{Don’t you fear me?’ says Yahweh; ‘Won’t you tremble at my presence, who have placed the sand for the bound of the sea by a perpetual decree, that it can’t pass it? Though its waves toss themselves, yet they can’t prevail. Though they roar, they still can’t pass over it.’}
\VersePair{5:23}{But this people has a disobedient and rebellious heart; and they have turned aside and gone back:}{5:23}{“But this people has a revolting and a rebellious heart. They have revolted and gone.}
\VersePair{5:24}{and they have not said in their heart, Let us fear now the Lord our God, who gives us the early and latter rain, according to the season of the fulfilment of the ordinance of harvest, and has preserved it for us.}{5:24}{They don’t say in their heart, ‘Let’s now fear Yahweh our God, who gives rain, both the former and the latter, in its season, who preserves to us the appointed weeks of the harvest.’}
\VersePair{5:25}{Your transgressions have turned away these things, and your sins have removed good things from you.}{5:25}{“Your iniquities have turned away these things, and your sins have withheld good from you.}
\VersePair{5:26}{For among my people were found ungodly men; and they have set snares to destroy men, and have caught them.}{5:26}{For wicked men are found among my people. They watch, as fowlers lie in wait. They set a trap. They catch men.}
\VersePair{5:27}{As a snare which has been set is full of birds, so are their houses full of deceit: therefore have they grown great, and become rich:}{5:27}{As a cage is full of birds, so are their houses full of deceit. Therefore they have become great, and grew rich.}
\VersePair{5:28}{and they have transgressed the rule of judgment; they have not judged the cause of the orphan, nor have they judged the cause of the widow.}{5:28}{They have grown fat. They shine; yes, they excel in deeds of wickedness. They don’t plead the cause, the cause of the fatherless, that they may prosper; and they don’t defend the rights of the needy.}
\VersePair{5:29}{Shall I not visit for these things? saith the Lord: and shall not my soul be avenged on such a nation as this?}{5:29}{“Shouldn’t I punish for these things?” says Yahweh. “Shouldn’t my soul be avenged on such a nation as this?}
\VersePair{5:30}{Shocking and horrible deeds have been done on the land;}{5:30}{“An astonishing and horrible thing has happened in the land.}
\VersePair{5:31}{the prophets utter unrighteous prophecies, and the priests have clapped their hands: and my people has loved to have it thus: and what will ye do for the future?}{5:31}{The prophets prophesy falsely, and the priests rule by their own authority; and my people love to have it so. What will you do in the end of it?}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{6}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{6:1}{Strengthen yourselves, ye children of Benjamin, to flee out of the midst of Jerusalem, and sound an alarm with the trumpet in Thecue, and set up a signal over Bæthacharma: for evil threatens from the north, and a great destruction is coming.}{6:1}{“Flee for safety, you children of Benjamin, out of the middle of Jerusalem! Blow the trumpet in Tekoa and raise up a signal on Beth Haccherem, for evil looks out from the north with a great destruction.}
\VersePair{6:2}{And thy pride, O daughter of Sion, shall be taken away.}{6:2}{I will cut off the beautiful and delicate one, the daughter of Zion.}
\VersePair{6:3}{The shepherds and their flocks shall come to her; and they shall pitch their tents against her round about, and shall feed their flocks each with his hand.}{6:3}{Shepherds with their flocks will come to her. They will pitch their tents against her all around. They will feed everyone in his place.”}
\VersePair{6:4}{Prepare yourselves for war against her; rise up, and let us go up against her at noon. Woe to us! for the day has gone down, for the shadows of the day fail.}{6:4}{“Prepare war against her! Arise! Let’s go up at noon. Woe to us! For the day declines, for the shadows of the evening are stretched out.}
\VersePair{6:5}{Rise, and let us go up against her by night, and destroy her foundations.}{6:5}{Arise! Let’s go up by night, and let’s destroy her palaces.”}
\VersePair{6:6}{For thus saith the Lord, Hew down her trees, array a numerous force against Jerusalem. O false city; there is all oppression in her.}{6:6}{For Yahweh of Armies said, “Cut down trees, and cast up a mound against Jerusalem. This is the city to be visited. She is filled with oppression within herself.}
\VersePair{6:7}{As a cistern cools water, so her wickedness cools her, ungodliness and misery shall be heard in her, as continually before her.}{6:7}{As a well produces its waters, so she produces her wickedness. Violence and destruction is heard in her. Sickness and wounds are continually before me.}
\VersePair{6:8}{Thou shalt be chastened, O Jerusalem, with pain and the scourge, lest my soul depart from thee; lest I make thee a desert land, which shall not be inhabited.}{6:8}{Be instructed, Jerusalem, lest my soul be alienated from you, lest I make you a desolation, an uninhabited land.”}
\VersePair{6:9}{For thus saith the Lord, Glean, glean thoroughly as a vine the remnant of Israel: turn back your hands as a grape-gatherer to his basket.}{6:9}{Yahweh of Armies says, “They will thoroughly glean the remnant of Israel like a vine. Turn again your hand as a grape gatherer into the baskets.”}
\VersePair{6:10}{To whom shall I speak, and testify, that he may hearken? behold, thine ears are uncircumcised, and they shall not be able to hear: behold, the word of the Lord is become to them a reproach, they will not at all desire it.}{6:10}{To whom should I speak and testify, that they may hear? Behold, their ear is uncircumcised, and they can’t listen. Behold, Yahweh’s word has become a reproach to them. They have no delight in it.}
\VersePair{6:11}{And I allowed my wrath to come to the full, yet I kept it in, and did not utterly destroy them: I will pour it out on the children without, and on the assembly of young men together: for man and woman shall be taken together, the old man with him that is full of days.}{6:11}{{\raggedright Therefore I am full of Yahweh’s wrath. I am weary with holding it in. \poemline{1}{“Pour it out on the children in the street,}\poemline{2}{and on the assembly of young men together;}\poemline{1}{for even the husband with the wife will be taken,}\poemline{2}{the aged with him who is full of days.}}}
\VersePair{6:12}{And their houses shall be turned to others, with their fields and their wives together: for I will stretch out my hand upon the inhabitants of this land, saith the Lord.}{6:12}{{\raggedright Their houses will be turned to others, \poemline{2}{their fields and their wives together;}\poemline{1}{for I will stretch out my hand on the inhabitants of the land, says Yahweh.”}}}
\VersePair{6:13}{For from the least of them even to the greatest they have all committed iniquity; from the priest even to the false prophet they have all wrought falsely.}{6:13}{{\raggedright “For from their least even to their greatest, everyone is given to covetousness. \poemline{2}{From the prophet even to the priest, everyone deals falsely.}}}
\VersePair{6:14}{And they healed the breach of my people imperfectly, making light of it, and saying, Peace, peace: and where is peace?}{6:14}{{\raggedright They have healed also the hurt of my people superficially, \poemline{2}{saying, ‘Peace, peace!’ when there is no peace.}}}
\VersePair{6:15}{They were ashamed because they failed; yet they were not ashamed as those who are truly ashamed, and they knew not their own disgrace: therefore shall they utterly fall when they do fall, and in the time of visitation shall they perish, said the Lord.}{6:15}{{\raggedright Were they ashamed when they had committed abomination? \poemline{2}{No, they were not at all ashamed, neither could they blush.}\poemline{1}{Therefore they will fall among those who fall.}\poemline{2}{When I visit them, they will be cast down,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{6:16}{Thus saith the Lord, Stand ye in the ways, and see, and ask for the old paths of the Lord; and see what is the good way, and walk in it, and ye shall find purification for your souls. But they said, We will not walk in them.}{6:16}{Yahweh says, “Stand in the ways and see, and ask for the old paths, ‘Where is the good way?’ and walk in it, and you will find rest for your souls. But they said, ‘We will not walk in it.’}
\VersePair{6:17}{I have set watchmen over you, saying, Hear ye the sound of the trumpet. But they said, We will not hear it.}{6:17}{I set watchmen over you, saying, ‘Listen to the sound of the trumpet!’ But they said, ‘We will not listen!’}
\VersePair{6:18}{Therefore have the nations heard, and they that feed their flocks.}{6:18}{Therefore hear, you nations, and know, congregation, what is among them.}
\VersePair{6:19}{Hear, O earth: behold, I will bring evils upon this people, even the fruit of their rebellions; for they have not heeded my words, and they have rejected my law.}{6:19}{Hear, earth! Behold, I will bring evil on this people, even the fruit of their thoughts, because they have not listened to my words; and as for my law, they have rejected it.}
\VersePair{6:20}{Wherefore do ye bring me frankincense from Saba, and cinnamon from a land afar off? your whole-burnt-offerings are not acceptable, and your sacrifices have not been pleasant to me.}{6:20}{To what purpose does frankincense from Sheba come to me, and the sweet cane from a far country? Your burnt offerings are not acceptable, and your sacrifices are not pleasing to me.”}
\VersePair{6:21}{Therefore thus saith the Lord, Behold, I will bring weakness upon this people, and the fathers and sons shall be weak together; the neighbour and his friend shall perish.}{6:21}{Therefore Yahweh says, “Behold, I will lay stumbling blocks before this people. The fathers and the sons together will stumble against them. The neighbor and his friend will perish.”}
\VersePair{6:22}{Thus saith the Lord, Behold, a people comes from the north, and nations shall be stirred up from the end of the earth.}{6:22}{Yahweh says, “Behold, a people comes from the north country. A great nation will be stirred up from the uttermost parts of the earth.}
\VersePair{6:23}{They shall lay hold on bow and spear; the people is fierce, and will have no mercy; their voice is as the roaring sea; they shall array themselves for war against thee as fire on horses and chariots, O daughter of Sion.}{6:23}{They take hold of bow and spear. They are cruel, and have no mercy. Their voice roars like the sea, and they ride on horses, everyone set in array, as a man to the battle, against you, daughter of Zion.”}
\VersePair{6:24}{We have heard the report of them: our hands are weakened: anguish has seized us, the pangs as of a woman in travail.}{6:24}{We have heard its report. Our hands become feeble. Anguish has taken hold of us, and pains as of a woman in labor.}
\VersePair{6:25}{Go not forth into the field, and walk not in the ways; for the sword of the enemy lingers round about.}{6:25}{Don’t go out into the field or walk by the way; for the sword of the enemy and terror are on every side.}
\VersePair{6:26}{O daughter of my people, gird thyself with sackcloth: sprinkle thyself with ashes; make for thyself pitiable lamentation, as the mourning for a beloved son: for misery will come suddenly upon you.}{6:26}{Daughter of my people, clothe yourself with sackcloth, and wallow in ashes! Mourn, as for an only son, most bitter lamentation, for the destroyer will suddenly come on us.}
\VersePair{6:27}{I have caused thee to be tried among tried nations, and thou shalt know me when I have tried their way.}{6:27}{“I have made you a tester of metals and a fortress among my people, that you may know and try their way.}
\VersePair{6:28}{They are all disobedient, walking perversely: they are brass and iron; they are all corrupted.}{6:28}{They are all grievous rebels, going around to slander. They are bronze and iron. All of them deal corruptly.}
\VersePair{6:29}{The bellows have failed from the fire, the lead has failed: the silversmith works at his trade in vain; their wickedness is not consumed.}{6:29}{The bellows blow fiercely. The lead is consumed in the fire. In vain they go on refining, for the wicked are not plucked away.}
\VersePair{6:30}{Call ye them reprobate silver, because the Lord has rejected them.}{6:30}{Men will call them rejected silver, because Yahweh has rejected them.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{7}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{7:2}{Hear ye the word of the Lord, all Judea.}{7:1-7:2}{The word that came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, saying, “Stand in the gate of Yahweh’s house, and proclaim this word there, and say, ‘Hear Yahweh’s word, all you of Judah, who enter in at these gates to worship Yahweh.’”}
\VersePair{7:3}{Thus saith the Lord God of Israel, Correct your ways and your devices, and I will cause you to dwell in this place.}{7:3}{Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says, “Amend your ways and your doings, and I will cause you to dwell in this place.}
\VersePair{7:4}{Trust not in yourselves with lying words, for they shall not profit you at all, saying, It is the temple of the Lord, the temple of the Lord.}{7:4}{Don’t trust in lying words, saying, ‘Yahweh’s temple, Yahweh’s temple, Yahweh’s temple, are these.’}
\VersePair{7:5}{For if ye thoroughly correct your ways and your practices, and do indeed execute judgment between a man and his neighbour;}{7:5}{For if you thoroughly amend your ways and your doings, if you thoroughly execute justice between a man and his neighbor;}
\VersePair{7:6}{and oppress not the stranger, and the orphan, and the widow, and shed not innocent blood in this place, and go not after strange gods to your hurt:}{7:6}{if you don’t oppress the foreigner, the fatherless, and the widow, and don’t shed innocent blood in this place, and don’t walk after other gods to your own hurt,}
\VersePair{7:7}{then will I cause you to dwell in this place, in the land which I gave to your fathers of old and for ever.}{7:7}{then I will cause you to dwell in this place, in the land that I gave to your fathers, from of old even forever more.}
\VersePair{7:8}{But whereas ye have trusted in lying words, whereby ye shall not be profited;}{7:8}{Behold, you trust in lying words that can’t profit.}
\VersePair{7:9}{and ye murder, and commit adultery, and steal, and swear falsely, and burn incense to Baal, and are gone after strange gods whom ye know not,}{7:9}{Will you steal, murder, commit adultery, swear falsely, burn incense to Baal, and walk after other gods that you have not known,}
\VersePair{7:10}{so that it is evil with you; yet have ye come, and stood before me in the house, whereon my name is called, and ye have said, We have refrained from doing all these abominations.}{7:10}{then come and stand before me in this house, which is called by my name, and say, ‘We are delivered,’ that you may do all these abominations?}
\VersePair{7:11}{Is my house, whereon my name is called, a den of robbers in your eyes? And, behold, I have seen it, saith the Lord.}{7:11}{Has this house, which is called by my name, become a den of robbers in your eyes? Behold, I myself have seen it,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{7:12}{For go ye to my place which is in Selo, where I caused my name to dwell before, and see what I did to it because of the wickedness of my people Israel.}{7:12}{“But go now to my place which was in Shiloh, where I caused my name to dwell at the first, and see what I did to it for the wickedness of my people Israel.}
\VersePair{7:13}{And now, because ye have done all these deeds, and I spoke to you, but ye hearkened not to me; and I called you, but ye answered not;}{7:13}{Now, because you have done all these works,” says Yahweh, “and I spoke to you, rising up early and speaking, but you didn’t hear; and I called you, but you didn’t answer;}
\VersePair{7:14}{therefore I also will do to the house whereon my name is called, wherein ye trust, and to the place which I gave to you and to your fathers, as I did to Selo.}{7:14}{therefore I will do to the house which is called by my name, in which you trust, and to the place which I gave to you and to your fathers, as I did to Shiloh.}
\VersePair{7:15}{And I will cast you out of my sight, as I cast away your brethren, all the seed of Ephraim.}{7:15}{I will cast you out of my sight, as I have cast out all your brothers, even the whole offspring of Ephraim. \footnote{7:15: or, seed}}
\VersePair{7:16}{Therefore pray not thou for this people, and intercede not for them to be pitied, yea, pray not, and approach me not for them: for I will not hearken unto thee.}{7:16}{“Therefore don’t pray for this people. Don’t lift up a cry or prayer for them or make intercession to me; for I will not hear you.}
\VersePair{7:17}{Seest thou not what they do in the cities of Juda, and in the streets of Jerusalem?}{7:17}{Don’t you see what they do in the cities of Judah and in the streets of Jerusalem?}
\VersePair{7:18}{Their children gather wood, and their fathers kindle a fire, and their women knead dough, to make cakes to the host of heaven; and they have poured out drink-offerings to strange gods, that they might provoke me to anger.}{7:18}{The children gather wood, and the fathers kindle the fire, and the women knead the dough, to make cakes to the queen of the sky, and to pour out drink offerings to other gods, that they may provoke me to anger.}
\VersePair{7:19}{Do they provoke me to anger? saith the Lord: do they not provoke themselves, that their faces may be ashamed?}{7:19}{Do they provoke me to anger?” says Yahweh. “Don’t they provoke themselves, to the confusion of their own faces?”}
\VersePair{7:20}{Therefore thus saith the Lord; Behold, my anger and wrath shall be poured out upon this place, and upon the men, and upon the cattle, and upon every tree of their field, and upon the fruits of the land; and it shall burn, and not be quenched.}{7:20}{Therefore the Lord Yahweh says: “Behold, my anger and my wrath will be poured out on this place, on man, on animal, on the trees of the field, and on the fruit of the ground; and it will burn and will not be quenched.”}
\VersePair{7:21}{Thus saith the Lord, Gather your whole-burnt-offerings with your meat-offerings, and eat flesh.}{7:21}{Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says: “Add your burnt offerings to your sacrifices and eat meat.}
\VersePair{7:22}{For I spoke not to your fathers, and commanded them not in the day wherein I brought them up out of the land of Egypt, concerning whole-burnt-offerings and sacrifice:}{7:22}{For I didn’t speak to your fathers or command them in the day that I brought them out of the land of Egypt concerning burnt offerings or sacrifices;}
\VersePair{7:23}{but I commanded them this thing, saying, Hear ye my voice, and I will be to you a God, and ye shall be to me a people: and walk ye in all my ways, which I shall command you, that it may be well with you.}{7:23}{but this thing I commanded them, saying, ‘Listen to my voice, and I will be your God, and you shall be my people. Walk in all the way that I command you, that it may be well with you.’}
\VersePair{7:24}{But they hearkened not to me, and their ear gave no heed, but they walked in the imaginations of their evil heart, and went backward, and not forward;}{7:24}{But they didn’t listen or turn their ear, but walked in their own counsels and in the stubbornness of their evil heart, and went backward, and not forward.}
\VersePair{7:25}{from the day that their fathers went forth out of the land of Egypt, even until this day. And I sent to you all my servants, the prophets, by day and early in the morning: yea, I sent them,}{7:25}{Since the day that your fathers came out of the land of Egypt to this day, I have sent to you all my servants the prophets, daily rising up early and sending them.}
\VersePair{7:26}{but they hearkened not to me, and their ear gave no heed; and they made their neck harder than their fathers.}{7:26}{Yet they didn’t listen to me or incline their ear, but made their neck stiff. They did worse than their fathers.}
\VersePair{7:27}{Therefore thou shalt speak this word to them;}{7:27}{“You shall speak all these words to them, but they will not listen to you. You shall also call to them, but they will not answer you.}
\VersePair{7:28}{This is the nation which has not hearkened to the voice of the Lord, nor received correction: truth has failed from their mouth.}{7:28}{You shall tell them, ‘This is the nation that has not listened to Yahweh their God’s voice, nor received instruction. Truth has perished, and is cut off from their mouth.’}
\VersePair{7:29}{Cut off thine hair, and cast it away, and take up a lamentation on thy lips; for the Lord has reprobated and rejected the generation that does these things.}{7:29}{Cut off your hair, and throw it away, and take up a lamentation on the bare heights; for Yahweh has rejected and forsaken the generation of his wrath.}
\VersePair{7:30}{For the children of Juda have wrought evil before me, saith the Lord; they have set their abominations in the house on which my name is called, to defile it.}{7:30}{“For the children of Judah have done that which is evil in my sight,” says Yahweh. “They have set their abominations in the house which is called by my name, to defile it.}
\VersePair{7:31}{And they have built the altar of Tapheth, which is in the valley of the son of Ennom, to burn their sons and their daughters with fire; which I did not command them to do, neither did I design it in my heart.}{7:31}{They have built the high places of Topheth, which is in the valley of the son of Hinnom, to burn their sons and their daughters in the fire, which I didn’t command, nor did it come into my mind.}
\VersePair{7:32}{Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when they shall no more say, The altar of Tapheth, and the valley of the son of Ennom, but, The valley of the slain; and they shall bury in Tapheth, for want of room.}{7:32}{Therefore behold, the days come ”, says Yahweh, “that it will no more be called ‘Topheth’or ‘The valley of the son of Hinnom ’, but ‘The valley of Slaughter ’; for they will bury in Topheth until there is no place to bury.}
\VersePair{7:33}{And the dead bodies of this people shall be for food to the birds of the sky, and to the wild beasts of the earth; and there shall be none to drive them away.}{7:33}{The dead bodies of this people will be food for the birds of the sky, and for the animals of the earth. No one will frighten them away.}
\VersePair{7:34}{And I will destroy out of the cities of Juda, and the streets of Jerusalem, the voice of them that make merry, and the voice of them that rejoice, the voice of the bridegroom, and the voice of the bride; for the whole land shall become a desolation.}{7:34}{Then I will cause to cease from the cities of Judah and from the streets of Jerusalem the voice of mirth and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom and the voice of the bride; for the land will become a waste.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{8}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{8:1}{At that time, saith the Lord, they shall bring out the bones of the kings of Juda, and the bones of his princes, and the bones of the priests, and the bones of the prophets, and the bones of the inhabitants of Jerusalem, out of their graves;}{8:1}{“At that time,” says Yahweh, “they will bring the bones of the kings of Judah, the bones of his princes, the bones of the priests, the bones of the prophets, and the bones of the inhabitants of Jerusalem, out of their graves.}
\VersePair{8:2}{and they shall spread them out to the sun, and the moon, and to all the stars, and to all the host of heaven, which they have loved, and which they have served, and after which they have walked, and to which they have held, and which they have worshipped; they shall not be mourned for, neither shall they be buried; but they shall be for an example on the face of the earth,}{8:2}{They will spread them before the sun, the moon, and all the army of the sky, which they have loved, which they have served, after which they have walked, which they have sought, and which they have worshiped. They will not be gathered or be buried. They will be like dung on the surface of the earth.}
\VersePair{8:3}{because they chose death rather than life, even to all the remnant that are left of that family, in every place whither I shall drive them out.}{8:3}{Death will be chosen rather than life by all the residue that remain of this evil family, that remain in all the places where I have driven them,” says Yahweh of Armies.}
\VersePair{8:4}{For thus saith the Lord, Shall not he that falls arise? or he that turns away, shall he not turn back again?}{8:4}{{\raggedright “Moreover you shall tell them, ‘Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“‘Do men fall, and not rise up again?}\poemline{2}{Does one turn away, and not return?}}}
\VersePair{8:5}{Wherefore has this my people turned away with a shameless revolting, and strengthened themselves in their wilfulness, and refused to return?}{8:5}{{\raggedright Why then have the people of Jerusalem fallen back by a perpetual backsliding? \poemline{2}{They cling to deceit.}\poemline{2}{They refuse to return.}}}
\VersePair{8:6}{Hearken, I pray you, and hear: will they not speak thus, There is no man that repents of his wickedness, saying, What have I done? the runner has failed from his course, as a tired horse in his neighing.}{8:6}{{\raggedright I listened and heard, but they didn’t say what is right. \poemline{2}{No one repents of his wickedness, saying, “What have I done?”}\poemline{1}{Everyone turns to his course,}\poemline{2}{as a horse that rushes headlong in the battle.}}}
\VersePair{8:7}{Yea, the stork in the heaven knows her time, also the turtle-dove and wild swallow; the sparrows observe the times of their coming in; but this my people knows not the judgments of the Lord.}{8:7}{{\raggedright Yes, the stork in the sky knows her appointed times. \poemline{2}{The turtledove, the swallow, and the crane observe the time of their coming;}\poemline{2}{but my people don’t know Yahweh’s law.}}}
\VersePair{8:8}{How will ye say, We are wise, and the law of the Lord is with us? In vain have the scribes used a false pen.}{8:8}{{\raggedright “‘How do you say, “We are wise, and Yahweh’s law is with us ”? \poemline{2}{But, behold, the false pen of the scribes has made that a lie.}}}
\VersePair{8:9}{The wise men are ashamed, and alarmed, and taken; because they have rejected the word of the Lord; what wisdom is there in them?}{8:9}{{\raggedright The wise men are disappointed. \poemline{2}{They are dismayed and trapped.}\poemline{1}{Behold, they have rejected Yahweh’s word.}\poemline{2}{What kind of wisdom is in them?}}}
\VersePair{8:10}{Therefore will I give their wives to others, and their fields to new inheritors; and they shall gather their fruits, saith the Lord.}{8:10}{{\raggedright Therefore I will give their wives to others \poemline{2}{and their fields to those who will possess them.}\poemline{1}{For everyone from the least even to the greatest is given to covetousness;}\poemline{2}{from the prophet even to the priest everyone deals falsely.}}}
\VersePair{8:11}{}{8:11}{{\raggedright They have healed the hurt of the daughter of my people slightly, saying, \poemline{2}{“Peace, peace,” when there is no peace.}}}
\VersePair{8:12}{}{8:12}{{\raggedright Were they ashamed when they had committed abomination? \poemline{2}{No, they were not at all ashamed.}\poemline{2}{They couldn’t blush.}\poemline{1}{Therefore they will fall among those who fall.}\poemline{2}{In the time of their visitation they will be cast down, says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{8:13}{There are no grapes on the vines, and there are no figs on the fig-trees, and the leaves have fallen off.}{8:13}{{\raggedright “‘I will utterly consume them, says Yahweh. \poemline{2}{No grapes will be on the vine,}\poemline{2}{no figs on the fig tree,}\poemline{2}{and the leaf will fade.}\poemline{1}{The things that I have given them}\poemline{2}{will pass away from them.’”}}}
\VersePair{8:14}{Why do we sit still? assemble yourselves, and let us enter into the strong cities, and let us be cast out there: for God has cast us out, and made us drink water of gall, because we have sinned before him.}{8:14}{{\raggedright “Why do we sit still? \poemline{2}{Assemble yourselves!}\poemline{2}{Let’s enter into the fortified cities,}\poemline{2}{and let’s be silent there;}\poemline{1}{for Yahweh our God has put us to silence,}\poemline{2}{and given us poisoned water to drink,}\poemline{2}{because we have sinned against Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{8:15}{We assembled for peace, but there was no prosperity; for a time of healing, but behold anxiety.}{8:15}{{\raggedright We looked for peace, but no good came; \poemline{2}{and for a time of healing, and behold, dismay!}}}
\VersePair{8:16}{We shall hear the neighing of his swift horses out of Dan: the whole land quaked at the sound of the neighing of his horses; and he shall come, and devour the land and the fulness of it; the city, and them that dwell in it.}{8:16}{{\raggedright The snorting of his horses is heard from Dan. \poemline{2}{The whole land trembles at the sound of the neighing of his strong ones;}\poemline{1}{for they have come, and have devoured the land and all that is in it,}\poemline{2}{the city and those who dwell therein.”}}}
\VersePair{8:17}{For, behold, I send forth against you deadly serpents, which cannot be charmed, and they shall bite you}{8:17}{{\raggedright “For, behold, I will send serpents, \poemline{2}{adders among you,}\poemline{2}{which will not be charmed;}\poemline{2}{and they will bite you,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{8:18}{mortally with the pain of your distressed heart.}{8:18}{{\raggedright Oh that I could comfort myself against sorrow! \poemline{2}{My heart is faint within me.}}}
\VersePair{8:19}{Behold, there is a sound of the cry of the daughter of my people from a land afar off: Is not the Lord in Sion? is there not a king there? because they have provoked me with their graven images, and with strange vanities.}{8:19}{{\raggedright Behold, the voice of the cry of the daughter of my people from a land that is very far off: \poemline{2}{“Isn’t Yahweh in Zion?}\poemline{2}{Isn’t her King in her?”}\poemline{1}{“Why have they provoked me to anger with their engraved images,}\poemline{2}{and with foreign idols?”}}}
\VersePair{8:20}{The summer is gone, the harvest is past, and we are not saved.}{8:20}{{\raggedright “The harvest is past. \poemline{2}{The summer has ended,}\poemline{2}{and we are not saved.”}}}
\VersePair{8:21}{For the breach of the daughter of my people I have been saddened: in my perplexity pangs have seized upon me as of a woman in travail.}{8:21}{{\raggedright For the hurt of the daughter of my people, I am hurt. \poemline{2}{I mourn.}\poemline{2}{Dismay has taken hold of me.}}}
\VersePair{8:22}{And is there no balm in Galaad, or is there no physician there? why has not the healing of the daughter of my people taken place?}{8:22}{{\raggedright Is there no balm in Gilead? \poemline{2}{Is there no physician there?}\poemline{1}{Why then isn’t the health of the daughter of my people recovered?}}}
\VersePair{8:23}{Who will give water to my head, and a fountain of tears to my eyes? then would I weep for this my people day and night, even for the slain of the daughter of my people.}{9:1}{{\raggedright Oh that my head were waters, \poemline{2}{and my eyes a spring of tears,}\poemline{1}{that I might weep day and night}\poemline{2}{for the slain of the daughter of my people!}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{9}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{9:1}{Who would give me a most distant lodge in the wilderness, that I might leave my people, and depart from them? for they all commit adultery, an assembly of treacherous men.}{9:2}{{\raggedright Oh that I had in the wilderness \poemline{2}{a lodging place of wayfaring men,}\poemline{1}{that I might leave my people}\poemline{2}{and go from them!}\poemline{1}{For they are all adulterers,}\poemline{2}{an assembly of treacherous men.}}}
\VersePair{9:2}{And they have bent their tongue like a bow: falsehood and not faithfulness has prevailed upon the earth; for they have gone on from evil to evil, and have not known me, saith the Lord.}{9:3}{{\raggedright “They bend their tongue, \poemline{2}{as their bow, for falsehood.}\poemline{1}{They have grown strong in the land,}\poemline{2}{but not for truth;}\poemline{1}{for they proceed from evil to evil,}\poemline{2}{and they don’t know me,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{9:3}{Beware ye each of his neighbour, and trust ye not in your brethren: for every one will surely supplant, and every friend will walk craftily.}{9:4}{{\raggedright “Everyone beware of his neighbor, \poemline{2}{and don’t trust in any brother;}\poemline{1}{for every brother will utterly supplant,}\poemline{2}{and every neighbor will go around like a slanderer.}}}
\VersePair{9:4}{Every one will mock his friend; they will not speak truth: their tongue has learned to speak falsehoods; they have committed iniquity, they ceased not, so as to return.}{9:5}{{\raggedright Friends deceive each other, \poemline{2}{and will not speak the truth.}\poemline{1}{They have taught their tongue to speak lies.}\poemline{2}{They weary themselves committing iniquity.}}}
\VersePair{9:5}{There is usury upon usury, and deceit upon deceit: they would not know me, saith the Lord.}{9:6}{{\raggedright Your habitation is in the middle of deceit. \poemline{2}{Through deceit, they refuse to know me,” says Yahweh.}}}
