\VersePair{9:6}{Therefore thus saith the Lord, Behold, I will try them with fire, and prove them; for I will do thus because of the wickedness of the daughter of my people.}{9:7}{{\raggedright Therefore Yahweh of Armies says, \poemline{1}{“Behold, I will melt them and test them;}\poemline{2}{for how should I deal with the daughter of my people?}}}
\VersePair{9:7}{Their tongue is a wounding arrow; the words of their mouth are deceitful: one speaks peaceably to his neighbour, but in himself retains enmity.}{9:8}{{\raggedright Their tongue is a deadly arrow. \poemline{2}{It speaks deceit.}\poemline{1}{One speaks peaceably to his neighbor with his mouth,}\poemline{2}{but in his heart, he waits to ambush him.}}}
\VersePair{9:8}{Shall I not visit for these things? saith the Lord: and shall not my soul be avenged on such a people as this?}{9:9}{{\raggedright Shouldn’t I punish them for these things?” says Yahweh. \poemline{2}{“Shouldn’t my soul be avenged on a nation such as this?}}}
\VersePair{9:9}{Take up a lamentation for the mountains, and a mournful dirge for the paths of the wilderness, for they are desolate for want of men; they heard not the sound of life from the birds of the sky, nor the cattle: they were amazed, they are gone.}{9:10}{{\raggedright I will weep and wail for the mountains, \poemline{2}{and lament for the pastures of the wilderness,}\poemline{1}{because they are burned up, so that no one passes through;}\poemline{2}{Men can’t hear the voice of the livestock.}\poemline{1}{Both the birds of the sky and the animals have fled.}\poemline{2}{They are gone.}}}
\VersePair{9:10}{And I will remove the inhabitants of Jerusalem, and make it a dwelling-place of dragons; and I will utterly waste the cities of Juda, so that they shall not be inhabited.}{9:11}{{\raggedright “I will make Jerusalem heaps, \poemline{2}{a dwelling place of jackals.}\poemline{1}{I will make the cities of Judah a desolation,}\poemline{2}{without inhabitant.”}}}
\VersePair{9:11}{Who is the wise man, that he may understand this? and he that has the word of the mouth of the Lord addressed to him, let him tell you wherefore the land has been destroyed, has been ravaged by fire like a desert, so that no one passes through it.}{9:12}{Who is wise enough to understand this? Who is he to whom the mouth of Yahweh has spoken, that he may declare it? Why has the land perished and burned up like a wilderness, so that no one passes through?}
\VersePair{9:12}{And the Lord said to me, Because they have forsaken my law, which I set before them, and have not hearkened to my voice;}{9:13}{Yahweh says, “Because they have forsaken my law which I set before them, and have not obeyed my voice or walked in my ways,}
\VersePair{9:13}{but went after the lusts of their evil heart, and after the idols which their fathers taught them to worship:}{9:14}{but have walked after the stubbornness of their own heart and after the Baals, which their fathers taught them.”}
\VersePair{9:14}{therefore thus saith the Lord God of Israel, Behold, I will feed them with trouble and will cause them to drink water of gall:}{9:15}{Therefore Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says, “Behold, I will feed them, even this people, with wormwood and give them poisoned water to drink.}
\VersePair{9:15}{and I will scatter them among the nations, to them whom neither they nor their fathers knew; and I will send a sword upon them, until I have consumed them with it.}{9:16}{I will scatter them also among the nations, whom neither they nor their fathers have known. I will send the sword after them, until I have consumed them.”}
\VersePair{9:16}{Thus saith the Lord, Call ye the mourning women, and let them come; and send to the wise women, and let them utter their voice;}{9:17}{{\raggedright Yahweh of Armies says, \poemline{1}{“Consider, and call for the mourning women, that they may come.}\poemline{2}{Send for the skillful women, that they may come.}}}
\VersePair{9:17}{and let them take up a lamentation for you, and let your eyes pour down tears, and your eyelids drop water.}{9:18}{{\raggedright Let them make haste \poemline{2}{and take up a wailing for us,}\poemline{1}{that our eyes may run down with tears}\poemline{2}{and our eyelids gush out with waters.}}}
\VersePair{9:18}{For a voice of lamentation has been heard in Sion, How are we become wretched! we are greatly ashamed, for we have forsaken the land, and have abandoned our tabernacles!}{9:19}{{\raggedright For a voice of wailing is heard out of Zion, \poemline{2}{‘How we are ruined!}\poemline{1}{We are greatly confounded}\poemline{2}{because we have forsaken the land,}\poemline{2}{because they have cast down our dwellings.’”}}}
\VersePair{9:19}{Hear now, ye women, the word of God, and let your ears receive the words of his mouth, and teach your daughters lamentation, and every woman her neighbour a dirge.}{9:20}{{\raggedright Yet hear Yahweh’s word, you women. \poemline{2}{Let your ear receive the word of his mouth.}\poemline{1}{Teach your daughters wailing.}\poemline{2}{Everyone teach her neighbor a lamentation.}}}
\VersePair{9:20}{For death has come up through your windows, it has entered into our land, to destroy the infants without, and the young men from the streets.}{9:21}{{\raggedright For death has come up into our windows. \poemline{2}{It has entered into our palaces}\poemline{1}{to cut off the children from outside,}\poemline{2}{and the young men from the streets.}}}
\VersePair{9:21}{And the carcases of the men shall be for an example on the face of the field of your land, like grass after the mower, and there shall be none to gather them.}{9:22}{{\raggedright Speak, “Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“‘The dead bodies of men will fall as dung on the open field,}\poemline{2}{and as the handful after the harvester.}\poemline{2}{No one will gather them.’”}}}
\VersePair{9:22}{Thus saith the Lord, Let not the wise man boast in his wisdom, and let not the strong man boast in his strength, and let not the rich man boast in his wealth;}{9:23}{{\raggedright Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“Don’t let the wise man glory in his wisdom.}\poemline{2}{Don’t let the mighty man glory in his might.}\poemline{2}{Don’t let the rich man glory in his riches.}}}
\VersePair{9:23}{but let him that boasts boast in this, the understanding and knowing that I am the Lord that exercise mercy, and judgment, and righteousness, upon the earth; for in these things is my pleasure, saith the Lord.}{9:24}{{\raggedright But let him who glories glory in this, \poemline{2}{that he has understanding, and knows me,}\poemline{1}{that I am Yahweh who exercises loving kindness, justice, and righteousness in the earth,}\poemline{2}{for I delight in these things,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{9:24}{Behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when I will visit upon all the circumcised their uncircumcision;}{9:25}{“Behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, “that I will punish all those who are circumcised only in their flesh:}
\VersePair{9:25}{on Egypt, and on Idumea, and on Edom, and on the children of Ammon, and on the children of Moab, and on every one that shaves his face round about, even them that dwell in the wilderness; for all the Gentiles are uncircumcised in flesh, and all the house of Israel are uncircumcised in their hearts.}{9:26}{Egypt, Judah, Edom, the children of Ammon, Moab, and all who have the corners of their hair cut off, who dwell in the wilderness, for all the nations are uncircumcised, and all the house of Israel are uncircumcised in heart.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{10}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{10:1}{Hear ye the word of the Lord, which he has spoken to you, O house of Israel.}{10:1}{Hear the word which Yahweh speaks to you, house of Israel!}
\VersePair{10:2}{Thus saith the Lord, Learn ye not the ways of the heathen, and be not alarmed at the signs of the sky; for they are alarmed at them, falling on their faces.}{10:2}{{\raggedright Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“Don’t learn the way of the nations,}\poemline{2}{and don’t be dismayed at the signs of the sky;}\poemline{2}{for the nations are dismayed at them.}}}
\VersePair{10:3}{For the customs of the nations are vain; it is a tree cut out of the forest, the work of the carpenter, or a molten image.}{10:3}{{\raggedright For the customs of the peoples are vanity; \poemline{2}{for one cuts a tree out of the forest,}\poemline{2}{the work of the hands of the workman with the ax.}}}
\VersePair{10:4}{They are beautified with silver and gold, they fix them with hammers and nails;}{10:4}{{\raggedright They deck it with silver and with gold. \poemline{2}{They fasten it with nails and with hammers,}\poemline{2}{so that it can’t move.}}}
\VersePair{10:5}{they will set them up that they may not move; it is wrought silver, they will not walk,}{10:5}{{\raggedright They are like a palm tree, of turned work, \poemline{2}{and don’t speak.}\poemline{1}{They must be carried,}\poemline{2}{because they can’t move.}\poemline{1}{Don’t be afraid of them;}\poemline{2}{for they can’t do evil,}\poemline{2}{neither is it in them to do good.”}}}
\VersePair{10:6}{}{10:6}{{\raggedright There is no one like you, Yahweh. \poemline{2}{You are great,}\poemline{2}{and your name is great in might.}}}
\VersePair{10:7}{}{10:7}{{\raggedright Who shouldn’t fear you, \poemline{2}{King of the nations?}\poemline{2}{For it belongs to you.}\poemline{1}{Because among all the wise men of the nations,}\poemline{2}{and in all their royal estate,}\poemline{2}{there is no one like you.}}}
\VersePair{10:8}{}{10:8}{{\raggedright But they are together brutish and foolish, \poemline{2}{instructed by idols!}\poemline{2}{It is just wood.}}}
\VersePair{10:9}{it is forged silver brought from Tharsis, gold will come from Mophaz, and the work of goldsmiths: they are all the works of craftsmen, they will clothe themselves with blue and scarlet.}{10:9}{{\raggedright There is silver beaten into plates, which is brought from Tarshish, \poemline{2}{and gold from Uphaz,}\poemline{2}{the work of the engraver and of the hands of the goldsmith.}\poemline{1}{Their clothing is blue and purple.}\poemline{2}{They are all the work of skillful men.}}}
\VersePair{10:10}{}{10:10}{{\raggedright But Yahweh is the true God. \poemline{2}{He is the living God,}\poemline{2}{and an everlasting King.}\poemline{1}{At his wrath, the earth trembles.}\poemline{2}{The nations aren’t able to withstand his indignation.}}}
\VersePair{10:11}{Thus shall ye say to them, Let the gods which have not made heaven and earth perish from off the earth, and from under this sky.}{10:11}{“You shall say this to them: ‘The gods that have not made the heavens and the earth will perish from the earth, and from under the heavens.’”}
\VersePair{10:12}{It is the Lord that made the earth by his strength, who set up the world by his wisdom, and by his understanding stretched out the sky,}{10:12}{{\raggedright God has made the earth by his power. \poemline{2}{He has established the world by his wisdom,}\poemline{2}{and by his understanding has he stretched out the heavens.}}}
\VersePair{10:13}{and set abundance of waters in the sky, and brought up clouds from the ends of the earth; he made lightnings for the rain, and brought forth light out of his treasures.}{10:13}{{\raggedright When he utters his voice, \poemline{2}{the waters in the heavens roar,}\poemline{2}{and he causes the vapors to ascend from the ends of the earth.}\poemline{1}{He makes lightnings for the rain,}\poemline{2}{and brings the wind out of his treasuries.}}}
\VersePair{10:14}{Every man is deprived of knowledge, every goldsmith is confounded because of his graven images; for he has cast false gods, there is no breath in them.}{10:14}{{\raggedright Every man has become brutish and without knowledge. \poemline{2}{Every goldsmith is disappointed by his engraved image;}\poemline{1}{for his molten image is falsehood,}\poemline{2}{and there is no breath in them.}}}
\VersePair{10:15}{They are vain works, wrought in mockery; in the time of their visitation they shall perish.}{10:15}{{\raggedright They are vanity, a work of delusion. \poemline{2}{In the time of their visitation they will perish.}}}
\VersePair{10:16}{Such is not the portion of Jacob; for he that formed all things, he is his inheritance; the Lord is his name.}{10:16}{{\raggedright The portion of Jacob is not like these; \poemline{2}{for he is the maker of all things;}\poemline{1}{and Israel is the tribe of his inheritance.}\poemline{2}{Yahweh of Armies is his name.}}}
\VersePair{10:17}{He has gathered thy substance from without that lodged in choice vessels.}{10:17}{{\raggedright Gather up your wares out of the land, \poemline{2}{you who live under siege.}}}
\VersePair{10:18}{For thus saith the Lord, Behold, I will overthrow the inhabitants of this land with affliction, that thy plague may be discovered.}{10:18}{{\raggedright For Yahweh says, \poemline{2}{“Behold, I will sling out the inhabitants of the land at this time,}\poemline{2}{and will distress them, that they may feel it.”}}}
\VersePair{10:19}{Alas for thy ruin! thy plague is grievous: and I said, Surely this is thy wound, and it has overtaken thee.}{10:19}{{\raggedright Woe is me because of my injury! \poemline{2}{My wound is serious;}\poemline{1}{but I said,}\poemline{2}{“Truly this is my grief, and I must bear it.”}}}
\VersePair{10:20}{Thy tabernacle is in a ruinous state, it has perished; and all thy curtains have been torn asunder: my children and my cattle are no more: there is no more any place for my tabernacle, nor place for my curtains.}{10:20}{{\raggedright My tent has been destroyed, \poemline{2}{and all my cords are broken.}\poemline{1}{My children have gone away from me, and they are no more.}\poemline{2}{There is no one to spread my tent any more,}\poemline{2}{to set up my curtains.}}}
\VersePair{10:21}{For the shepherds have become foolish, and have not sought the Lord; therefore the whole pasture has failed, and the sheep have been scattered.}{10:21}{{\raggedright For the shepherds have become brutish, \poemline{2}{and have not inquired of Yahweh.}\poemline{1}{Therefore they have not prospered,}\poemline{2}{and all their flocks have scattered.}}}
\VersePair{10:22}{Behold, there comes a sound of a noise, and a great earthquake from the land of the north, to make the cities of Juda a desolation, and a resting-place for ostriches.}{10:22}{{\raggedright The voice of news, behold, it comes, \poemline{2}{and a great commotion out of the north country,}\poemline{1}{to make the cities of Judah a desolation,}\poemline{2}{a dwelling place of jackals.}}}
\VersePair{10:23}{I know, O Lord, that man's way is not his own; neither shall a man go, and direct his going.}{10:23}{{\raggedright Yahweh, I know that the way of man is not in himself. \poemline{2}{It is not in man who walks to direct his steps.}}}
\VersePair{10:24}{Chasten us, O Lord, but with judgment; and not in wrath, lest thou make us few.}{10:24}{{\raggedright Yahweh, correct me, but gently; \poemline{2}{not in your anger,}\poemline{2}{lest you reduce me to nothing.}}}
\VersePair{10:25}{Pour out thy wrath upon the nations that have not known thee, and upon the families that have not called upon thy name: for they have devoured Jacob, and consumed him, and have made his pasture desolate.}{10:25}{{\raggedright Pour out your wrath on the nations that don’t know you, \poemline{2}{and on the families that don’t call on your name;}\poemline{1}{for they have devoured Jacob.}\poemline{2}{Yes, they have devoured him, consumed him,}\poemline{2}{and have laid waste his habitation.}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{11}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{11:1}{The word that came to Jeremias from the Lord, saying,}{11:1}{The word that came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, saying,}
\VersePair{11:2}{Hear ye the words of this covenant, and thou shalt speak to the men of Juda, and to the dwellers in Jerusalem;}{11:2}{“Hear the words of this covenant, and speak to the men of Judah, and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem;}
\VersePair{11:3}{and thou shalt say to them, Thus saith the Lord God of Israel, Cursed is the man, who shall not hearken to the words of this covenant,}{11:3}{and say to them, Yahweh, the God of Israel says: ‘Cursed is the man who doesn’t hear the words of this covenant,}
\VersePair{11:4}{which I commanded your fathers, in the day wherein I brought them up out of the land of Egypt, out of the iron furnace, saying, Hearken to my voice, and do all things that I shall command you; so shall ye be to me a people, and I will be to you a God;}{11:4}{which I commanded your fathers in the day that I brought them out of the land of Egypt, out of the iron furnace,’ saying, ‘Obey my voice and do them, according to all which I command you; so you shall be my people, and I will be your God;}
\VersePair{11:5}{that I may confirm mine oath, which I sware to your fathers, to give them a land flowing with milk and honey, as it is this day. Then I answered and said, So be it, O Lord.}{11:5}{that I may establish the oath which I swore to your fathers, to give them a land flowing with milk and honey,’ as it is today.” Then I answered, and said, “Amen, Yahweh.”}
\VersePair{11:6}{And the Lord said to me, Read these words in the cities of Juda, and in the streets of Jerusalem, saying, Hear ye the words of this covenant, and do them.}{11:6}{Yahweh said to me, “Proclaim all these words in the cities of Judah, and in the streets of Jerusalem, saying, ‘Hear the words of this covenant, and do them.}
\VersePair{11:7}{}{11:7}{For I earnestly protested to your fathers in the day that I brought them up out of the land of Egypt, even to this day, rising early and protesting, saying, “Obey my voice.”}
\VersePair{11:8}{But they did them not.}{11:8}{Yet they didn’t obey, nor turn their ear, but everyone walked in the stubbornness of their evil heart. Therefore I brought on them all the words of this covenant, which I commanded them to do, but they didn’t do them.’”}
\VersePair{11:9}{And the Lord said to me, A conspiracy is found among the men of Juda, and among the dwellers in Jerusalem.}{11:9}{Yahweh said to me, “A conspiracy is found among the men of Judah, and among the inhabitants of Jerusalem.}
\VersePair{11:10}{They are turned aside to the iniquities of their fathers that were of old, who would not hearken to my words: and, behold, they go after strange gods, to serve them: and the house of Israel and the house of Juda have broken my covenant, which I made with their fathers.}{11:10}{They have turned back to the iniquities of their forefathers, who refused to hear my words. They have gone after other gods to serve them. The house of Israel and the house of Judah have broken my covenant which I made with their fathers.}
\VersePair{11:11}{Therefore thus saith the Lord, Behold, I bring evils upon this people, out of which they shall not be able to come forth; and they shall presently cry to me, but I will not hearken to them.}{11:11}{Therefore Yahweh says, ‘Behold, I will bring evil on them which they will not be able to escape; and they will cry to me, but I will not listen to them.}
\VersePair{11:12}{And the cities of Juda and the dwellers in Jerusalem shall go, and cry to the gods to whom they burn incense; which shall not deliver them in the time of their troubles.}{11:12}{Then the cities of Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem will go and cry to the gods to which they offer incense, but they will not save them at all in the time of their trouble.}
\VersePair{11:13}{For according to the number of thy cities were thy gods, O Juda; and according to the number of the streets of Jerusalem have ye set up altars to burn incense to Baal.}{11:13}{For according to the number of your cities are your gods, Judah; and according to the number of the streets of Jerusalem you have set up altars to the shameful thing, even altars to burn incense to Baal.’}
\VersePair{11:14}{And thou, pray not for this people, and intercede not for them in supplication and prayer: for I will not hear in the day in which they call upon me, in the day of their affliction.}{11:14}{“Therefore don’t pray for this people. Don’t lift up cry or prayer for them; for I will not hear them in the time that they cry to me because of their trouble.}
\VersePair{11:15}{Why has my beloved wrought abomination in my house? will prayers and holy offerings take away thy wickedness from thee, or shalt thou escape by these things?}{11:15}{{\raggedright What has my beloved to do in my house, \poemline{2}{since she has behaved lewdly with many,}\poemline{2}{and the holy flesh has passed from you?}\poemline{1}{When you do evil,}\poemline{2}{then you rejoice.”}}}
\VersePair{11:16}{The Lord called thy name a fair olive tree, of a goodly shade in appearance, at the noise of its being lopped, fire was kindled against it; great is the affliction coming upon thee: her branches are become good for nothing.}{11:16}{{\raggedright Yahweh called your name, “A green olive tree, \poemline{2}{beautiful with goodly fruit.”}\poemline{1}{With the noise of a great roar he has kindled fire on it,}\poemline{2}{and its branches are broken.}}}
\VersePair{11:17}{And the Lord that planted thee has pronounced evils against thee, because of the iniquity of the house of Israel and the house of Juda, whatsoever they have done against themselves to provoke me to anger by burning incense to Baal.}{11:17}{For Yahweh of Armies, who planted you, has pronounced evil against you, because of the evil of the house of Israel and of the house of Judah, which they have done to themselves in provoking me to anger by offering incense to Baal.}
\VersePair{11:18}{O Lord, teach me, and I shall know: then I saw their practices.}{11:18}{Yahweh gave me knowledge of it, and I knew it. Then you showed me their doings.}
\VersePair{11:19}{But I as an innocent lamb led to the slaughter, knew not: against me they devised an evil device, saying, Come and let us put wood into his bread, and let us utterly destroy him from off the land of the living, and let his name not be remembered any more.}{11:19}{{\raggedright But I was like a gentle lamb that is led to the slaughter. I didn’t know that they had devised plans against me, saying, \poemline{1}{“Let’s destroy the tree with its fruit,}\poemline{2}{and let’s cut him off from the land of the living,}\poemline{2}{that his name may be no more remembered.”}}}
\VersePair{11:20}{O Lord, that judgest righteously, trying the reins and hearts, let me see thy vengeance taken upon them, for to thee I have declared my cause.}{11:20}{{\raggedright But, Yahweh of Armies, who judges righteously, \poemline{2}{who tests the heart and the mind,}\poemline{1}{I will see your vengeance on them;}\poemline{2}{for to you I have revealed my cause.}}}
\VersePair{11:21}{Therefore thus saith the Lord concerning the men of Anathoth, that seek my life, that say, Thou shalt not prophesy at all in the name of the Lord, but if thou dost, thou shalt die by our hands:}{11:21}{“Therefore Yahweh says concerning the men of Anathoth, who seek your life, saying, ‘You shall not prophesy in Yahweh’s name, that you not die by our hand ’—}
\VersePair{11:22}{behold, I will visit them: their young men shall die by the sword; and their sons and their daughters shall die of famine:}{11:22}{therefore Yahweh of Armies says, ‘Behold, I will punish them. The young men will die by the sword. Their sons and their daughters will die by famine.}
\VersePair{11:23}{and there shall be no remnant left of them; for I will bring evil upon the dwellers in Anathoth, in the year of their visitation.}{11:23}{There will be no remnant to them, for I will bring evil on the men of Anathoth, even the year of their visitation.’”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{12}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{12:1}{Righteous art thou, O Lord, that I may make my defence to thee, yea, I will speak to thee of judgments. Why is it that the way of ungodly men prospers? that all that deal very treacherously are flourishing?}{12:1}{{\raggedright You are righteous, Yahweh, \poemline{2}{when I contend with you;}\poemline{1}{yet I would like to plead a case with you.}\poemline{2}{Why does the way of the wicked prosper?}\poemline{2}{Why are they all at ease who deal very treacherously?}}}
\VersePair{12:2}{Thou hast planted them, and they have taken root; they have begotten children, and become fruitful; thou art near to their mouth, and far from their reins.}{12:2}{{\raggedright You have planted them. Yes, they have taken root. \poemline{2}{They grow. Yes, they produce fruit.}\poemline{1}{You are near in their mouth,}\poemline{2}{and far from their heart.}}}
\VersePair{12:3}{But thou, Lord, knowest me; thou hast proved my heart before thee; purify them for the day of their slaughter.}{12:3}{{\raggedright But you, Yahweh, know me. \poemline{2}{You see me, and test my heart toward you.}\poemline{1}{Pull them out like sheep for the slaughter,}\poemline{2}{and prepare them for the day of slaughter.}}}
\VersePair{12:4}{How long shall the land mourn, and the grass of the field wither, for the wickedness of them that dwell in it? the beasts and birds are utterly destroyed; because the people said, God shall not see our ways.}{12:4}{{\raggedright How long will the land mourn, \poemline{2}{and the herbs of the whole country wither?}\poemline{1}{Because of the wickedness of those who dwell therein,}\poemline{2}{the animals and birds are consumed;}\poemline{1}{because they said,}\poemline{2}{“He won’t see our latter end.”}}}
\VersePair{12:5}{Thy feet run, and they cause thee to faint; how wilt thou prepare to ride upon horses? and thou hast been confident in the land of thy peace? how wilt thou do in the roaring of Jordan?}{12:5}{{\raggedright “If you have run with the footmen, \poemline{2}{and they have wearied you,}\poemline{2}{then how can you contend with horses?}\poemline{1}{Though in a land of peace you are secure,}\poemline{2}{yet how will you do in the pride of the Jordan?}}}
\VersePair{12:6}{For even thy brethren and the house of thy father, even these have dealt treacherously with thee; and they have cried out, they are gathered together in pursuit of thee; trust not thou in them, though they shall speak fair words to thee.}{12:6}{{\raggedright For even your brothers, and the house of your father, \poemline{2}{even they have dealt treacherously with you!}\poemline{2}{Even they have cried aloud after you!}\poemline{1}{Don’t believe them,}\poemline{2}{though they speak beautiful words to you.}}}
\VersePair{12:7}{I have forsaken mine house, I have left mine heritage; I have given my beloved one into the hands of her enemies.}{12:7}{{\raggedright “I have forsaken my house. \poemline{2}{I have cast off my heritage.}\poemline{2}{I have given the dearly beloved of my soul into the hand of her enemies.}}}
\VersePair{12:8}{My inheritance has become to me as a lion in a forest; she has uttered her voice against me; therefore have I hated her.}{12:8}{{\raggedright My heritage has become to me as a lion in the forest. \poemline{2}{She has uttered her voice against me.}\poemline{2}{Therefore I have hated her.}}}
\VersePair{12:9}{Is not my inheritance to me a hyæna's cave, or a cave round about her? Go ye, gather together all the wild beasts of the field, and let them come to devour her.}{12:9}{{\raggedright Is my heritage to me as a speckled bird of prey? \poemline{2}{Are the birds of prey against her all around?}\poemline{1}{Go, assemble all the animals of the field.}\poemline{2}{Bring them to devour.}}}
\VersePair{12:10}{Many shepherds have destroyed my vineyard, they have defiled my portion, they have made my desirable portion a trackless wilderness;}{12:10}{{\raggedright Many shepherds have destroyed my vineyard. \poemline{2}{They have trodden my portion under foot.}\poemline{2}{They have made my pleasant portion a desolate wilderness.}}}
\VersePair{12:11}{it is made a complete ruin: for my sake the whole land has been utterly ruined, because there is none that lays the matter to heart.}{12:11}{{\raggedright They have made it a desolation. \poemline{2}{It mourns to me, being desolate.}\poemline{1}{The whole land is made desolate,}\poemline{2}{because no one cares.}}}
\VersePair{12:12}{The ravagers are come to every passage in the wilderness: for the sword of the Lord will devour from one end of the land to the other: no flesh has any peace.}{12:12}{{\raggedright Destroyers have come on all the bare heights in the wilderness; \poemline{2}{for the sword of Yahweh devours from the one end of the land even to the other end of the land.}\poemline{2}{No flesh has peace.}}}
\VersePair{12:13}{Sow wheat, and reap thorns; their portions shall not profit them: be ashamed of your boasting, because of reproach before the Lord.}{12:13}{{\raggedright They have sown wheat, \poemline{2}{and have reaped thorns.}\poemline{1}{They have exhausted themselves,}\poemline{2}{and profit nothing.}\poemline{1}{You will be ashamed of your fruits,}\poemline{2}{because of Yahweh’s fierce anger.”}}}
\VersePair{12:14}{For thus saith the Lord concerning all the evil neighbours that touch mine inheritance, which I have divided to my people Israel; Behold, I will draw them away from their land, and I will cast out Juda from the midst of them.}{12:14}{Yahweh says, “Concerning all my evil neighbors, who touch the inheritance which I have caused my people Israel to inherit: Behold, I will pluck them up from off their land, and will pluck up the house of Judah from among them.}
\VersePair{12:15}{And it shall come to pass, after I have cast them out, that I will return, and have mercy upon them, and will cause them to dwell every one in his inheritance, and every one in his land.}{12:15}{It will happen that after I have plucked them up, I will return and have compassion on them. I will bring them again, every man to his heritage, and every man to his land.}
\VersePair{12:16}{And it shall be, if they will indeed learn the way of my people, to swear by my name, saying, The Lord lives; as they taught my people to swear by Baal; then shall that nation be built in the midst of my people.}{12:16}{It will happen, if they will diligently learn the ways of my people, to swear by my name, ‘As Yahweh lives;’ even as they taught my people to swear by Baal, then they will be built up in the middle of my people.}
\VersePair{12:17}{But if they will not return, then will I cut off that nation with utter ruin and destruction.}{12:17}{But if they will not hear, then I will pluck up that nation, plucking up and destroying it,” says Yahweh.}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{13}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{13:1}{Thus saith the Lord, Go and procure for thyself a linen girdle, and put it about thy loins, and let it not be put in water.}{13:1}{Yahweh said to me, “Go, and buy yourself a linen belt, and put it on your waist, and don’t put it in water.”}
\VersePair{13:2}{So I procured the girdle according to the word of the Lord, and put it about my loins.}{13:2}{So I bought a belt according to Yahweh’s word, and put it on my waist.}
\VersePair{13:3}{And the word of the Lord came to me, saying,}{13:3}{Yahweh’s word came to me the second time, saying,}
\VersePair{13:4}{Take the girdle that is upon thy loins, and arise, and go to the Euphrates, and hide it there in a hole of the rock.}{13:4}{“Take the belt that you have bought, which is on your waist, and arise, go to the Euphrates, and hide it there in a cleft of the rock.”}
\VersePair{13:5}{So I went, and hid it by the Euphrates, as the Lord commanded me.}{13:5}{So I went and hid it by the Euphrates, as Yahweh commanded me.}
\VersePair{13:6}{And it came to pass after many days, that the Lord said to me, Arise, go to the Euphrates, and take thence the girdle, which I commanded thee to hide there.}{13:6}{After many days, Yahweh said to me, “Arise, go to the Euphrates, and take the belt from there, which I commanded you to hide there.”}
\VersePair{13:7}{So I went to the river Euphrates, and dug, and took the girdle out of the place where I had buried it: and, behold, it was rotten, utterly good for nothing.}{13:7}{Then I went to the Euphrates, and dug, and took the belt from the place where I had hidden it; and behold, the belt was ruined. It was profitable for nothing.}
\VersePair{13:8}{And the word of the Lord came to me, saying, Thus saith the Lord,}{13:8}{Then Yahweh’s word came to me, saying,}
\VersePair{13:9}{Thus will I mar the pride of Juda, and the pride of Jerusalem;}{13:9}{“Yahweh says, ‘In this way I will ruin the pride of Judah, and the great pride of Jerusalem.}
\VersePair{13:10}{even this great pride of the men that will not hearken to my words, and have gone after strange gods, to serve them, and to worship them: and they shall be as this girdle, which can be used for nothing.}{13:10}{This evil people, who refuse to hear my words, who walk in the stubbornness of their heart, and have gone after other gods to serve them and to worship them, will even be as this belt, which is profitable for nothing.}
\VersePair{13:11}{For as a girdle cleaves about the loins of a man, so have I caused to cleave to myself the house of Israel, and the whole house of Juda; that they might be to me a famous people, and a praise, and a glory: but they did not hearken to me.}{13:11}{For as the belt clings to the waist of a man, so I have caused the whole house of Israel and the whole house of Judah to cling to me,’ says Yahweh; ‘that they may be to me for a people, for a name, for praise, and for glory; but they would not hear.’}
\VersePair{13:12}{And thou shalt say to this people, Every bottle shall be filled with wine: and it shall come to pass, if they shall say to thee, Shall we not certainly know that every bottle shall be filled with wine? that thou shalt say to them,}{13:12}{“Therefore you shall speak to them this word: ‘Yahweh, the God of Israel says, “Every container should be filled with wine.”’ They will tell you, ‘Do we not certainly know that every container should be filled with wine?’}
\VersePair{13:13}{Thus saith the Lord, Behold, I will fill the inhabitants of this land, and their kings the sons of David that sit upon their throne, and the priests, and the prophets, and Juda and all the dwellers in Jerusalem, with strong drink.}{13:13}{Then tell them, ‘Yahweh says, “Behold, I will fill all the inhabitants of this land, even the kings who sit on David’s throne, the priests, the prophets, and all the inhabitants of Jerusalem, with drunkenness.}
\VersePair{13:14}{And I will scatter them a man and his brother, and their fathers and their sons together: I will not have compassion, saith the Lord, and I will not spare, neither will I pity to save them from destruction.}{13:14}{I will dash them one against another, even the fathers and the sons together,” says Yahweh: “I will not pity, spare, or have compassion, that I should not destroy them.”’”}
\VersePair{13:15}{Hear ye, and give ear, and be not proud: for the Lord has spoken.}{13:15}{{\raggedright Hear, and give ear. \poemline{2}{Don’t be proud,}\poemline{2}{for Yahweh has spoken.}}}
\VersePair{13:16}{Give glory to the Lord your God, before he cause darkness, and before your feet stumble on the dark mountains, and ye shall wait for light, and behold the shadow of death, and they shall be brought into darkness.}{13:16}{{\raggedright Give glory to Yahweh your God, \poemline{2}{before he causes darkness,}\poemline{2}{and before your feet stumble on the dark mountains,}\poemline{1}{and while you look for light,}\poemline{2}{he turns it into the shadow of death,}\poemline{2}{and makes it deep darkness.}}}
\VersePair{13:17}{But if ye will not hearken, your soul shall weep in secret because of pride, and your eyes shall pour down tears, because the Lord's flock is sorely bruised.}{13:17}{{\raggedright But if you will not hear it, \poemline{2}{my soul will weep in secret for your pride.}\poemline{1}{My eye will weep bitterly,}\poemline{2}{and run down with tears,}\poemline{2}{because Yahweh’s flock has been taken captive.}}}
\VersePair{13:18}{Say ye to the king and the princes, Humble yourselves, and sit down; for your crown of glory is removed from your head.}{13:18}{{\raggedright Say to the king and to the queen mother, \poemline{2}{“Humble yourselves.}\poemline{1}{Sit down, for your crowns have come down,}\poemline{2}{even the crown of your glory.}}}
\VersePair{13:19}{The cities toward the south were shut, and there was none to open them: Juda is removed into captivity, they have suffered a complete removal.}{13:19}{{\raggedright The cities of the South are shut up, \poemline{2}{and there is no one to open them.}\poemline{1}{Judah is carried away captive: all of them.}\poemline{2}{They are wholly carried away captive.}}}
\VersePair{13:20}{Lift up thine eyes, O Jerusalem, and behold them that come from the north; where is the flock that was given thee, the sheep of thy glory?}{13:20}{{\raggedright Lift up your eyes, \poemline{2}{and see those who come from the north.}\poemline{1}{Where is the flock that was given to you,}\poemline{2}{your beautiful flock?}}}
\VersePair{13:21}{What wilt thou say when they shall visit thee, for thou didst teach them lessons for rule against thyself; shall not pangs seize thee as a woman in travail?}{13:21}{{\raggedright What will you say when he sets over you as head those whom you have yourself taught to be friends to you? \poemline{2}{Won’t sorrows take hold of you, as of a woman in travail?}}}
\VersePair{13:22}{And if thou shouldest say in thine heart, Wherefore have these things happened to me? Because of the abundance of thine iniquity have thy skirts been discovered, that thine heels might be exposed.}{13:22}{{\raggedright If you say in your heart, \poemline{2}{“Why have these things come on me?”}\poemline{1}{Your skirts are uncovered because of the greatness of your iniquity,}\poemline{2}{and your heels suffer violence.}}}
\VersePair{13:23}{If the Ethiopian shall change his skin, or the leopardess her spots, then shall ye be able to do good, having learnt evil.}{13:23}{{\raggedright Can the Ethiopian change his skin, \poemline{2}{or the leopard his spots?}\poemline{1}{Then may you also do good,}\poemline{2}{who are accustomed to do evil.}}}
\VersePair{13:24}{So I scattered them as sticks carried by the wind into the wilderness.}{13:24}{{\raggedright “Therefore I will scatter them \poemline{2}{as the stubble that passes away}\poemline{2}{by the wind of the wilderness.}}}
\VersePair{13:25}{Thus is thy lot, and the reward of your disobedience to me, saith the Lord; as thou didst forget me, and trust in lies,}{13:25}{{\raggedright This is your lot, \poemline{2}{the portion measured to you from me,” says Yahweh,}\poemline{1}{“because you have forgotten me,}\poemline{2}{and trusted in falsehood.”}}}
\VersePair{13:26}{I also will expose thy skirts upon thy face, and thy shame shall be seen;}{13:26}{{\raggedright Therefore I will also uncover your skirts on your face, \poemline{2}{and your shame will appear.}}}
\VersePair{13:27}{thine adultery also, and thy neighing, and the looseness of thy fornication: on the hills and in the fields I have seen thine abominations. Woe to thee, O Jerusalem, for thou hast not been purified so as to follow me; how long yet shall it be?}{13:27}{{\raggedright I have seen your abominations, even your adulteries \poemline{2}{and your neighing, the lewdness of your prostitution,}\poemline{2}{on the hills in the field.}\poemline{1}{Woe to you, Jerusalem!}\poemline{2}{You will not be made clean.}\poemline{2}{How long will it yet be?”}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{14}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{14:1}{And the Word of the Lord came to Jeremias concerning the Drought.}{14:1}{This is Yahweh’s word that came to Jeremiah concerning the drought:}
\VersePair{14:2}{Judea has mourned, and her gates are emptied, and are darkened upon the earth; and the cry of Jerusalem is gone up.}{14:2}{{\raggedright “Judah mourns, \poemline{2}{and its gates languish.}\poemline{1}{They sit in black on the ground.}\poemline{2}{The cry of Jerusalem goes up.}}}
\VersePair{14:3}{And her nobles have sent their little ones to the water: they came to the wells, and found no water: and brought back their vessels empty.}{14:3}{{\raggedright Their nobles send their little ones to the waters. \poemline{2}{They come to the cisterns,}\poemline{2}{and find no water.}\poemline{1}{They return with their vessels empty.}\poemline{2}{They are disappointed and confounded,}\poemline{2}{and cover their heads.}}}
\VersePair{14:4}{And the labours of the land failed, because there was no rain: the husbandmen were ashamed, they covered their heads.}{14:4}{{\raggedright Because of the ground which is cracked, \poemline{2}{because no rain has been in the land,}\poemline{1}{the plowmen are disappointed.}\poemline{2}{They cover their heads.}}}
\VersePair{14:5}{And hinds calved in the field, and forsook it, because there was no grass.}{14:5}{{\raggedright Yes, the doe in the field also calves and forsakes her young, \poemline{2}{because there is no grass.}}}
\VersePair{14:6}{The wild asses stood by the forests, and snuffed up the wind; their eyes failed, because there was no grass.}{14:6}{{\raggedright The wild donkeys stand on the bare heights. \poemline{2}{They pant for air like jackals.}\poemline{1}{Their eyes fail,}\poemline{2}{because there is no vegetation.}}}
\VersePair{14:7}{Our sins have risen up against us: O Lord, do thou for us for thine own sake; for our sins are many before thee; for we have sinned against thee.}{14:7}{{\raggedright Though our iniquities testify against us, \poemline{2}{work for your name’s sake, Yahweh;}\poemline{1}{for our rebellions are many.}\poemline{2}{We have sinned against you.}}}
\VersePair{14:8}{O Lord, thou art the hope of Israel, and deliverest us in time of troubles; why art thou become as a sojourner upon the land, or as one born in the land, yet turning aside for a resting-place?}{14:8}{{\raggedright You hope of Israel, \poemline{2}{its Savior in the time of trouble,}\poemline{1}{why should you be as a foreigner in the land,}\poemline{2}{and as a wayfaring man who turns aside to stay for a night?}}}
\VersePair{14:9}{Wilt thou be as a man asleep, or as a strong man that cannot save? yet thou art among us, O Lord, and thy name is called upon us; forget us not.}{14:9}{{\raggedright Why should you be like a scared man, \poemline{2}{as a mighty man who can’t save?}\poemline{1}{Yet you, Yahweh, are in the middle of us,}\poemline{2}{and we are called by your name.}\poemline{2}{Don’t leave us.}}}
\VersePair{14:10}{Thus saith the Lord to this people, They have loved to wander, and they have not spared, therefore God has not prospered them; now will he remember their iniquity.}{14:10}{{\raggedright Yahweh says to this people: \poemline{1}{“Even so they have loved to wander.}\poemline{2}{They have not restrained their feet.}\poemline{1}{Therefore Yahweh does not accept them.}\poemline{2}{Now he will remember their iniquity,}\poemline{2}{and punish them for their sins.”}}}
\VersePair{14:11}{And the Lord said to me, Pray not for this people for their good:}{14:11}{Yahweh said to me, “Don’t pray for this people for their good.}
\VersePair{14:12}{for though they fast, I will not hear their supplication; and though they offer whole-burnt-offerings and sacrifices, I will take no pleasure in them: for I will consume them with sword, and with famine, and with pestilence.}{14:12}{When they fast, I will not hear their cry; and when they offer burnt offering and meal offering, I will not accept them; but I will consume them by the sword, by famine, and by pestilence.”}
\VersePair{14:13}{And I said, O ever living Lord! behold, their prophets prophesy, and say, Ye shall not see a sword, nor shall famine be among you; for I will give truth and peace on the land, and in this place.}{14:13}{Then I said, “Ah, Lord Yahweh! Behold, the prophets tell them, ‘You will not see the sword, neither will you have famine; but I will give you assured peace in this place.’”}
\VersePair{14:14}{Then the Lord said to me, The prophets prophesy lies in my name: I sent them not, and I commanded them not, and I spoke not to them: for they prophesy to you false visions, and divinations, and auguries, and devices of their own heart.}{14:14}{Then Yahweh said to me, “The prophets prophesy lies in my name. I didn’t send them. I didn’t command them. I didn’t speak to them. They prophesy to you a lying vision, divination, and a thing of nothing, and the deceit of their own heart.}
\VersePair{14:15}{Therefore thus saith the Lord concerning the prophets that prophesy lies in my name, and I sent them not, who say, Sword and famine shall not be upon this land; they shall die by a grievous death, and the prophets shall be consumed by famine.}{14:15}{Therefore Yahweh says concerning the prophets who prophesy in my name, but I didn’t send them, yet they say, ‘Sword and famine will not be in this land.’ Those prophets will be consumed by sword and famine.}
\VersePair{14:16}{And the people to whom they prophesy, they also shall be cast out in the streets of Jerusalem, because of the sword and famine; and there shall be none to bury them: their wives also, and their sons, and their daughters shall die thus; and I will pour out their wickedness upon them.}{14:16}{The people to whom they prophesy will be cast out in the streets of Jerusalem because of the famine and the sword. They will have no one to bury them — them, their wives, their sons, or their daughters, for I will pour their wickedness on them.}
\VersePair{14:17}{And thou shalt speak this word to them; Let your eyes shed tears day and night, and let them not cease: for the daughter of my people has been sorely bruised, and her plague is very grievous.}{14:17}{{\raggedright “You shall say this word to them: \poemline{1}{“‘Let my eyes run down with tears night and day,}\poemline{2}{and let them not cease;}\poemline{1}{for the virgin daughter of my people is broken with a great breach,}\poemline{2}{with a very grievous wound.}}}
\VersePair{14:18}{If I go forth into the plain, then behold the slain by the sword! and if I enter into the city, then behold the distress of famine! for priest and prophet have gone to a land which they knew not.}{14:18}{{\raggedright If I go out into the field, \poemline{2}{then behold, the slain with the sword!}\poemline{1}{If I enter into the city,}\poemline{2}{then behold, those who are sick with famine!}\poemline{1}{For both the prophet and the priest go about in the land,}\poemline{2}{and have no knowledge.’”}}}
\VersePair{14:19}{Hast thou utterly rejected Juda? and has thy soul departed from Sion? wherefore hast thou smitten us, and there is no healing for us? we waited for peace, but there was no prosperity; for a time of healing, and behold trouble!}{14:19}{{\raggedright Have you utterly rejected Judah? \poemline{2}{Has your soul loathed Zion?}\poemline{1}{Why have you struck us, and there is no healing for us?}\poemline{2}{We looked for peace, but no good came;}\poemline{2}{and for a time of healing, and behold, dismay!}}}
\VersePair{14:20}{We know, O Lord, our sins, and the iniquities of our fathers: for we have sinned before thee.}{14:20}{{\raggedright We acknowledge, Yahweh, our wickedness, \poemline{2}{and the iniquity of our fathers;}\poemline{2}{for we have sinned against you.}}}
\VersePair{14:21}{Refrain for thy name's sake, destroy not the throne of thy glory: remember, break not thy covenant with us.}{14:21}{{\raggedright Do not abhor us, for your name’s sake. \poemline{2}{Do not disgrace the throne of your glory.}\poemline{2}{Remember, and don’t break your covenant with us.}}}
\VersePair{14:22}{Is there any one among the idols of the Gentiles that can give rain? and will the sky yield his fulness at their bidding? Art not thou he? we will even wait on thee, O Lord: for thou hast made all these things.}{14:22}{{\raggedright Are there any among the vanities of the nations that can cause rain? \poemline{2}{Or can the sky give showers?}\poemline{2}{Aren’t you he, Yahweh our God?}\poemline{1}{Therefore we will wait for you;}\poemline{2}{for you have made all these things.}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{15}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{15:1}{And the Lord said to me, Though Moses and Samuel stood before my face, my soul could not be toward them: dismiss this people, and let them go forth.}{15:1}{Then Yahweh said to me, “Though Moses and Samuel stood before me, yet my mind would not turn toward this people. Cast them out of my sight, and let them go out!}
\VersePair{15:2}{And it shall be, if they say to thee, Whither shall we go forth? then thou shalt say to them, Thus saith the Lord; As many as are for death, to death; and as many as are for famine, to famine; and as many as are for the sword, to the sword; and as many as are for captivity, to captivity.}{15:2}{{\raggedright It will happen when they ask you, ‘Where shall we go out?’ then you shall tell them, ‘Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Such as are for death, to death;}\poemline{1}{such as are for the sword, to the sword;}\poemline{1}{such as are for the famine, to the famine;}\poemline{1}{and such as are for captivity, to captivity.”’}}}
\VersePair{15:3}{And I will punish them with four kinds of death, saith the Lord, the sword to slay, and the dogs to tear, and the wild beasts of the earth, and the birds of the sky to devour and destroy.}{15:3}{“I will appoint over them four kinds,” says Yahweh: “the sword to kill, the dogs to tear, the birds of the sky, and the animals of the earth, to devour and to destroy.}
\VersePair{15:4}{And I will deliver them up for distress to all the kingdoms of the earth, because of Manasses son of Ezekias king of Juda, for all that he did in Jerusalem.}{15:4}{I will cause them to be tossed back and forth among all the kingdoms of the earth, because of Manasseh, the son of Hezekiah, king of Judah, for that which he did in Jerusalem.}
\VersePair{15:5}{Who will spare thee, O Jerusalem? and who will fear for thee? or who will turn back to ask for thy welfare?}{15:5}{{\raggedright For who will have pity on you, Jerusalem? \poemline{2}{Who will mourn you?}\poemline{2}{Who will come to ask of your welfare?}}}
\VersePair{15:6}{Thou hast turned away from me, saith the Lord, thou wilt go back: therefore I will stretch out my hand, and will destroy thee, and will no more spare them.}{15:6}{{\raggedright You have rejected me,” says Yahweh. \poemline{2}{“You have gone backward.}\poemline{1}{Therefore I have stretched out my hand against you}\poemline{2}{and destroyed you.}\poemline{2}{I am weary of showing compassion.}}}
\VersePair{15:7}{And I will completely scatter them; in the gates of my people they are bereaved of children: they have destroyed my people because of their iniquities.}{15:7}{{\raggedright I have winnowed them with a fan in the gates of the land. \poemline{2}{I have bereaved them of children.}\poemline{1}{I have destroyed my people.}\poemline{2}{They didn’t return from their ways.}}}
\VersePair{15:8}{Their widows have been multiplied more than the sand of the sea: I have brought young men against the mother, even distress at noon-day: I have suddenly cast upon her trembling and anxiety.}{15:8}{{\raggedright Their widows are increased more than the sand of the seas. \poemline{2}{I have brought on them against the mother of the young men a destroyer at noonday.}\poemline{2}{I have caused anguish and terrors to fall on her suddenly.}}}
\VersePair{15:9}{She that bore seven is spent; her soul has fainted under trouble; her sun is gone down while it is yet noon; she is ashamed and disgraced: I will give the remnant of them to the sword before their enemies.}{15:9}{{\raggedright She who has borne seven languishes. \poemline{2}{She has given up the spirit.}\poemline{1}{Her sun has gone down while it was yet day.}\poemline{2}{She has been disappointed and confounded.}\poemline{2}{I will deliver their residue to the sword before their enemies,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{15:10}{Woe is me, my mother! thou hast born me as some man of strife, and at variance with the whole earth; I have not helped others, nor has any one helped me; my strength has failed among them that curse me.}{15:10}{{\raggedright Woe is me, my mother, that you have borne me, a man of strife, \poemline{2}{and a man of contention to the whole earth!}\poemline{1}{I have not lent, neither have men lent to me;}\poemline{2}{yet every one of them curses me.}}}
\VersePair{15:11}{Be it so, Lord, in their prosperity; surely I stood before thee in the time of their calamities, and in the time of their affliction, for their good against the enemy.}{15:11}{{\raggedright Yahweh said, \poemline{1}{“Most certainly I will strengthen you for good.}\poemline{2}{Most certainly I will cause the enemy to make supplication to you in the time of evil}\poemline{2}{and in the time of affliction.}}}
\VersePair{15:12}{Will iron be known? whereas thy strength is a brazen covering.}{15:12}{{\raggedright Can one break iron, \poemline{2}{even iron from the north, and bronze?}}}
\VersePair{15:13}{Yea, I will give thy treasures for a spoil as a recompence, because of all thy sins, and that in all thy borders.}{15:13}{{\raggedright I will give your substance and your treasures for a plunder without price, \poemline{2}{and that for all your sins,}\poemline{2}{even in all your borders.}}}
\VersePair{15:14}{And I will enslave thee to thine enemies round about, in a land which thou hast not known; for a fire has been kindled out of my wrath; it shall burn upon you.}{15:14}{{\raggedright I will make them to pass with your enemies into a land which you don’t know; \poemline{2}{for a fire is kindled in my anger,}\poemline{2}{which will burn on you.”}}}
\VersePair{15:15}{O Lord, remember me, and visit me, and vindicate me before them that persecute me; do not bear long with them; know how I have met with reproach for thy sake, from those who set at nought thy words;}{15:15}{{\raggedright Yahweh, you know. \poemline{2}{Remember me, visit me,}\poemline{2}{and avenge me of my persecutors.}\poemline{1}{You are patient, so don’t take me away.}\poemline{2}{Know that for your sake I have suffered reproach.}}}
\VersePair{15:16}{consume them; and thy word shall be to me for the joy and gladness of my heart: for thy name has been called upon me, O Lord Almighty.}{15:16}{{\raggedright Your words were found, \poemline{2}{and I ate them.}\poemline{1}{Your words were to me a joy and the rejoicing of my heart,}\poemline{2}{for I am called by your name, Yahweh, God of Armies.}}}
\VersePair{15:17}{I have not sat in the assembly of them as they mocked, but I feared because of thy power: I sat alone, for I was filled with bitterness.}{15:17}{{\raggedright I didn’t sit in the assembly of those who make merry and rejoice. \poemline{2}{I sat alone because of your hand,}\poemline{2}{for you have filled me with indignation.}}}
\VersePair{15:18}{Why do they that grieve me prevail against me? my wound is severe; whence shall I be healed? it is indeed become to me as deceitful water, that has no faithfulness.}{15:18}{{\raggedright Why is my pain perpetual, \poemline{2}{and my wound incurable,}\poemline{2}{which refuses to be healed?}\poemline{1}{Will you indeed be to me as a deceitful brook,}\poemline{2}{like waters that fail?}}}
\VersePair{15:19}{Therefore thus saith the Lord, If thou wilt return, then will I restore thee, and thou shalt stand before my face: and if thou wilt bring forth the precious from the worthless, thou shalt be as my mouth: and they shall return to thee; but thou shalt not return to them.}{15:19}{{\raggedright Therefore Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“If you return, then I will bring you again,}\poemline{2}{that you may stand before me;}\poemline{1}{and if you take out the precious from the vile,}\poemline{2}{you will be as my mouth.}\poemline{1}{They will return to you,}\poemline{2}{but you will not return to them.}}}
\VersePair{15:20}{And I will make thee to this people as a strong brazen wall; and they shall fight against thee, but they shall by no means prevail against thee;}{15:20}{{\raggedright I will make you to this people a fortified bronze wall. \poemline{2}{They will fight against you,}\poemline{2}{but they will not prevail against you;}\poemline{1}{for I am with you to save you}\poemline{2}{and to deliver you,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{15:21}{for I am with thee to save thee, and to deliver thee out of the hand of wicked men; and I will ransom thee out of the hand of pestilent men.}{15:21}{{\raggedright “I will deliver you out of the hand of the wicked, \poemline{2}{and I will redeem you out of the hand of the terrible.”}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{16}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{16:1}{And thou shalt not take a wife, saith the Lord God of Israel:}{16:1}{Then Yahweh’s word came to me, saying,}
\VersePair{16:2}{and there shall be no son born to thee, nor daughter in this place.}{16:2}{“You shall not take a wife, neither shall you have sons or daughters, in this place.”}
\VersePair{16:3}{For thus saith the Lord concerning the sons and concerning the daughters that are born in this place, and concerning their mothers that have born them, and concerning their fathers that have begotten them in this land;}{16:3}{For Yahweh says concerning the sons and concerning the daughters who are born in this place, and concerning their mothers who bore them, and concerning their fathers who became their father in this land:}
\VersePair{16:4}{They shall die of grievous death; they shall not be lamented, nor buried; they shall be for an example on the face of the earth; and they shall be for the wild beasts of the land, and for the birds of the sky: they shall fall by the sword, and shall be consumed with famine.}{16:4}{“They will die grievous deaths. They will not be lamented, neither will they be buried. They will be as dung on the surface of the ground. They will be consumed by the sword and by famine. Their dead bodies will be food for the birds of the sky and for the animals of the earth.”}
\VersePair{16:5}{Thus saith the Lord, Enter not into their mourning feast, and go not to lament, and mourn not for them: for I have removed my peace from this people.}{16:5}{For Yahweh says, “Don’t enter into the house of mourning. Don’t go to lament. Don’t bemoan them, for I have taken away my peace from this people,” says Yahweh, “even loving kindness and tender mercies.}
\VersePair{16:6}{They shall not bewail them, nor make cuttings for them, and they shall not shave themselves for them:}{16:6}{Both great and small will die in this land. They will not be buried. Men won’t lament for them, cut themselves, or make themselves bald for them.}
\VersePair{16:7}{and there shall be no bread broken in mourning for them for consolation over the dead: they shall not give one to drink a cup for consolation over his father or his mother.}{16:7}{Men won’t break bread for them in mourning, to comfort them for the dead. Men won’t give them the cup of consolation to drink for their father or for their mother.}
\VersePair{16:8}{Thou shalt not enter into the banquet-house, to sit with them to eat and to drink.}{16:8}{“You shall not go into the house of feasting to sit with them, to eat and to drink.”}
\VersePair{16:9}{For thus saith the Lord God of Israel; Behold, I will make to cease out of this place before your eyes, and in your days, the voice of joy, and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom, and the voice of the bride.}{16:9}{For Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says: “Behold, I will cause to cease out of this place, before your eyes and in your days, the voice of mirth and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom and the voice of the bride.}
\VersePair{16:10}{And it shall come to pass, when thou shalt report to this people all these words, and they shall say to thee, Wherefore has the Lord pronounced against us all these evils? what is our unrighteousness? and what is our sin which we have sinned before the Lord our God?}{16:10}{It will happen, when you tell this people all these words, and they ask you, ‘Why has Yahweh pronounced all this great evil against us?’ or ‘What is our iniquity?’ or ‘What is our sin that we have committed against Yahweh our God?’}
\VersePair{16:11}{Then thou shalt say to them, Because your fathers forsook me, saith the Lord, and went after strange gods and served them, and worshipped them, and forsook me, and kept not my law;}{16:11}{then you shall tell them, ‘Because your fathers have forsaken me,’ says Yahweh, ‘and have walked after other gods, have served them, have worshiped them, have forsaken me, and have not kept my law.}
\VersePair{16:12}{(and ye sinned worse than your fathers; for, behold, ye walk every one after the lusts of your own evil heart, so as not to hearken to me);}{16:12}{You have done evil more than your fathers, for behold, you each walk after the stubbornness of his evil heart, so that you don’t listen to me.}
\VersePair{16:13}{therefore I will cast you off from this good land into a land which neither ye nor your fathers have known; and ye shall serve there other gods, who shall have no mercy upon you.}{16:13}{Therefore I will cast you out of this land into the land that you have not known, neither you nor your fathers. There you will serve other gods day and night, for I will show you no favor.’}
\VersePair{16:14}{Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when they shall no more say, The Lord lives, that brought up the children of Israel out of the land of Egypt;}{16:14}{“Therefore behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, “that it will no more be said, ‘As Yahweh lives, who brought up the children of Israel out of the land of Egypt;’}
\VersePair{16:15}{but, The Lord lives, who brought up the house of Israel from the land of the north, and from all the countries whither they were thrust out: and I will restore them to their own land, which I gave to their fathers.}{16:15}{but, ‘As Yahweh lives, who brought up the children of Israel from the land of the north, and from all the countries where he had driven them.’ I will bring them again into their land that I gave to their fathers.}
\VersePair{16:16}{Behold, I will send many fishers, saith the Lord, and they shall fish them; and afterward I will send many hunters, and they shall hunt them upon every mountain, and upon every hill, and out of the holes of the rocks.}{16:16}{“Behold, I will send for many fishermen,” says Yahweh, “and they will fish them up. Afterward I will send for many hunters, and they will hunt them from every mountain, from every hill, and out of the clefts of the rocks.}
\VersePair{16:17}{For mine eyes are upon all their ways; and their iniquities have not been hidden from mine eyes.}{16:17}{For my eyes are on all their ways. They are not hidden from my face. Their iniquity isn’t concealed from my eyes.}
\VersePair{16:18}{And I will recompense their mischiefs doubly, and their sins, whereby they have profaned my land with the carcases of their abominations, and with their iniquities, whereby they have trespassed against mine inheritance.}{16:18}{First I will recompense their iniquity and their sin double, because they have polluted my land with the carcasses of their detestable things, and have filled my inheritance with their abominations.”}
\VersePair{16:19}{O Lord, thou art my strength, and mine help, and my refuge in days of evil: to thee the Gentiles shall come from the end of the earth, and shall say, How vain were the idols which our fathers procured to themselves, and there is no help in them.}{16:19}{{\raggedright Yahweh, my strength, my stronghold, \poemline{2}{and my refuge in the day of affliction,}\poemline{1}{the nations will come to you from the ends of the earth,}\poemline{2}{and will say,}\poemline{1}{“Our fathers have inherited nothing but lies,}\poemline{2}{vanity and things in which there is no profit.}}}
\VersePair{16:20}{Will a man make gods for himself, whereas these are no gods?}{16:20}{{\raggedright Should a man make to himself gods \poemline{2}{which yet are no gods?”}}}
\VersePair{16:21}{Therefore, behold, I will at this time manifest my hand to them, and will make known to them my power; and they shall know that my name is the Lord.}{16:21}{{\raggedright “Therefore behold, I will cause them to know, \poemline{2}{this once I will cause them to know my hand and my might.}\poemline{2}{Then they will know that my name is Yahweh.”}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{17}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{17:1}{}{17:1}{{\raggedright “The sin of Judah is written with a pen of iron, \poemline{2}{and with the point of a diamond.}\poemline{1}{It is engraved on the tablet of their heart,}\poemline{2}{and on the horns of your altars.}}}
\VersePair{17:2}{}{17:2}{{\raggedright Even their children remember their altars \poemline{2}{and their Asherah poles by the green trees on the high hills.}}}
\VersePair{17:3}{}{17:3}{{\raggedright My mountain in the field, \poemline{2}{I will give your substance and all your treasures for a plunder,}\poemline{2}{and your high places, because of sin, throughout all your borders.}}}
\VersePair{17:4}{}{17:4}{{\raggedright You, even of yourself, will discontinue from your heritage that I gave you. \poemline{2}{I will cause you to serve your enemies in the land which you don’t know,}\poemline{2}{for you have kindled a fire in my anger which will burn forever.”}}}
\VersePair{17:5}{Cursed is the man who trusts in man, and will lean his arm of flesh upon him, while his heart departs from the Lord.}{17:5}{{\raggedright Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Cursed is the man who trusts in man,}\poemline{2}{relies on strength of flesh,}\poemline{2}{and whose heart departs from Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{17:6}{And he shall be as the wild tamarisk in the desert: he shall not see when good comes; but he shall dwell in barren places, and in the wilderness, in a salt land which is not inhabited.}{17:6}{{\raggedright For he will be like a bush in the desert, \poemline{2}{and will not see when good comes,}\poemline{1}{but will inhabit the parched places in the wilderness,}\poemline{2}{an uninhabited salt land.}}}
\VersePair{17:7}{But blessed is the man who trusts in the Lord, and whose hope the Lord shall be.}{17:7}{{\raggedright “Blessed is the man who trusts in Yahweh, \poemline{2}{and whose confidence is in Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{17:8}{And he shall be as a thriving tree by the waters, and he shall cast forth his root toward a moist place: he shall not fear when heat comes, and there shall be upon him shady branches: he shall not fear in a year of drought, and he shall not fail to bear fruit.}{17:8}{{\raggedright For he will be as a tree planted by the waters, \poemline{2}{who spreads out its roots by the river,}\poemline{1}{and will not fear when heat comes,}\poemline{2}{but its leaf will be green,}\poemline{1}{and will not be concerned in the year of drought.}\poemline{2}{It won’t cease from yielding fruit.}}}
\VersePair{17:9}{The heart is deep beyond all things, and it is the man, and who can know him?}{17:9}{{\raggedright The heart is deceitful above all things \poemline{2}{and it is exceedingly corrupt.}\poemline{2}{Who can know it?}}}
\VersePair{17:10}{I the Lord try the hearts, and prove the reins, to give to every one according to his ways, and according to the fruits of his devices.}{17:10}{{\raggedright “I, Yahweh, search the mind. \poemline{2}{I try the heart,}\poemline{1}{even to give every man according to his ways,}\poemline{2}{according to the fruit of his doings.”}}}
\VersePair{17:11}{The partridge utters her voice, she gathers eggs which she did not lay; so is a man gaining his wealth unjustly; in the midst of his days his riches shall leave him, and at his latter end he will be a fool.}{17:11}{{\raggedright As the partridge that sits on eggs which she has not laid, \poemline{2}{so is he who gets riches, and not by right.}\poemline{1}{In the middle of his days, they will leave him.}\poemline{2}{At his end, he will be a fool.}}}
\VersePair{17:12}{An exalted throne of glory is our sanctuary.}{17:12}{{\raggedright A glorious throne, set on high from the beginning, \poemline{2}{is the place of our sanctuary.}}}
\VersePair{17:13}{O Lord, the hope of Israel, let all that have left thee be ashamed, let them that have revolted be written on the earth, because they have forsaken the fountain of life, the Lord.}{17:13}{{\raggedright Yahweh, the hope of Israel, \poemline{2}{all who forsake you will be disappointed.}\poemline{1}{Those who depart from me will be written in the earth,}\poemline{2}{because they have forsaken Yahweh,}\poemline{2}{the spring of living waters.}}}
\VersePair{17:14}{Heal me, O Lord, and I shall be healed; save me, and I shall be saved; for thou art my boast.}{17:14}{{\raggedright Heal me, O Yahweh, and I will be healed. \poemline{2}{Save me, and I will be saved;}\poemline{2}{for you are my praise.}}}
\VersePair{17:15}{Behold, they say to me, Where is the word of the Lord? let it come.}{17:15}{{\raggedright Behold, they ask me, \poemline{2}{“Where is Yahweh’s word?}\poemline{2}{Let it be fulfilled now.”}}}
\VersePair{17:16}{But I have not been weary of following thee, nor have I desired the day of man; thou knowest; the words that proceed out of my lips are before thy face.}{17:16}{{\raggedright As for me, I have not hurried from being a shepherd after you. \poemline{2}{I haven’t desired the woeful day. You know.}\poemline{2}{That which came out of my lips was before your face.}}}
\VersePair{17:17}{Be not to me a stranger, but spare me in the evil day.}{17:17}{{\raggedright Don’t be a terror to me. \poemline{2}{You are my refuge in the day of evil.}}}
\VersePair{17:18}{Let them that persecute me be ashamed, but let me not be ashamed: let them be alarmed, but let me not be alarmed: bring upon them the evil day, crush them with double destruction.}{17:18}{{\raggedright Let them be disappointed who persecute me, \poemline{2}{but don’t let me be disappointed.}\poemline{1}{Let them be dismayed,}\poemline{2}{but don’t let me be dismayed.}\poemline{1}{Bring on them the day of evil,}\poemline{2}{and destroy them with double destruction.}}}
\VersePair{17:19}{Thus saith the Lord; Go and stand in the gates of the children of thy people, by which the kings of Juda enter, and by which they go out, and in all the gates of Jerusalem:}{17:19}{Yahweh said this to me: “Go and stand in the gate of the children of the people, through which the kings of Judah come in and by which they go out, and in all the gates of Jerusalem.}
\VersePair{17:20}{and thou shalt say to them, Hear the word of the Lord, ye kings of Juda, and all Judea, and all Jerusalem, all who go in at these gates:}{17:20}{Tell them, ‘Hear Yahweh’s word, you kings of Judah, all Judah, and all the inhabitants of Jerusalem, that enter in by these gates:}
\VersePair{17:21}{thus saith the Lord; Take heed to your souls, and take up no burdens on the sabbath-day, and go not forth through the gates of Jerusalem;}{17:21}{Yahweh says, “Be careful, and bear no burden on the Sabbath day, nor bring it in by the gates of Jerusalem.}
\VersePair{17:22}{and carry forth no burdens out of your houses on the sabbath-day, and ye shall do no work: sanctify the sabbath-day, as I commanded your fathers.}{17:22}{Don’t carry a burden out of your houses on the Sabbath day. Don’t do any work, but make the Sabbath day holy, as I commanded your fathers.}
\VersePair{17:23}{But they hearkened not, and inclined not their ear, but stiffened their neck more than their fathers did, so as not to hear me, and not to receive correction.}{17:23}{But they didn’t listen. They didn’t turn their ear, but made their neck stiff, that they might not hear, and might not receive instruction.}
\VersePair{17:24}{And it shall come to pass, if ye will hearken to me, saith the Lord, to carry in no burdens through the gates of this city on the sabbath-day, and to sanctify the sabbath-day, so as to do no work upon it,}{17:24}{It will happen, if you diligently listen to me,” says Yahweh, “to bring in no burden through the gates of this city on the Sabbath day, but to make the Sabbath day holy, to do no work therein;}
\VersePair{17:25}{that there shall enter through the gates of this city kings and princes sitting on the throne of David, and riding on their chariots and horses, they, and their princes, the men of Juda, and the dwellers in Jerusalem: and this city shall be inhabited for ever.}{17:25}{then there will enter in by the gates of this city kings and princes sitting on David’s throne, riding in chariots and on horses, they and their princes, the men of Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem; and this city will remain forever.}
\VersePair{17:26}{And men shall come out of the cities of Juda, and from round about Jerusalem, and out of the land of Benjamin, and out of the plain country, and from the hill country, and from the south country, bringing whole-burnt-offerings, and sacrifices, and incense, and manna, and frankincense, bringing praise to the house of the Lord.}{17:26}{They will come from the cities of Judah, and from the places around Jerusalem, from the land of Benjamin, from the lowland, from the hill country, and from the South, bringing burnt offerings, sacrifices, meal offerings, and frankincense, and bringing sacrifices of thanksgiving to Yahweh’s house.}
\VersePair{17:27}{But it shall come to pass, if ye will not hearken to me to sanctify the sabbath-day, to bear no burdens, nor go in with them by the gates of Jerusalem on the sabbath-day; then will I kindle a fire in the gates thereof, and it shall devour the streets of Jerusalem, and shall not be quenched.}{17:27}{But if you will not listen to me to make the Sabbath day holy, and not to bear a burden and enter in at the gates of Jerusalem on the Sabbath day, then I will kindle a fire in its gates, and it will devour the palaces of Jerusalem. It will not be quenched.”’”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{18}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{18:1}{The word that came from the Lord to}{18:1}{The word which came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, saying,}
\VersePair{18:2}{Jeremias, saying, Arise, and go down to the potter's house, and there thou shalt hear my words.}{18:2}{“Arise, and go down to the potter’s house, and there I will cause you to hear my words.”}
\VersePair{18:3}{So I went down to the potter's house, and behold, he was making a vessel on the stones.}{18:3}{Then I went down to the potter’s house, and behold, he was making something on the wheels.}
\VersePair{18:4}{And the vessel which he was making with his hands fell: so he made it again another vessel, as it seemed good to him to make it.}{18:4}{When the vessel that he made of the clay was marred in the hand of the potter, he made it again another vessel, as seemed good to the potter to make it.}
\VersePair{18:5}{And the word of the Lord came to me, saying,}{18:5}{Then Yahweh’s word came to me, saying,}
\VersePair{18:6}{Shall I not be able, O house of Israel, to do to you as this potter? behold, as the clay of the potter are ye in my hands.}{18:6}{“House of Israel, can’t I do with you as this potter?” says Yahweh. “Behold, as the clay in the potter’s hand, so are you in my hand, house of Israel.}
\VersePair{18:7}{If I shall pronounce a decree upon a nation, or upon a kingdom, to cut them off, and to destroy them;}{18:7}{At the instant I speak concerning a nation, and concerning a kingdom, to pluck up and to break down and to destroy it,}
\VersePair{18:8}{and that nation turn from all their sins, then will I repent of the evils which I purposed to do to them.}{18:8}{if that nation, concerning which I have spoken, turns from their evil, I will repent of the evil that I thought to do to them.}
\VersePair{18:9}{And if I shall pronounce a decree upon a nation and kingdom, to rebuild and to plant it;}{18:9}{At the instant I speak concerning a nation, and concerning a kingdom, to build and to plant it,}
\VersePair{18:10}{and they do evil before me, so as not to hearken to my voice, then will I repent of the good which I spoke of, to do it to them.}{18:10}{if they do that which is evil in my sight, that they don’t obey my voice, then I will repent of the good with which I said I would benefit them.}
\VersePair{18:11}{And now say to the men of Juda, and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem, Behold, I prepare evils against you, and devise a device against you: let every one turn now from his evil way, and amend your practices.}{18:11}{“Now therefore, speak to the men of Judah, and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem, saying, ‘Yahweh says: “Behold, I frame evil against you, and devise a plan against you. Everyone return from his evil way now, and amend your ways and your doings.”’}
\VersePair{18:12}{And they said, We will quit ourselves like men, for we will pursue our perverse ways, and we will perform each the lusts of his evil heart.}{18:12}{But they say, ‘It is in vain; for we will walk after our own plans, and we will each follow the stubbornness of his evil heart.’”}
\VersePair{18:13}{Therefore thus saith the Lord; Enquire now among the nations, who has heard such very horrible things as the virgin of Israel has done?}{18:13}{{\raggedright Therefore Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Ask now among the nations,}\poemline{2}{‘Who has heard such things?’}\poemline{2}{The virgin of Israel has done a very horrible thing.}}}
\VersePair{18:14}{Will fertilising streams fail to flow from a rock, or snow fail from Libanus? will water violently impelled by the wind turn aside?}{18:14}{{\raggedright Will the snow of Lebanon fail from the rock of the field? \poemline{2}{Will the cold waters that flow down from afar be dried up?}}}
\VersePair{18:15}{For my people have forgotten me, they have offered incense in vain, and they fail in their ways, leaving the ancient tracks, to enter upon impassable paths;}{18:15}{{\raggedright For my people have forgotten me. \poemline{2}{They have burned incense to false gods.}\poemline{1}{They have been made to stumble in their ways}\poemline{2}{in the ancient paths,}\poemline{2}{to walk in byways, in a way not built up,}}}
\VersePair{18:16}{to make their land a desolation, and a perpetual hissing; all that go through it shall be amazed, and shall shake their heads.}{18:16}{{\raggedright to make their land an astonishment, \poemline{2}{and a perpetual hissing.}\poemline{1}{Everyone who passes by it will be astonished,}\poemline{2}{and shake his head.}}}
\VersePair{18:17}{I will scatter them before their enemies like an east wind; I will shew them the day of their destruction.}{18:17}{{\raggedright I will scatter them as with an east wind before the enemy. \poemline{2}{I will show them the back, and not the face,}\poemline{2}{in the day of their calamity.}}}
\VersePair{18:18}{Then they said, Come, and let us devise a device against Jeremias; for the law shall not perish from the priest, nor counsel from the wise, nor the word from the prophet. Come, and let us smite him with the tongue, and we will hear all his words.}{18:18}{Then they said, “Come! Let’s devise plans against Jeremiah; for the law won’t perish from the priest, nor counsel from the wise, nor the word from the prophet. Come, and let’s strike him with the tongue, and let’s not give heed to any of his words.”}
\VersePair{18:19}{Hear me, O Lord, and hear the voice of my pleading.}{18:19}{{\raggedright Give heed to me, Yahweh, \poemline{2}{and listen to the voice of those who contend with me.}}}
