\VersePair{27:40}{As God overthrew Sodom and Gomorrha, and the cities bordering upon them, saith the Lord: no man shall dwell there, and no son of man shall sojourn there.}{50:40}{{\raggedright As when God overthrew Sodom and Gomorrah and its neighbor cities,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“so no man will dwell there,}\poemline{2}{neither will any son of man live therein.}}}
\VersePair{27:41}{Behold, a people comes from the north, and a great nation, and many kings shall be stirred up from the end of the earth; holding bow and dagger:}{50:41}{{\raggedright “Behold, a people comes from the north. \poemline{2}{A great nation and many kings will be stirred up from the uttermost parts of the earth.}}}
\VersePair{27:42}{the people is fierce, and will have no mercy: their voices shall sound as the sea, they shall ride upon horses, prepared for war, like fire, against thee, O daughter of Babylon.}{50:42}{{\raggedright They take up bow and spear. \poemline{2}{They are cruel, and have no mercy.}\poemline{2}{Their voice roars like the sea.}\poemline{1}{They ride on horses,}\poemline{2}{everyone set in array,}\poemline{2}{as a man to the battle,}\poemline{2}{against you, daughter of Babylon.}}}
\VersePair{27:43}{The king of Babylon heard the sound of them, and his hands were enfeebled: anguish overcame him, pangs as of a woman in travail.}{50:43}{{\raggedright The king of Babylon has heard the news of them, \poemline{2}{and his hands become feeble.}\poemline{1}{Anguish has taken hold of him,}\poemline{2}{pains as of a woman in labor.}}}
\VersePair{27:44}{Behold, he shall come up as a lion from Jordan to Gæthan; for I will speedily drive them from her, and I will set all the youths against her: for who is like me? and who will resist me? and who is this shepherd who will stand before me?}{50:44}{{\raggedright Behold, the enemy will come up like a lion \poemline{2}{from the thickets of the Jordan against the strong habitation;}\poemline{2}{for I will suddenly make them run away from it.}\poemline{1}{Whoever is chosen,}\poemline{2}{I will appoint him over it,}\poemline{2}{for who is like me?}\poemline{1}{Who will appoint me a time?}\poemline{2}{Who is the shepherd who can stand before me?”}}}
\VersePair{27:45}{Therefore hear ye the counsel of the Lord, which he has taken against Babylon; and his devices, which he has devised upon the Chaldeans inhabiting it: surely lambs of their flock shall be destroyed: surely pasture shall be cut off from them.}{50:45}{{\raggedright Therefore hear the counsel of Yahweh \poemline{2}{that he has taken against Babylon;}\poemline{1}{and his purposes}\poemline{2}{that he has purposed against the land of the Chaldeans:}\poemline{1}{Surely they will drag them away,}\poemline{2}{even the little ones of the flock.}\poemline{2}{Surely he will make their habitation desolate over them.}}}
\VersePair{27:46}{For at the sound of the taking of Babylon the earth shall quake, and a cry shall be heard among the nations.}{50:46}{{\raggedright The earth trembles at the noise of the taking of Babylon. \poemline{2}{The cry is heard among the nations.}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{28}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{28:1}{Thus saith the Lord; Behold, I stir up against Babylon, and against the Chaldeans dwelling therein, a deadly burning wind.}{51:1}{{\raggedright Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Behold, I will raise up against Babylon,}\poemline{2}{and against those who dwell in Lebkamai, a destroying wind.}}}
\VersePair{28:2}{And I will send forth against Babylon spoilers, and they shall spoil her, and shall ravage her land. Woe to Babylon round about her in the day of her affliction.}{51:2}{{\raggedright I will send to Babylon strangers, who will winnow her. \poemline{2}{They will empty her land;}\poemline{2}{for in the day of trouble they will be against her all around.}}}
\VersePair{28:3}{Let the archer bend his bow, and him that has armour put it on: and spare ye not her young men, but destroy ye all her host.}{51:3}{{\raggedright Against him who bends, let the archer bend his bow, \poemline{2}{also against him who lifts himself up in his coat of mail.}\poemline{1}{Don’t spare her young men!}\poemline{2}{Utterly destroy all her army!}}}
\VersePair{28:4}{And slain men shall fall in the land of the Chaldeans, and men pierced through shall fall without it.}{51:4}{{\raggedright They will fall down slain in the land of the Chaldeans, \poemline{2}{and thrust through in her streets.}}}
\VersePair{28:5}{For Israel and Juda have not been forsaken of their God, of the Lord Almighty; whereas their land was filled with iniquity against the holy things of Israel.}{51:5}{{\raggedright For Israel is not forsaken, nor Judah, by his God, \poemline{2}{by Yahweh of Armies;}\poemline{2}{though their land is full of guilt against the Holy One of Israel.}}}
\VersePair{28:6}{Flee ye out of the midst of Babylon, and deliver every one his soul: and be not overthrown in her iniquity; for it is the time of her retribution from the Lord; he is rendering to her a recompence.}{51:6}{{\raggedright “Flee out of the middle of Babylon! \poemline{2}{Everyone save his own life!}\poemline{1}{Don’t be cut off in her iniquity,}\poemline{2}{for it is the time of Yahweh’s vengeance.}\poemline{2}{He will give to her a recompense.}}}
\VersePair{28:7}{Babylon has been a golden cup in the Lord's hand, causing all the earth to be drunken: the nations have drunk of her wine; therefore they were shaken.}{51:7}{{\raggedright Babylon has been a golden cup in Yahweh’s hand, \poemline{2}{who made all the earth drunk.}\poemline{1}{The nations have drunk of her wine;}\poemline{2}{therefore the nations have gone mad.}}}
\VersePair{28:8}{And Babylon is fallen suddenly, and is broken to pieces: lament for her; take balm for her deadly wound, if by any means she may be healed.}{51:8}{{\raggedright Babylon has suddenly fallen and been destroyed! \poemline{2}{Wail for her!}\poemline{1}{Take balm for her pain.}\poemline{2}{Perhaps she may be healed.}}}
\VersePair{28:9}{We tried to heal Babylon, but she was not healed: let us forsake her, and depart every one to his own country: for her judgment has reached to the heaven, it has mounted up to the stars.}{51:9}{{\raggedright “We would have healed Babylon, \poemline{2}{but she is not healed.}\poemline{1}{Forsake her,}\poemline{2}{and let’s each go into his own country;}\poemline{1}{for her judgment reaches to heaven,}\poemline{2}{and is lifted up even to the skies.}}}
\VersePair{28:10}{The Lord has brought forth his judgment: come, and let us declare in Sion the works of the Lord our God.}{51:10}{{\raggedright ‘Yahweh has produced our righteousness. \poemline{2}{Come, and let’s declare in Zion the work of Yahweh our God.’}}}
\VersePair{28:11}{Prepare the arrows; fill the quivers: the Lord has stirred up the spirit of the king of the Medes: for his wrath is against Babylon, to destroy it utterly; for it is the Lord's vengeance, it is the vengeance of his people.}{51:11}{{\raggedright “Make the arrows sharp! \poemline{2}{Hold the shields firmly!}\poemline{1}{Yahweh has stirred up the spirit of the kings of the Medes,}\poemline{2}{because his purpose is against Babylon, to destroy it;}\poemline{1}{for it is the vengeance of Yahweh,}\poemline{2}{the vengeance of his temple.}}}
\VersePair{28:12}{Lift up a standard on the walls of Babylon, prepare the quivers, rouse the guards, prepare the weapons: for the Lord has taken the work in hand, and will execute what he has spoken against the inhabitants of Babylon,}{51:12}{{\raggedright Set up a standard against the walls of Babylon! \poemline{2}{Make the watch strong!}\poemline{1}{Set the watchmen,}\poemline{2}{and prepare the ambushes;}\poemline{1}{for Yahweh has both purposed and done}\poemline{2}{that which he spoke concerning the inhabitants of Babylon.}}}
\VersePair{28:13}{dwelling on many waters, and amidst the abundance of her treasures; thine end is come verily into thy bowels.}{51:13}{{\raggedright You who dwell on many waters, abundant in treasures, \poemline{2}{your end has come, the measure of your covetousness.}}}
\VersePair{28:14}{For the Lord has sworn by his arm, saying, I will fill thee with men as with locusts; and they that come down shall cry against thee.}{51:14}{{\raggedright Yahweh of Armies has sworn by himself, saying, \poemline{2}{‘Surely I will fill you with men,}\poemline{2}{as with locusts,}\poemline{2}{and they will lift up a shout against you.’}}}
\VersePair{28:15}{The Lord made the earth by his power, preparing the world by his wisdom, by his understanding he stretched out the heaven.}{51:15}{{\raggedright “He has made the earth by his power. \poemline{2}{He has established the world by his wisdom.}\poemline{2}{By his understanding he has stretched out the heavens.}}}
\VersePair{28:16}{At his voice he makes a sound of water in the heaven, and brings up clouds from the extremity of the earth; he makes lightnings for rain, and brings light out of his treasures.}{51:16}{{\raggedright When he utters his voice, \poemline{2}{there is a roar of waters in the heavens,}\poemline{2}{and he causes the vapors to ascend from the ends of the earth.}\poemline{1}{He makes lightning for the rain,}\poemline{2}{and brings the wind out of his treasuries.}}}
\VersePair{28:17}{Every man has completely lost understanding; every goldsmith is confounded because of his graven images: for they have cast false gods, there is no breath in them.}{51:17}{{\raggedright “Every man has become stupid and without knowledge. \poemline{2}{Every goldsmith is disappointed by his image,}\poemline{1}{for his molten images are falsehood,}\poemline{2}{and there is no breath in them.}}}
\VersePair{28:18}{They are vain works, objects of scorn; in the time of their visitation they shall perish.}{51:18}{{\raggedright They are vanity, \poemline{2}{a work of delusion.}\poemline{2}{In the time of their visitation, they will perish.}}}
\VersePair{28:19}{Not such is Jacob's portion; for he that formed all things, he is his inheritance; the Lord is his name.}{51:19}{{\raggedright The portion of Jacob is not like these, \poemline{2}{for he formed all things,}\poemline{2}{including the tribe of his inheritance.}\poemline{2}{Yahweh of Armies is his name.}}}
\VersePair{28:20}{Thou scatterest for me the weapons of war: and I will scatter nations by thee, and will destroy kings by means of thee.}{51:20}{{\raggedright “You are my battle ax and weapons of war. \poemline{2}{With you I will break the nations into pieces.}\poemline{2}{With you I will destroy kingdoms.}}}
\VersePair{28:21}{And by thee I will scatter the horse and his rider; and by thee I will scatter chariots and them that ride in them.}{51:21}{{\raggedright With you I will break in pieces \poemline{2}{the horse and his rider.}}}
\VersePair{28:22}{And by thee I will scatter youth and maid; and by thee I will scatter man and woman.}{51:22}{{\raggedright With you I will break in pieces \poemline{2}{the chariot and him who rides therein.}\poemline{1}{With you I will break in pieces}\poemline{2}{man and woman.}\poemline{1}{With you I will break in pieces}\poemline{2}{the old man and the youth.}\poemline{1}{With you I will break in pieces}\poemline{2}{the young man and the virgin.}}}
\VersePair{28:23}{And by thee I will scatter the shepherd and his flock; and by thee I will scatter the husbandman and his husbandry; and by thee I will scatter leaders and the captains.}{51:23}{{\raggedright With you I will break in pieces \poemline{2}{the shepherd and his flock.}\poemline{1}{With you I will break in pieces}\poemline{2}{the farmer and his yoke.}\poemline{1}{With you I will break in pieces}\poemline{2}{governors and deputies.}}}
\VersePair{28:24}{And I will recompense to Babylon and to all the Chaldeans that dwell there all their mischiefs that they have done to Sion before your eyes, saith the Lord.}{51:24}{“I will give to Babylon and to all the inhabitants of Chaldea all their evil that they have done in Zion in your sight,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{28:25}{Behold, I am against thee, the ruined mountain, that destroys the whole earth; and I will stretch out mine hand upon thee, and will roll thee down upon the rocks, and will make thee as a burnt mountain.}{51:25}{{\raggedright “Behold, I am against you, destroying mountain,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“which destroys all the earth.}\poemline{1}{I will stretch out my hand on you,}\poemline{2}{roll you down from the rocks,}\poemline{2}{and will make you a burned mountain.}}}
\VersePair{28:26}{And they shall not take from thee a stone for a corner, nor a stone for a foundation: for thou shalt be a desolation for ever, saith the Lord.}{51:26}{{\raggedright They won’t take a cornerstone from you, \poemline{2}{nor a stone for foundations;}\poemline{2}{but you will be desolate forever,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{28:27}{Lift up a standard in the land, sound the trumpet among the nations, consecrate the nations against her, raise up kings against her by me, and that for the people of Achanaz; set against her engines of war; bring up against her horses as a multitude of locusts.}{51:27}{{\raggedright “Set up a standard in the land! \poemline{2}{Blow the trumpet among the nations!}\poemline{1}{Prepare the nations against her!}\poemline{2}{Call together against her the kingdoms of Ararat, Minni, and Ashkenaz!}\poemline{1}{Appoint a marshal against her!}\poemline{2}{Cause the horses to come up as the swarming locusts!}}}
\VersePair{28:28}{Bring up nations against her, even the king of the Medes and of the whole earth, his rulers, and all his captains.}{51:28}{{\raggedright Prepare against her the nations, \poemline{2}{the kings of the Medes, its governors, and all its deputies, and all the land of their dominion!}}}
\VersePair{28:29}{The earth has quaked and been troubled, because the purpose of the Lord has risen up against Babylon, to make the land of Babylon a desolation, and uninhabitable.}{51:29}{{\raggedright The land trembles and is in pain; \poemline{2}{for the purposes of Yahweh against Babylon stand,}\poemline{2}{to make the land of Babylon a desolation, without inhabitant.}}}
\VersePair{28:30}{The warrior of Babylon has failed to fight; they shall sit there in the siege; their power is broken; they are become like women; her tabernacles have been set on fire; her bars are broken.}{51:30}{{\raggedright The mighty men of Babylon have stopped fighting, \poemline{2}{they remain in their strongholds.}\poemline{1}{Their might has failed.}\poemline{2}{They have become as women.}\poemline{1}{Her dwelling places are set on fire.}\poemline{2}{Her bars are broken.}}}
\VersePair{28:31}{One shall rush, running to meet another runner, and one shall go with tidings to meet another with tidings, to bring tidings to the king of Babylon, that his city is taken.}{51:31}{{\raggedright One runner will run to meet another, \poemline{2}{and one messenger to meet another,}\poemline{2}{to show the king of Babylon that his city is taken on every quarter.}}}
\VersePair{28:32}{At the end of his passages they were taken, and his cisterns they have burnt with fire, and his warriors are going forth.}{51:32}{{\raggedright So the passages are seized. \poemline{2}{They have burned the reeds with fire.}\poemline{2}{The men of war are frightened.”}}}
\VersePair{28:33}{For thus saith the Lord, The houses of the king of Babylon shall be threshed as a floor in the season; yet a little while, and her harvest shall come.}{51:33}{{\raggedright For Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says: \poemline{1}{“The daughter of Babylon is like a threshing floor at the time when it is trodden.}\poemline{2}{Yet a little while, and the time of harvest comes for her.”}}}
\VersePair{28:34}{He has devoured me, he has torn me asunder, airy darkness has come upon me; Nabuchodonosor king of Babylon has swallowed me up, as a dragon has he filled his belly with my delicacies.}{51:34}{{\raggedright “Nebuchadnezzar the king of Babylon has devoured me. \poemline{2}{He has crushed me.}\poemline{2}{He has made me an empty vessel.}\poemline{1}{He has, like a monster, swallowed me up.}\poemline{2}{He has filled his mouth with my delicacies.}\poemline{2}{He has cast me out.}}}
\VersePair{28:35}{My troubles and my distresses have driven me out into Babylon, shall she that dwells in Sion say; and my blood shall be upon the Chaldeans dwelling there, shall Jerusalem say.}{51:35}{{\raggedright May the violence done to me and to my flesh be on Babylon!” \poemline{2}{the inhabitant of Zion will say; and,}\poemline{1}{“May my blood be on the inhabitants of Chaldea!”}\poemline{2}{will Jerusalem say.}}}
\VersePair{28:36}{Therefore thus saith the Lord, Behold, I will judge thine adversary, and I will execute vengeance for thee; and I will waste her sea, and dry up her fountain.}{51:36}{{\raggedright Therefore Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Behold, I will plead your cause,}\poemline{2}{and take vengeance for you.}\poemline{1}{I will dry up her sea,}\poemline{2}{and make her fountain dry.}}}
\VersePair{28:37}{And Babylon shall be a desolation, and shall not be inhabited.}{51:37}{{\raggedright Babylon will become heaps, \poemline{2}{a dwelling place for jackals,}\poemline{2}{an astonishment, and a hissing,}\poemline{2}{without inhabitant.}}}
\VersePair{28:38}{For they rose up together as lions, and as lions'whelps.}{51:38}{{\raggedright They will roar together like young lions. \poemline{2}{They will growl as lions’cubs.}}}
\VersePair{28:39}{In their heat I will give them a draught, and make them drunk, that they may be stupified, and sleep an everlasting sleep, and not awake, saith the Lord.}{51:39}{{\raggedright When they are inflamed, I will make their feast, \poemline{2}{and I will make them drunk,}\poemline{1}{that they may rejoice,}\poemline{2}{and sleep a perpetual sleep,}\poemline{2}{and not wake up,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{28:40}{And bring thou them down as lambs to the slaughter, and rams with kids.}{51:40}{{\raggedright “I will bring them down like lambs to the slaughter, \poemline{2}{like rams with male goats.}}}
\VersePair{28:41}{How has the boast of all the earth been taken and caught in a snare! how has Babylon become a desolation among the nations!}{51:41}{{\raggedright “How Sheshach is taken! \poemline{2}{How the praise of the whole earth is seized!}\poemline{2}{How Babylon has become a desolation among the nations!}}}
\VersePair{28:42}{The sea has come up upon Babylon with the sound of its waves, and she is covered.}{51:42}{{\raggedright The sea has come up on Babylon. \poemline{2}{She is covered with the multitude of its waves.}}}
\VersePair{28:43}{Her cities are become like a dry and trackless land; not so much as one man shall dwell in it, neither shall a son of man lodge in it.}{51:43}{{\raggedright Her cities have become a desolation, \poemline{2}{a dry land, and a desert,}\poemline{2}{a land in which no man dwells.}\poemline{2}{No son of man passes by it.}}}
\VersePair{28:44}{And I will take vengeance on Babylon, and bring forth out of her mouth what she has swallowed down, and the nations shall no more be gathered to her:}{51:44}{{\raggedright I will execute judgment on Bel in Babylon, \poemline{2}{and I will bring out of his mouth that which he has swallowed up.}\poemline{1}{The nations will not flow any more to him.}\poemline{2}{Yes, the wall of Babylon will fall.}}}
\VersePair{28:45}{}{51:45}{{\raggedright “My people, go away from the middle of her, \poemline{2}{and each of you save yourselves from Yahweh’s fierce anger.}}}
\VersePair{28:46}{}{51:46}{{\raggedright Don’t let your heart faint. \poemline{2}{Don’t fear for the news that will be heard in the land.}\poemline{1}{For news will come one year,}\poemline{2}{and after that in another year news will come,}\poemline{2}{and violence in the land,}\poemline{2}{ruler against ruler.}}}
\VersePair{28:47}{}{51:47}{{\raggedright Therefore behold, the days come that I will execute judgment on the engraved images of Babylon; \poemline{2}{and her whole land will be confounded.}\poemline{2}{All her slain will fall in the middle of her.}}}
\VersePair{28:48}{}{51:48}{{\raggedright Then the heavens and the earth, \poemline{2}{and all that is therein,}\poemline{1}{will sing for joy over Babylon;}\poemline{2}{for the destroyers will come to her from the north,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{28:49}{and in Babylon the slain men of all the earth shall fall.}{51:49}{{\raggedright “As Babylon has caused the slain of Israel to fall, \poemline{2}{so the slain of all the land will fall at Babylon.}}}
\VersePair{28:50}{Go forth of the land, ye that escape, and stay not; ye that are afar off, remember the Lord, and let Jerusalem come into your mind.}{51:50}{{\raggedright You who have escaped the sword, go! \poemline{2}{Don’t stand still!}\poemline{1}{Remember Yahweh from afar,}\poemline{2}{and let Jerusalem come into your mind.”}}}
\VersePair{28:51}{We are ashamed, because we have heard our reproach; disgrace has covered our face; aliens are come into our sanctuary, even into the house of the Lord.}{51:51}{{\raggedright “We are confounded \poemline{2}{because we have heard reproach.}\poemline{1}{Confusion has covered our faces,}\poemline{2}{for strangers have come into the sanctuaries of Yahweh’s house.”}}}
\VersePair{28:52}{Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when I will take vengeance upon her graven images: and slain men shall fall in all her land.}{51:52}{{\raggedright “Therefore behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“that I will execute judgment on her engraved images;}\poemline{2}{and through all her land the wounded will groan.}}}
\VersePair{28:53}{For though Babylon should go up as the heaven, and though she should strengthen her walls with her power, from me shall come they that shall destroy her, saith the Lord.}{51:53}{{\raggedright Though Babylon should mount up to the sky, \poemline{2}{and though she should fortify the height of her strength,}\poemline{2}{yet destroyers will come to her from me,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{28:54}{A sound of a cry in Babylon, and great destruction in the land of the Chaldeans:}{51:54}{{\raggedright “The sound of a cry comes from Babylon, \poemline{2}{and of great destruction from the land of the Chaldeans!}}}
\VersePair{28:55}{for the Lord has utterly destroyed Babylon, and cut off from her the great voice sounding as many waters: he has consigned her voice to destruction.}{51:55}{{\raggedright For Yahweh lays Babylon waste, \poemline{2}{and destroys out of her the great voice!}\poemline{1}{Their waves roar like many waters.}\poemline{2}{The noise of their voice is uttered.}}}
\VersePair{28:56}{For distress has come upon Babylon, her warriors are taken, their bows are useless: for God recompenses them.}{51:56}{{\raggedright For the destroyer has come on her, \poemline{2}{even on Babylon.}\poemline{1}{Her mighty men are taken.}\poemline{2}{Their bows are broken in pieces,}\poemline{1}{for Yahweh is a God of retribution.}\poemline{2}{He will surely repay.}}}
\VersePair{28:57}{The Lord recompenses, and will make her leaders and her wise men and her captains completely drunk, saith the King, the Lord Almighty is his name.}{51:57}{{\raggedright I will make her princes, her wise men, \poemline{2}{her governors, her deputies, and her mighty men drunk.}\poemline{1}{They will sleep a perpetual sleep,}\poemline{2}{and not wake up,”}\poemline{2}{says the King, whose name is Yahweh of Armies.}}}
\VersePair{28:58}{Thus saith the Lord, The wall of Babylon was made broad, but it shall be completely broken down, and her high gates shall be burnt with fire; and the peoples shall not labour in vain, nor the nations fail in their rule.}{51:58}{{\raggedright Yahweh of Armies says: \poemline{1}{“The wide walls of Babylon will be utterly overthrown.}\poemline{2}{Her high gates will be burned with fire.}\poemline{1}{The peoples will labor for vanity,}\poemline{2}{and the nations for the fire;}\poemline{2}{and they will be weary.”}}}
\VersePair{28:59}{The Word which the Lord commanded the Prophet Jeremias to say to Saræas son of Nerias, son of Maasæas, when he went from Sedekias king of Juda to Babylon, in the fourth year of his reign. And Saræas was over the bounties.}{51:59}{The word which Jeremiah the prophet commanded Seraiah the son of Neriah, the son of Mahseiah, when he went with Zedekiah the king of Judah to Babylon in the fourth year of his reign. Now Seraiah was chief quartermaster.}
\VersePair{28:60}{And Jeremias wrote in a book all the evils which should come upon Babylon, even all these words that are written against Babylon.}{51:60}{Jeremiah wrote in a book all the evil that should come on Babylon, even all these words that are written concerning Babylon.}
\VersePair{28:61}{And Jeremias said to Saræas, When thou art come to Babylon, and shalt see and read all these words;}{51:61}{Jeremiah said to Seraiah, “When you come to Babylon, then see that you read all these words,}
\VersePair{28:62}{then thou shalt say, O Lord God, thou hast spoken against this place, to destroy it, and that there should be none to dwell in it, neither man nor beast; for it shall be a desolation for ever.}{51:62}{and say, ‘Yahweh, you have spoken concerning this place, to cut it off, that no one will dwell in it, neither man nor animal, but that it will be desolate forever.’}
\VersePair{28:63}{And it shall come to pass, when thou shalt cease from reading this book, that thou shalt bind a stone upon it, and cast it into the midst of Euphrates;}{51:63}{It will be, when you have finished reading this book, that you shall bind a stone to it, and cast it into the middle of the Euphrates.}
\VersePair{28:64}{and shalt say, Thus shall Babylon sink, and not rise, because of the evils which I bring upon it.}{51:64}{Then you shall say, ‘Thus will Babylon sink, and will not rise again because of the evil that I will bring on her; and they will be weary.’” Thus far are the words of Jeremiah.}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{29}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{29:1}{Thus saith the Lord against the Philistines;}{47:1}{Yahweh’s word that came to Jeremiah the prophet concerning the Philistines, before Pharaoh struck Gaza.}
\VersePair{29:2}{Behold, waters come up from the north, and shall become a sweeping torrent, and it shall sweep away the land, and its fulness; the city, and them that dwell in it: and men shall cry and all that dwell in the land shall howl,}{47:2}{{\raggedright Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Behold, waters rise up out of the north,}\poemline{2}{and will become an overflowing stream,}\poemline{1}{and will overflow the land and all that is therein,}\poemline{2}{the city and those who dwell therein.}\poemline{1}{The men will cry,}\poemline{2}{and all the inhabitants of the land will wail.}}}
\VersePair{29:3}{at the sound of his rushing, at the sound of his hoofs, and at the rattling of his chariots, at the noise of his wheels: the fathers turned not to their children because of the weakness of their hands,}{47:3}{{\raggedright At the noise of the stamping of the hoofs of his strong ones, \poemline{2}{at the rushing of his chariots,}\poemline{2}{at the rumbling of his wheels,}\poemline{1}{the fathers don’t look back for their children}\poemline{2}{because their hands are so feeble,}}}
\VersePair{29:4}{in the day that is coming to destroy all the Philistines: and I will utterly destroy Tyre and Sidon, and all the rest of their allies: for the Lord will destroy the remaining inhabitants of the islands.}{47:4}{{\raggedright because of the day that comes to destroy all the Philistines, \poemline{2}{to cut off from Tyre and Sidon every helper who remains;}\poemline{1}{for Yahweh will destroy the Philistines,}\poemline{2}{the remnant of the isle of Caphtor.}}}
\VersePair{29:5}{Baldness is come upon Gaza; Ascalon is cast away, and the remnant of the Enakim.}{47:5}{{\raggedright Baldness has come on Gaza; \poemline{2}{Ashkelon is brought to nothing.}\poemline{1}{You remnant of their valley,}\poemline{2}{how long will you cut yourself?}}}
\VersePair{29:6}{How long wilt thou smite, O sword of the Lord? how long will it be ere thou art quiet? return into thy sheath, rest, and be removed.}{47:6}{{\raggedright “‘You sword of Yahweh, how long will it be before you are quiet? \poemline{2}{Put yourself back into your scabbard;}\poemline{2}{rest, and be still.’}}}
\VersePair{29:7}{How shall it be quiet, whereas the Lord has given it a commission against Ascalon, and against the regions on the sea-coast, to awake against the remaining countries!}{47:7}{{\raggedright “How can you be quiet, \poemline{2}{since Yahweh has given you a command?}\poemline{1}{Against Ashkelon, and against the seashore,}\poemline{2}{there he has appointed it.”}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{30}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{30:1}{Concerning Idumea, thus saith the Lord; There is no longer wisdom in Thæman, counsel has perished from the wise ones, their wisdom is gone,}{49:7}{{\raggedright Of Edom, Yahweh of Armies says: \poemline{1}{“Is wisdom no more in Teman?}\poemline{2}{Has counsel perished from the prudent?}\poemline{2}{Has their wisdom vanished?}}}
\VersePair{30:2}{their place has been deceived. Dig deep for a dwelling, ye that inhabit Dædam, for he has wrought grievously: I brought trouble upon him in the time at which I visited him.}{49:8}{{\raggedright Flee! Turn back! \poemline{2}{Dwell in the depths, inhabitants of Dedan;}\poemline{2}{for I will bring the calamity of Esau on him when I visit him.}}}
\VersePair{30:3}{For grape-gatherers are come, who shall not leave thee a remnant; as thieves by night, they shall lay their hand upon thy possessions.}{49:9}{{\raggedright If grape gatherers came to you, \poemline{2}{would they not leave some gleaning grapes?}\poemline{1}{If thieves came by night,}\poemline{2}{wouldn’t they steal until they had enough?}}}
\VersePair{30:4}{For I have stripped Esau, I have uncovered their secret places; they shall have no power to hide themselves, they have perished each by the hand of his brother, my neighbour, and it is impossible}{49:10}{{\raggedright But I have made Esau bare, \poemline{2}{I have uncovered his secret places,}\poemline{2}{and he will not be able to hide himself.}\poemline{1}{His offspring is destroyed,}\poemline{2}{with his brothers and his neighbors;}\poemline{2}{and he is no more.}}}
\VersePair{30:5}{for thy fatherless one to be left to live, but I shall live, and the widows trust in me.}{49:11}{{\raggedright Leave your fatherless children. \poemline{2}{I will preserve them alive.}\poemline{2}{Let your widows trust in me.”}}}
\VersePair{30:6}{For thus saith the Lord; They who were not appointed to drink the cup have drunk it; and thou shalt by no means be cleared:}{49:12}{For Yahweh says: “Behold, they to whom it didn’t pertain to drink of the cup will certainly drink; and are you he who will altogether go unpunished? You won’t go unpunished, but you will surely drink.}
\VersePair{30:7}{for by myself I have sworn, saith the Lord, that thou shalt be in the midst of her an impassable land, and a reproach, and a curse; and all her cities shall be desert for ever.}{49:13}{For I have sworn by myself,” says Yahweh, “that Bozrah will become an astonishment, a reproach, a waste, and a curse. All its cities will be perpetual wastes.”}
\VersePair{30:8}{I have heard a report from the Lord, and he has sent messengers to the nations, saying, Assemble yourselves, and come against her; rise ye up to war.}{49:14}{{\raggedright I have heard news from Yahweh, \poemline{2}{and an ambassador is sent among the nations,}\poemline{1}{saying, “Gather yourselves together!}\poemline{2}{Come against her!}\poemline{2}{Rise up to the battle!”}}}
\VersePair{30:9}{I have made thee small among the nations, utterly contemptible among men.}{49:15}{{\raggedright “For, behold, I have made you small among the nations, \poemline{2}{and despised among men.}}}
\VersePair{30:10}{Thine insolence has risen up against thee, the fierceness of thine heart has burst the holes of the rocks, it has seized upon the strength of a lofty hill; for as an eagle he set his nest on high: thence will I bring thee down.}{49:16}{{\raggedright As for your terror, \poemline{2}{the pride of your heart has deceived you,}\poemline{1}{O you who dwell in the clefts of the rock,}\poemline{2}{who hold the height of the hill,}\poemline{1}{though you should make your nest as high as the eagle,}\poemline{2}{I will bring you down from there,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{30:11}{And Idumea shall be a desert: every one that passes by shall hiss at it.}{49:17}{{\raggedright “Edom will become an astonishment. \poemline{2}{Everyone who passes by it will be astonished,}\poemline{2}{and will hiss at all its plagues.}}}
\VersePair{30:12}{As Sodom was overthrown and Gomorrha and they that sojourned in her, saith the Lord Almighty, no man shall dwell there, nor shall any son of man inhabit there.}{49:18}{{\raggedright As in the overthrow of Sodom and Gomorrah and its neighbor cities,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“no man will dwell there,}\poemline{2}{neither will any son of man live therein.}}}
\VersePair{30:13}{Behold, he shall come up as a lion out of the midst of Jordan to the place of Ætham: for I will speedily drive them from it, and do ye set the young men against her: for who is like me? and who will withstand me? and who is this shepherd, who shall confront me?}{49:19}{{\raggedright “Behold, he will come up like a lion from the pride of the Jordan against the strong habitation; \poemline{2}{for I will suddenly make them run away from it,}\poemline{1}{and whoever is chosen,}\poemline{2}{I will appoint him over it.}\poemline{1}{For who is like me?}\poemline{2}{Who will appoint me a time?}\poemline{2}{Who is the shepherd who will stand before me?”}}}
\VersePair{30:14}{Therefore hear ye the counsel of the Lord, which he has framed against Idumea; and his device, which he has devised against the inhabitants of Thæman: surely the least of the sheep shall be swept off; surely their dwelling shall be made desolate for them.}{49:20}{{\raggedright Therefore hear the counsel of Yahweh, that he has taken against Edom, \poemline{2}{and his purposes that he has purposed against the inhabitants of Teman:}\poemline{1}{Surely they will drag them away,}\poemline{2}{the little ones of the flock.}\poemline{2}{Surely he will make their habitation desolate over them.}}}
\VersePair{30:15}{For at the sound of their fall the earth was scared, and the cry of the sea was not heard.}{49:21}{{\raggedright The earth trembles at the noise of their fall; \poemline{2}{there is a cry, the noise which is heard in the Red Sea.}}}
\VersePair{30:16}{Behold, he shall look upon her as an eagle, and spread forth his wings over her strongholds; and the heart of the mighty men of Idumea shall be in that day as the heart of a woman in her pangs.}{49:22}{{\raggedright Behold, he will come up and fly as the eagle, \poemline{2}{and spread out his wings against Bozrah.}\poemline{2}{The heart of the mighty men of Edom at that day will be as the heart of a woman in her pangs.}}}
\VersePair{30:17}{Concerning the sons of Ammon thus saith the Lord, Are there no sons in Israel? or have they no one to succeed them? wherefore has Melchol inherited Galaad, and why shall their people dwell in their cities?}{49:1}{{\raggedright Of the children of Ammon. Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Has Israel no sons?}\poemline{2}{Has he no heir?}\poemline{1}{Why then does Malcam possess Gad,}\poemline{2}{and his people dwell in its cities?}}}
\VersePair{30:18}{Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when I will cause to be heard in Rabbath a tumult of wars; and they shall become a waste and ruined place, and her altars shall be burned with fire; then shall Israel succeed to his dominion.}{49:2}{{\raggedright Therefore behold, the days come,” \poemline{2}{says Yahweh,}\poemline{1}{“that I will cause an alarm of war to be heard against Rabbah of the children of Ammon,}\poemline{2}{and it will become a desolate heap,}\poemline{2}{and her daughters will be burned with fire;}\poemline{1}{then Israel will possess those who possessed him,”}\poemline{2}{says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{30:19}{Howl, O Esebon, for Gai has perished; cry, ye daughters of Rabbath, gird yourselves with sackclothes, and lament; for Melchol shall go into banishment, his priests and his princes together.}{49:3}{{\raggedright “Wail, Heshbon, for Ai is laid waste! \poemline{2}{Cry, you daughters of Rabbah!}\poemline{1}{Clothe yourself in sackcloth.}\poemline{2}{Lament, and run back and forth among the fences;}\poemline{1}{for Malcam will go into captivity,}\poemline{2}{his priests and his princes together.}}}
\VersePair{30:20}{Why do ye exult in the plains of the Enakim, thou haughty daughter, that trustest in thy treasures, that sayest, Who shall come in to me?}{49:4}{{\raggedright Why do you boast in the valleys, \poemline{2}{your flowing valley, backsliding daughter?}\poemline{1}{You trusted in her treasures,}\poemline{2}{saying, ‘Who will come to me?’}}}
\VersePair{30:21}{Behold, I will bring terror upon thee, saith the Lord, from all the country round about thee; and ye shall be scattered every one right before him, and there is none to gather you.}{49:5}{{\raggedright Behold, I will bring a terror on you,” \poemline{2}{says the Lord, Yahweh of Armies,}\poemline{1}{“from all who are around you.}\poemline{2}{All of you will be driven completely out,}\poemline{2}{and there will be no one to gather together the fugitives.}}}
\VersePair{30:22}{}{49:6}{{\raggedright “But afterward I will reverse the captivity of the children of Ammon,” \poemline{2}{says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{30:23}{Concerning Kedar the Queen of the Palace, whom Nabuchodonosor King of Babylon smote, thus saith the Lord; Arise ye, and go up to Kedar, and fill the sons of Kedem.}{49:28}{{\raggedright Of Kedar, and of the kingdoms of Hazor, which Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon struck, Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Arise, go up to Kedar,}\poemline{2}{and destroy the children of the east.}}}
\VersePair{30:24}{They shall take their tents and their sheep, they shall take for themselves their garments, and all their baggage and their camels; and summon ye destruction against them from every side.}{49:29}{{\raggedright They will take their tents and their flocks. \poemline{2}{they will carry away for themselves their curtains,}\poemline{2}{all their vessels, and their camels;}\poemline{2}{and they will cry to them, ‘Terror on every side!’}}}
\VersePair{30:25}{Flee ye, dig very deep for a dwelling-place, ye that dwell in the palace; for the king of Babylon has framed a counsel, and devised a device against you.}{49:30}{{\raggedright Flee! \poemline{2}{Wander far off!}\poemline{1}{Dwell in the depths, you inhabitants of Hazor,” says Yahweh;}\poemline{2}{“for Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon has taken counsel against you,}\poemline{2}{and has conceived a purpose against you.}}}
\VersePair{30:26}{Rise up, and go up against a nation settled and dwelling at ease, who have no doors, nor bolts, nor bars, who dwell alone.}{49:31}{{\raggedright Arise! Go up to a nation that is at ease, \poemline{2}{that dwells without care,” says Yahweh;}\poemline{2}{“that has neither gates nor bars,}\poemline{2}{that dwells alone.}}}
\VersePair{30:27}{And their camels shall be a spoil, and the multitude of their cattle shall be destroyed: and I will scatter them as chaff with every wind, having their hair cut about their foreheads, I will bring on their overthrow from all sides, saith the Lord.}{49:32}{{\raggedright Their camels will be a booty, \poemline{2}{and the multitude of their livestock a plunder.}\poemline{1}{I will scatter to all winds those who have the corners of their beards cut off;}\poemline{2}{and I will bring their calamity from every side of them,”}\poemline{2}{says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{30:28}{And the palace shall be a resting-place for ostriches, and desolate for ever: no man shall abide there, and no son of man shall dwell there.}{49:33}{{\raggedright Hazor will be a dwelling place of jackals, \poemline{2}{a desolation forever.}\poemline{1}{No man will dwell there,}\poemline{2}{neither will any son of man live therein.”}}}
\VersePair{30:29}{Concerning Damascus. Emath is brought to shame, and Arphath: for they have heard an evil report: they are amazed, they are angry, they shall be utterly unable to rest.}{49:23}{{\raggedright Of Damascus: \poemline{1}{“Hamath and Arpad are confounded,}\poemline{2}{for they have heard evil news.}\poemline{2}{They have melted away.}\poemline{1}{There is sorrow on the sea.}\poemline{2}{It can’t be quiet.}}}
\VersePair{30:30}{Damascus is utterly weakened, she is put to flight; trembling has seized upon her.}{49:24}{{\raggedright Damascus has grown feeble, \poemline{2}{she turns herself to flee,}\poemline{2}{and trembling has seized her.}\poemline{1}{Anguish and sorrows have taken hold of her,}\poemline{2}{as of a woman in travail.}}}
\VersePair{30:31}{How has she not left my city, they have loved the village?}{49:25}{{\raggedright How is the city of praise not forsaken, \poemline{2}{the city of my joy?}}}
\VersePair{30:32}{Therefore shall the young men fall in thy streets, and all thy warriors shall fall, saith the Lord.}{49:26}{{\raggedright Therefore her young men will fall in her streets, \poemline{2}{and all the men of war will be brought to silence in that day,”}\poemline{2}{says Yahweh of Armies.}}}
\VersePair{30:33}{And I will kindle a fire in the wall of Damascus, and it shall devour the streets of the son of Ader.}{49:27}{{\raggedright “I will kindle a fire in the wall of Damascus, \poemline{2}{and it will devour the palaces of Ben Hadad.”}}}
\end{paracol}

\VersePair{31:1}{Thus has the Lord said concerning Moab, Woe to Nabau! for it has perished: Cariathaim is taken: Amath and Agath are put to shame.}{48:1}{{\raggedright Of Moab. Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says: \poemline{1}{“Woe to Nebo!}\poemline{2}{For it is laid waste.}\poemline{1}{Kiriathaim is disappointed.}\poemline{2}{It is taken.}\poemline{1}{Misgab is put to shame}\poemline{2}{and broken down. \footnote{48:1: or, The stronghold}}}}
\VersePair{31:2}{There is no longer any healing for Moab, nor glorying in Esebon: he has devised evils against her: we have cut her off from being a nation, and she shall be completely still: after thee shall go a sword;}{48:2}{{\raggedright The praise of Moab is no more. \poemline{2}{In Heshbon they have devised evil against her:}\poemline{2}{‘Come! Let’s cut her off from being a nation.’}\poemline{1}{You also, Madmen, will be brought to silence.}\poemline{2}{The sword will pursue you.}}}
\VersePair{31:3}{for there is a voice of men crying out of Oronaim, destruction and great ruin.}{48:3}{{\raggedright The sound of a cry from Horonaim, \poemline{2}{desolation and great destruction!}}}
\VersePair{31:4}{Moab is ruined, proclaim it to Zogora:}{48:4}{{\raggedright Moab is destroyed. \poemline{2}{Her little ones have caused a cry to be heard.}}}
\VersePair{31:5}{for Aloth is filled with weeping: one shall go up weeping by the way of Oronaim; ye have heard a cry of destruction.}{48:5}{{\raggedright For they will go up by the ascent of Luhith with continual weeping. \poemline{2}{For at the descent of Horonaim they have heard the distress of the cry of destruction.}}}
\VersePair{31:6}{Flee ye, and save your lives, and ye shall be as a wild ass in the desert.}{48:6}{{\raggedright Flee! Save your lives! \poemline{2}{Be like the juniper bush in the wilderness.}}}
\VersePair{31:7}{Since thou hast trusted in thy strong-hold, therefore thou shalt be taken: and Chamos shall go forth into captivity, and his priests, and his princes together.}{48:7}{{\raggedright For, because you have trusted in your works and in your treasures, \poemline{2}{you also will be taken.}\poemline{1}{Chemosh will go out into captivity,}\poemline{2}{his priests and his princes together.}}}
\VersePair{31:8}{And destruction shall come upon every city, it shall by no means escape; the valley also shall perish, and the plain country shall be completely destroyed, as the Lord has said.}{48:8}{{\raggedright The destroyer will come on every city, \poemline{2}{and no city will escape;}\poemline{1}{the valley also will perish,}\poemline{2}{and the plain will be destroyed, as Yahweh has spoken.}}}
\VersePair{31:9}{Set marks upon Moab, for she shall be touched with a plague-spot, and all her cities shall become desolate; whence shall there be an inhabitant for her?}{48:9}{{\raggedright Give wings to Moab, \poemline{2}{that she may fly and get herself away:}\poemline{1}{and her cities will become a desolation,}\poemline{2}{without anyone to dwell in them.}}}
\VersePair{31:10}{Cursed is the man that does the works of the Lord carelessly, keeping back his sword from blood.}{48:10}{{\raggedright “Cursed is he who does the work of Yahweh negligently; \poemline{2}{and cursed is he who keeps back his sword from blood.}}}
\VersePair{31:11}{Moab has been at ease from a child, and trusted in his glory; he has not poured out his liquor from vessel to vessel, and has not gone into banishment, therefore his taste remained in him, and his smell departed not.}{48:11}{{\raggedright “Moab has been at ease from his youth, \poemline{2}{and he has settled on his dregs,}\poemline{1}{and has not been emptied from vessel to vessel,}\poemline{2}{neither has he gone into captivity;}\poemline{1}{therefore his taste remains in him,}\poemline{2}{and his scent is not changed.}}}
\VersePair{31:12}{Therefore, behold, his days come, saith the Lord, when I shall send upon him bad leaders, and they shall lead him astray, and they shall utterly break in pieces his possessions, and shall cut his horns asunder.}{48:12}{{\raggedright Therefore behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“that I will send to him those who pour off,}\poemline{1}{and they will pour him off;}\poemline{2}{and they will empty his vessels,}\poemline{2}{and break their containers in pieces.}}}
\VersePair{31:13}{And Moab shall be ashamed of Chamos, as the house of Israel was ashamed of Bæthel their hope, having trusted in them.}{48:13}{{\raggedright Moab will be ashamed of Chemosh, \poemline{2}{as the house of Israel was ashamed of Bethel, their confidence.}}}
\VersePair{31:14}{How will ye say, We are strong, and men strong for war?}{48:14}{{\raggedright “How do you say, ‘We are mighty men, \poemline{2}{and valiant men for the war ’?}}}
\VersePair{31:15}{Moab is ruined, even his city, and his choice young men have gone down to slaughter.}{48:15}{{\raggedright Moab is laid waste, \poemline{2}{and they have gone up into his cities,}\poemline{2}{and his chosen young men have gone down to the slaughter,”}\poemline{2}{says the King, whose name is Yahweh of Armies.}}}
\VersePair{31:16}{The day of Moab is near at hand, and his iniquity moves swiftly to vengeance.}{48:16}{{\raggedright “The calamity of Moab is near to come, \poemline{2}{and his affliction hurries fast.}}}
\VersePair{31:17}{Shake the head at him, all ye that are round about him; all of you utter his name; say ye, How is the glorious staff broken to pieces, the rod of magnificence!}{48:17}{{\raggedright All you who are around him, bemoan him; \poemline{2}{and all you who know his name, say,}\poemline{1}{‘How the strong staff is broken,}\poemline{2}{the beautiful rod!’}}}
\VersePair{31:18}{Come down from thy glory, and sit down in a damp place: Dæbon shall be broken, because Moab is destroyed: there has gone up against thee one to ravage thy strong-hold.}{48:18}{{\raggedright “You daughter who dwells in Dibon, \poemline{2}{come down from your glory,}\poemline{2}{and sit in thirst;}\poemline{1}{for the destroyer of Moab has come up against you.}\poemline{2}{He has destroyed your strongholds.}}}
\VersePair{31:19}{Stand by the way, and look, thou that dwellest in Arer; and ask him that is fleeing, and him that escapes, and say, What has happened?}{48:19}{{\raggedright Inhabitant of Aroer, stand by the way and watch. \poemline{2}{Ask him who flees, and her who escapes;}\poemline{2}{say, ‘What has been done?’}}}
\VersePair{31:20}{Moab is put to shame, because he is broken: howl and cry; proclaim in Arnon, that Moab has perished.}{48:20}{{\raggedright Moab is disappointed; \poemline{2}{for it is broken down.}\poemline{1}{Wail and cry!}\poemline{2}{Tell it by the Arnon, that Moab is laid waste.}}}

\VersePair{31:25}{The horn of Moab is broken, and his arm is crushed.}{48:25}{{\raggedright The horn of Moab is cut off, \poemline{2}{and his arm is broken,” says Yahweh.}}}

\VersePair{31:29}{And I have heard of the pride of Moab, he has greatly heightened his pride and his haughtiness, and his heart has been lifted up.}{48:29}{{\raggedright “We have heard of the pride of Moab. \poemline{2}{He is very proud in his loftiness, his pride,}\poemline{2}{his arrogance, and the arrogance of his heart.}}}
\VersePair{31:30}{But I know his works: is it not enough for him? has he not done thus?}{48:30}{{\raggedright I know his wrath,” says Yahweh, “that it is nothing; \poemline{2}{his boastings have done nothing.}}}
\VersePair{31:31}{Therefore howl ye for Moab on all sides; cry out against the shorn men in a gloomy place. I will weep for thee,}{48:31}{{\raggedright Therefore I will wail for Moab. \poemline{2}{Yes, I will cry out for all Moab.}\poemline{2}{They will mourn for the men of Kir Heres.}}}
\VersePair{31:32}{O vine of Aserema, as with the weeping of Jazer: thy branches are gone over the sea, they reached the cities of Jazer: destruction has come upon thy fruits, and upon thy grape-gatherers.}{48:32}{{\raggedright With more than the weeping of Jazer \poemline{2}{I will weep for you, vine of Sibmah.}\poemline{1}{Your branches passed over the sea.}\poemline{2}{They reached even to the sea of Jazer.}\poemline{1}{The destroyer has fallen on your summer fruits}\poemline{2}{and on your vintage.}}}
\VersePair{31:33}{Joy and gladness have been utterly swept off the land of Moab: and though there was wine in thy presses, in the morning they trod it not, neither in the evening did they raise the cry of joy.}{48:33}{{\raggedright Gladness and joy is taken away from the fruitful field \poemline{2}{and from the land of Moab.}\poemline{1}{I have caused wine to cease from the wine presses.}\poemline{2}{No one will tread with shouting.}\poemline{2}{The shouting will be no shouting.}}}
\VersePair{31:34}{From the cry of Esebon even to Ætam their cities uttered their voice, from Zogor to Oronaim, and their tidings as a heifer of three years old, for the water also of Nebrin shall be dried up.}{48:34}{{\raggedright From the cry of Heshbon even to Elealeh, \poemline{2}{even to Jahaz they have uttered their voice,}\poemline{2}{from Zoar even to Horonaim, to Eglath Shelishiyah;}\poemline{2}{for the waters of Nimrim will also become desolate.}}}
\VersePair{31:35}{And I will destroy Moab, saith the Lord, as he comes up to the altar, and burns incense to his gods.}{48:35}{{\raggedright Moreover I will cause to cease in Moab,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“him who offers in the high place,}\poemline{2}{and him who burns incense to his gods.}}}
\VersePair{31:36}{Therefore the heart of Moab shall sound as pipes, my heart shall sound as a pipe for the shorn men; forasmuch as what every man has gained has perished from him.}{48:36}{{\raggedright Therefore my heart sounds for Moab like flutes, \poemline{2}{and my heart sounds like flutes for the men of Kir Heres.}\poemline{2}{Therefore the abundance that he has gotten has perished.}}}
\VersePair{31:37}{They shall all have their heads shaved in every place, and every beard shall be shaved; and all hands shall beat the breasts, and on all loins shall be sackcloth.}{48:37}{{\raggedright For every head is bald, \poemline{2}{and every beard clipped.}\poemline{1}{There are cuttings on all the hands,}\poemline{2}{and sackcloth on the waist.}}}
\VersePair{31:38}{And on all the housetops of Moab, and in his streets shall be mourning: for I have broken him, saith the Lord, as a vessel, which is useless.}{48:38}{{\raggedright On all the housetops of Moab, \poemline{2}{and in its streets, there is lamentation everywhere;}\poemline{2}{for I have broken Moab like a vessel in which no one delights,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{31:39}{How has he changed! how has Moab turned his back! Moab is put to shame, and become a laughing-stock, and an object of anger to all that are round about him.}{48:39}{{\raggedright “How it is broken down! \poemline{2}{How they wail!}\poemline{1}{How Moab has turned the back with shame!}\poemline{2}{So will Moab become a derision}\poemline{2}{and a terror to all who are around him.”}}}
\VersePair{31:40}{For thus said the Lord;}{48:40}{{\raggedright For Yahweh says: “Behold, he will fly as an eagle, \poemline{2}{and will spread out his wings against Moab.}}}
\VersePair{31:41}{Carioth is taken, and the strong-holds have been taken together.}{48:41}{{\raggedright Kerioth is taken, \poemline{2}{and the strongholds are seized.}\poemline{1}{The heart of the mighty men of Moab at that day}\poemline{2}{will be as the heart of a woman in her pangs.}}}
\VersePair{31:42}{And Moab shall perish from being a multitude, because he has magnified himself against the Lord.}{48:42}{{\raggedright Moab will be destroyed from being a people, \poemline{2}{because he has magnified himself against Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{31:43}{A snare, and fear, and the pit, are upon thee, O inhabitant of Moab.}{48:43}{{\raggedright Terror, the pit, and the snare are on you, \poemline{2}{inhabitant of Moab,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{31:44}{He that flees from the terror shall fall into the pit, and he that comes up out of the pit shall even be taken in the snare: for I will bring these things upon Moab in the year of their visitation.}{48:44}{{\raggedright “He who flees from the terror will fall into the pit; \poemline{2}{and he who gets up out of the pit will be taken in the snare,}\poemline{1}{for I will bring on him, even on Moab,}\poemline{2}{the year of their visitation,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{31:45}{}{48:45}{{\raggedright “Those who fled stand without strength under the shadow of Heshbon; \poemline{2}{for a fire has gone out of Heshbon,}\poemline{2}{and a flame from the middle of Sihon,}\poemline{1}{and has devoured the corner of Moab,}\poemline{2}{and the crown of the head of the tumultuous ones.}}}
\VersePair{31:46}{}{48:46}{{\raggedright Woe to you, O Moab! \poemline{2}{The people of Chemosh are undone;}\poemline{1}{for your sons are taken away captive,}\poemline{2}{and your daughters into captivity.}}}

\ChapterHeading{32}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{32:15}{Thus said the Lord God of Israel; Take the cup of this unmixed wine from mine hand, and thou shalt cause all the nations to drink, to whom I send thee.}{25:15}{For Yahweh, the God of Israel, says to me: “Take this cup of the wine of wrath from my hand, and cause all the nations to whom I send you to drink it.}
\VersePair{32:16}{And they shall drink, and vomit, and be mad, because of the sword which I send among them.}{25:16}{They will drink, and reel back and forth, and be insane, because of the sword that I will send among them.”}
\VersePair{32:17}{So I took the cup out of the Lord's hand, and caused the nations to whom the Lord sent me to drink:}{25:17}{Then I took the cup at Yahweh’s hand, and made all the nations to drink, to whom Yahweh had sent me:}
\VersePair{32:18}{Jerusalem, and the cities of Juda, and the kings of Juda, and his princes, to make them a desert place, a desolation, and a hissing;}{25:18}{Jerusalem, and the cities of Judah, with its kings and its princes, to make them a desolation, an astonishment, a hissing, and a curse, as it is today;}
\VersePair{32:19}{and Pharao king of Egypt, and his servants, and his nobles, and all his people;}{25:19}{Pharaoh king of Egypt, with his servants, his princes, and all his people;}
\VersePair{32:20}{and all the mingled people, and all the kings of the Philistines, and Ascalon, and Gaza, and Accaron, and the remnant of Azotus,}{25:20}{and all the mixed people, and all the kings of the land of Uz, all the kings of the Philistines, Ashkelon, Gaza, Ekron, and the remnant of Ashdod;}
\VersePair{32:21}{and Idumea, and the land of Moab, and the children of Ammon,}{25:21}{Edom, Moab, and the children of Ammon;}
\VersePair{32:22}{and the kings of Tyre, and the kings of Sidon, and the kings in the country beyond the sea,}{25:22}{and all the kings of Tyre, all the kings of Sidon, and the kings of the isle which is beyond the sea;}
\VersePair{32:23}{and Dædan, and Thæman, and Ros, and every one that is shaved round about the face,}{25:23}{Dedan, Tema, Buz, and all who have the corners of their beard cut off;}
\VersePair{32:24}{and all the mingled people lodging in the wilderness,}{25:24}{and all the kings of Arabia, all the kings of the mixed people who dwell in the wilderness;}
\VersePair{32:25}{and all the kings of Ælam, and all the kings of the Persians,}{25:25}{and all the kings of Zimri, all the kings of Elam, and all the kings of the Medes;}
\VersePair{32:26}{and all the kings from the north, the far and the near, each one with his brother, and all the kingdoms which are on the face of the earth.}{25:26}{and all the kings of the north, far and near, one with another; and all the kingdoms of the world, which are on the surface of the earth. The king of Sheshach will drink after them.}
\VersePair{32:27}{And thou shalt say to them, Thus said the Lord Almighty; Drink ye, be ye drunken; and ye shall vomit, and shall fall, and shall in nowise rise, because of the sword which I send among you.}{25:27}{“You shall tell them, ‘Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says: “Drink, and be drunk, vomit, fall, and rise no more, because of the sword which I will send among you.”’}
\VersePair{32:28}{And it shall come to pass, when they refuse to take the cup out of thine hand, to drink it, that thou shalt say, Thus said the Lord; Ye shall surely drink.}{25:28}{It shall be, if they refuse to take the cup at your hand to drink, then you shall tell them, ‘Yahweh of Armies says: “You shall surely drink.}
\VersePair{32:29}{For I am beginning to afflict the city whereon my name is called, and ye shall by no means be held guiltless: for I am calling a sword upon all that dwell upon the earth.}{25:29}{For, behold, I begin to work evil at the city which is called by my name; and should you be utterly unpunished? You will not be unpunished; for I will call for a sword on all the inhabitants of the earth, says Yahweh of Armies.”’}
\VersePair{32:30}{And thou shalt prophesy against them these words, and shalt say, The Lord shall speak from on high, from his sanctuary he will utter his voice; he will pronounce a declaration on his place; and these shall answer like men gathering grapes: and destruction is coming on them that dwell on the earth,}{25:30}{{\raggedright “Therefore prophesy against them all these words, and tell them, \poemline{1}{“‘Yahweh will roar from on high,}\poemline{2}{and utter his voice from his holy habitation.}\poemline{2}{He will mightily roar against his fold.}\poemline{1}{He will give a shout, as those who tread grapes,}\poemline{2}{against all the inhabitants of the earth.}}}
\VersePair{32:31}{even upon the extreme part of the earth; for the Lord has a controversy with the nations, he is pleading with all flesh, and the ungodly are given to the sword, saith the Lord.}{25:31}{{\raggedright A noise will come even to the end of the earth; \poemline{2}{for Yahweh has a controversy with the nations.}\poemline{1}{He will enter into judgment with all flesh.}\poemline{2}{As for the wicked, he will give them to the sword,”’ says Yahweh.”}}}
\VersePair{32:32}{Thus said the Lord; Behold, evils are proceeding from nation to nation, and a great whirlwind goes forth from the end of the earth.}{25:32}{{\raggedright Yahweh of Armies says, \poemline{1}{“Behold, evil will go out from nation to nation,}\poemline{2}{and a great storm will be raised up from the uttermost parts of the earth.”}}}
\VersePair{32:33}{And the slain of the Lord shall be in the day of the Lord from one end of the earth even to the other end of the earth: they shall not be buried; they shall be as dung on the face of the earth.}{25:33}{The slain of Yahweh will be at that day from one end of the earth even to the other end of the earth. They won’t be lamented. They won’t be gathered or buried. They will be dung on the surface of the ground.}
\VersePair{32:34}{Howl, ye shepherds, and cry; and lament, ye rams of the flock: for your days have been completed for slaughter, and ye shall fall as the choice rams.}{25:34}{{\raggedright Wail, you shepherds, and cry. \poemline{2}{Wallow in dust, you leader of the flock;}\poemline{1}{for the days of your slaughter and of your dispersions have fully come,}\poemline{2}{and you will fall like fine pottery.}}}
\VersePair{32:35}{And flight shall perish from the shepherds, and safety from the rams of the flock.}{25:35}{{\raggedright The shepherds will have no way to flee. \poemline{2}{The leader of the flock will have no escape.}}}
\VersePair{32:36}{A voice of the crying of the shepherds, and a moaning of the sheep and the rams: for the Lord has destroyed their pastures.}{25:36}{{\raggedright A voice of the cry of the shepherds, \poemline{2}{and the wailing of the leader of the flock,}\poemline{2}{for Yahweh destroys their pasture.}}}
\VersePair{32:37}{And the peaceable abodes that remain shall be destroyed before the fierceness of my anger.}{25:37}{{\raggedright The peaceful folds are brought to silence \poemline{2}{because of the fierce anger of Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{32:38}{He has forsaken his lair, as a lion: for their land is become desolate before the great sword.}{25:38}{{\raggedright He has left his covert, as the lion; \poemline{2}{for their land has become an astonishment because of the fierceness of the oppression,}\poemline{2}{and because of his fierce anger.}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{33}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{33:1}{In the beginning of the Reign of King Joakim Son of Josias there came this Word from the Lord.}{26:1}{In the beginning of the reign of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, king of Judah, this word came from Yahweh:}
\VersePair{33:2}{Thus said the Lord; Stand in the court of the Lord's house, and thou shalt declare to all the Jews, and to all that come to worship in the house of the Lord, all the words which I commanded thee to speak to them; abate not one word.}{26:2}{“Yahweh says: ‘Stand in the court of Yahweh’s house, and speak to all the cities of Judah which come to worship in Yahweh’s house, all the words that I command you to speak to them. Don’t omit a word.}
\VersePair{33:3}{Peradventure they will hear, and turn every one from his evil way: then I will cease from the evils which I purpose to do to them, because of their evil practices.}{26:3}{It may be they will listen, and every man turn from his evil way, that I may relent from the evil which I intend to do to them because of the evil of their doings.’”}
\VersePair{33:4}{And thou shalt say, Thus said the Lord; If ye will not hearken to me, to walk in my statutes which I set before you,}{26:4}{You shall tell them, “Yahweh says: ‘If you will not listen to me, to walk in my law which I have set before you,}
\VersePair{33:5}{to hearken to the words of my servants the prophets, whom I send to you early in the morning; yea, I sent them, but ye hearkened not to me;}{26:5}{to listen to the words of my servants the prophets whom I send to you, even rising up early and sending them — but you have not listened —}
\VersePair{33:6}{then will I make this house as Selo, and I will make this city a curse to all the nations of all the earth.}{26:6}{then I will make this house like Shiloh, and will make this city a curse to all the nations of the earth.’”}
\VersePair{33:7}{And the priests, and the false prophets, and all the people heard Jeremias speaking these words in the house of the Lord.}{26:7}{The priests and the prophets and all the people heard Jeremiah speaking these words in Yahweh’s house.}
\VersePair{33:8}{And it came to pass, when Jeremias had ceased speaking all that the Lord had ordered him to speak to all the people, that the priests and the false prophets and all the people took him, saying,}{26:8}{When Jeremiah had finished speaking all that Yahweh had commanded him to speak to all the people, the priests and the prophets and all the people seized him, saying, “You shall surely die!}
\VersePair{33:9}{Thou shalt surely die, because thou hast prophesied in the name of the Lord, saying, This house shall be as Selo, and this city shall be made quite destitute of inhabitants. And all the people assembled against Jeremias in the house of the Lord.}{26:9}{Why have you prophesied in Yahweh’s name, saying, ‘This house will be like Shiloh, and this city will be desolate, without inhabitant ’?” All the people were crowded around Jeremiah in Yahweh’s house.}
\VersePair{33:10}{And the princes of Juda heard this word, and they went up out of the house of the king to the house of the Lord, and sat in the entrance of the new gate.}{26:10}{When the princes of Judah heard these things, they came up from the king’s house to Yahweh’s house; and they sat in the entry of the new gate of Yahweh’s house.}
\VersePair{33:11}{Then the priests and the false prophets said to the princes and to all the people, The judgment of death is due to this man; because he has prophesied against this city, as ye have heard with your ears.}{26:11}{Then the priests and the prophets spoke to the princes and to all the people, saying, “This man is worthy of death, for he has prophesied against this city, as you have heard with your ears.”}
\VersePair{33:12}{Then Jeremias spoke to the princes, and to all the people, saying, The Lord sent me to prophesy against this house and against this city, all the words which ye have heard.}{26:12}{Then Jeremiah spoke to all the princes and to all the people, saying, “Yahweh sent me to prophesy against this house and against this city all the words that you have heard.}
\VersePair{33:13}{And now amend your ways and your works, and hearken to the voice of the Lord; and the Lord shall cease from the evils which he has pronounced against you.}{26:13}{Now therefore amend your ways and your doings, and obey Yahweh your God’s voice; then Yahweh will relent from the evil that he has pronounced against you.}
\VersePair{33:14}{And behold, I am in your hands; do to me as is expedient, and as it is best for you.}{26:14}{But as for me, behold, I am in your hand. Do with me what is good and right in your eyes.}
\VersePair{33:15}{But know for a certainty, that if ye slay me, ye bring innocent blood upon yourselves, and upon this city, and upon them that dwell in it; for in truth the Lord has sent me to you to speak in your ears all these words.}{26:15}{Only know for certain that if you put me to death, you will bring innocent blood on yourselves, on this city, and on its inhabitants; for in truth Yahweh has sent me to you to speak all these words in your ears.”}
\VersePair{33:16}{Then the princes and all the people said to the priests and to the false prophets; Judgment of death is not due to this man; for he has spoken to us in the name of the Lord our God.}{26:16}{Then the princes and all the people said to the priests and to the prophets: “This man is not worthy of death; for he has spoken to us in the name of Yahweh our God.”}
\VersePair{33:17}{And there rose up men of the elders of the land, and said to all the assembly of the people,}{26:17}{Then certain of the elders of the land rose up, and spoke to all the assembly of the people, saying,}
\VersePair{33:18}{Michæas the Morathite lived in the days of Ezekias king of Juda, and said to all the people of Juda, Thus saith the Lord; Sion shall be ploughed as a field, and Jerusalem shall become a desolation, and the mountain of the house shall be a thicket of trees.}{26:18}{{\raggedright “Micah the Morashtite prophesied in the days of Hezekiah king of Judah; and he spoke to all the people of Judah, saying, ‘Yahweh of Armies says: \poemline{1}{“‘Zion will be plowed as a field,}\poemline{2}{and Jerusalem will become heaps,}\poemline{2}{and the mountain of the house as the high places of a forest.’}}}
\VersePair{33:19}{Did Ezekias and all Juda in any way slay him? Was it not that they feared the Lord, and they made supplication before the Lord, and the Lord ceased from the evils which he had pronounced against them? whereas we have wrought great evil against our own souls.}{26:19}{Did Hezekiah king of Judah and all Judah put him to death? Didn’t he fear Yahweh, and entreat the favor of Yahweh, and Yahweh relented of the disaster which he had pronounced against them? We would commit great evil against our own souls that way!”}
\VersePair{33:20}{And there was another man prophesying in the name of the Lord, Urias the son of Samæas of Cariathiarim; and he prophesied concerning this land according to all the words of Jeremias.}{26:20}{There was also a man who prophesied in Yahweh’s name, Uriah the son of Shemaiah of Kiriath Jearim; and he prophesied against this city and against this land according to all the words of Jeremiah.}
\VersePair{33:21}{And king Joakim and all the princes heard all his words, and sought to slay him; and Urias heard it and went into Egypt.}{26:21}{When Jehoiakim the king, with all his mighty men and all the princes heard his words, the king sought to put him to death; but when Uriah heard it, he was afraid, and fled, and went into Egypt.}
\VersePair{33:22}{And the king sent men into Egypt;}{26:22}{Then Jehoiakim the king sent Elnathan the son of Achbor and certain men with him into Egypt.}
\VersePair{33:23}{and they brought him thence, and brought him in to the king; and he smote him with the sword, and cast him into the sepulchre of the children of his people.}{26:23}{They fetched Uriah out of Egypt and brought him to Jehoiakim the king, who killed him with the sword and cast his dead body into the graves of the common people.}
\VersePair{33:24}{Nevertheless the hand of Achicam son of Saphan was with Jeremias, to prevent his being delivered into the hands of the people, or being killed.}{26:24}{But the hand of Ahikam the son of Shaphan was with Jeremiah, so that they didn’t give him into the hand of the people to put him to death.}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{34}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{34:1}{}{27:1}{In the beginning of the reign of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, king of Judah, this word came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, saying,}
\VersePair{34:2}{Thus said the Lord; Make to thyself bonds and yokes, and put them about thy neck,}{27:2}{Yahweh says to me: “Make bonds and bars, and put them on your neck.}
\VersePair{34:3}{and thou shalt send them to the king of Idumea, and to the king of Moab, and to the king of the children of Ammon, and to the king of Tyre, and to the king of Sidon, by the hands of their messengers that come to meet them at Jerusalem to Sedekias king of Juda.}{27:3}{Then send them to the king of Edom, to the king of Moab, to the king of the children of Ammon, to the king of Tyre, and to the king of Sidon, by the hand of the messengers who come to Jerusalem to Zedekiah king of Judah.}
\VersePair{34:4}{And thou shalt commission them to say to their lords, Thus said the Lord God of Israel; Thus shall ye say to your lords;}{27:4}{Give them a command to their masters, saying, ‘Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says, “You shall tell your masters:}
\VersePair{34:5}{I have made the earth by my great power, and with my high arm, and I will give it to whomsoever it shall seem good in mine eyes.}{27:5}{‘I have made the earth, the men, and the animals that are on the surface of the earth by my great power and by my outstretched arm. I give it to whom it seems right to me.}
\VersePair{34:6}{I gave the earth to Nabuchodonosor king of Babylon to serve him, and the wild beasts of the field to labour for him.}{27:6}{Now I have given all these lands into the hand of Nebuchadnezzar the king of Babylon, my servant. I have also given the animals of the field to him to serve him.}
\VersePair{34:8}{And the nation and kingdom, all that shall not put their neck under the yoke of the king of Babylon, with sword and famine will I visit them, saith the Lord, until they are consumed by his hand.}{27:8}{“‘“‘It will happen that I will punish the nation and the kingdom which will not serve the same Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon, and that will not put their neck under the yoke of the king of Babylon,’ says Yahweh, ‘with the sword, with famine, and with pestilence, until I have consumed them by his hand.}
\VersePair{34:9}{And hearken ye not to your false prophets, nor to them that divine to you, nor to them that foretel events by dreams to you, nor to your auguries, nor your sorcerers, that say, Ye shall by no means work for the king of Babylon:}{27:9}{But as for you, don’t listen to your prophets, to your diviners, to your dreams, to your soothsayers, or to your sorcerers, who speak to you, saying, “You shall not serve the king of Babylon;”}
\VersePair{34:10}{for they prophesy lies to you, to remove you far from your land.}{27:10}{for they prophesy a lie to you, to remove you far from your land, so that I would drive you out, and you would perish.}
\VersePair{34:11}{But the nation which shall put its neck under the yoke of the king of Babylon, and serve him, I will even leave it upon its land, and it shall serve him, and dwell in it.}{27:11}{But the nation that brings their neck under the yoke of the king of Babylon and serves him, that nation I will let remain in their own land,’ says Yahweh; ‘and they will till it and dwell in it.’”’”}
\VersePair{34:12}{I spoke also to Sedekias king of Juda according to all these words, saying, Put your neck into the yoke,}{27:12}{I spoke to Zedekiah king of Judah according to all these words, saying, “Bring your necks under the yoke of the king of Babylon, and serve him and his people, and live.}
\VersePair{34:14}{and serve the king of Babylon. For they prophesy unrighteous words to you,}{27:14}{Don’t listen to the words of the prophets who speak to you, saying, ‘You shall not serve the king of Babylon;’ for they prophesy a lie to you.}
\VersePair{34:15}{for I sent them not, saith the Lord; and they prophesy in my name unjustly, that I might destroy you, and ye should perish, and your prophets, who unrighteously prophesy lies to you.}{27:15}{For I have not sent them,” says Yahweh, “but they prophesy falsely in my name; that I may drive you out, and that you may perish, you, and the prophets who prophesy to you.”}
\VersePair{34:16}{I spoke to you, and to all this people, and to the priests, saying, Thus said the Lord; Hearken not to the words of the prophets that prophesy to you, saying, Behold, the vessels of the Lord's house shall return from Babylon: for they prophesy to you unrighteous words. I sent them not.}{27:16}{Also I spoke to the priests and to all this people, saying, Yahweh says, “Don’t listen to the words of your prophets who prophesy to you, saying, ‘Behold, the vessels of Yahweh’s house will now shortly be brought again from Babylon;’ for they prophesy a lie to you.}
\VersePair{34:18}{If they are prophets, and if the word of the Lord is in them, let them meet me, for thus has the Lord said.}{27:18}{But if they are prophets, and if Yahweh’s word is with them, let them now make intercession to Yahweh of Armies, that the vessels which are left in Yahweh’s house, in the house of the king of Judah, and at Jerusalem, don’t go to Babylon.}
\VersePair{34:19}{And as for the remaining vessels,}{27:19}{For Yahweh of Armies says concerning the pillars, concerning the sea, concerning the bases, and concerning the rest of the vessels that are left in this city,}
\VersePair{34:20}{which the king of Babylon took not, when he carried Jechonias prisoner out of Jerusalem,}{27:20}{which Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon didn’t take when he carried away captive Jeconiah the son of Jehoiakim, king of Judah, from Jerusalem to Babylon, and all the nobles of Judah and Jerusalem —}
\VersePair{34:22}{they shall go into Babylon, saith the Lord.}{27:22}{‘They will be carried to Babylon, and there they will be, until the day that I visit them,’ says Yahweh; ‘then I will bring them up, and restore them to this place.’”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{35}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{35:1}{And it came to pass in the fourth year of Sedekias king of Juda, in the fifth month, that Ananias the false prophet, the son of Azor, from Gabaon, spoke to me in the house of the Lord, in the sight of the priests and all the people, saying,}{28:1}{That same year, in the beginning of the reign of Zedekiah king of Judah, in the fourth year, in the fifth month, Hananiah the son of Azzur, the prophet, who was of Gibeon, spoke to me in Yahweh’s house, in the presence of the priests and of all the people, saying,}
\VersePair{35:2}{Thus saith the Lord; I have broken the yoke of the king of Babylon.}{28:2}{“Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says, ‘I have broken the yoke of the king of Babylon.}
\VersePair{35:3}{Yet two full years, and I will return into this place the vessels of the house of the Lord,}{28:3}{Within two full years I will bring again into this place all the vessels of Yahweh’s house that Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon took away from this place and carried to Babylon.}
\VersePair{35:4}{and Jechonias, and the captivity of Juda: for I will break the yoke of the king of Babylon.}{28:4}{I will bring again to this place Jeconiah the son of Jehoiakim, king of Judah, with all the captives of Judah, who went to Babylon,’ says Yahweh; ‘for I will break the yoke of the king of Babylon.’”}
\VersePair{35:5}{Then Jeremias spoke to Ananias in the sight of all the people, and in the sight of the priests that stood in the house of the Lord,}{28:5}{Then the prophet Jeremiah said to the prophet Hananiah in the presence of the priests, and in the presence of all the people who stood in Yahweh’s house,}
\VersePair{35:6}{and Jeremias said, May the Lord indeed do thus; may he confirm thy word which thou dost prophesy, to return the vessels of the house of the Lord, and all the captivity, out of Babylon to this place.}{28:6}{even the prophet Jeremiah said, “Amen! May Yahweh do so. May Yahweh perform your words which you have prophesied, to bring again the vessels of Yahweh’s house, and all those who are captives, from Babylon to this place.}
\VersePair{35:7}{Nevertheless hear ye the word of the Lord which I speak in your ears, and in the ears of all the people.}{28:7}{Nevertheless listen now to this word that I speak in your ears, and in the ears of all the people:}
\VersePair{35:8}{The prophets that were before me and before you of old, also prophesied over much country, and against great kingdoms, concerning war.}{28:8}{The prophets who have been before me and before you of old prophesied against many countries, and against great kingdoms, of war, of evil, and of pestilence.}
\VersePair{35:9}{As for the prophet that has prophesied for peace, when the word has come to pass, they shall know the prophet whom the Lord has sent them in truth.}{28:9}{As for the prophet who prophesies of peace, when the word of the prophet happens, then the prophet will be known, that Yahweh has truly sent him.”}
\VersePair{35:10}{Then Ananias took the yokes from the neck of Jeremias in the sight of all the people, and broke them to pieces.}{28:10}{Then Hananiah the prophet took the bar from off the prophet Jeremiah’s neck, and broke it.}
\VersePair{35:11}{And Ananias spoke in the presence of all the people, saying, Thus said the Lord; Thus will I break the yoke of the king of Babylon from the necks of all the nations.
