And Jeremias went his way.}{28:11}{Hananiah spoke in the presence of all the people, saying, “Yahweh says: ‘Even so I will break the yoke of Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon from off the neck of all the nations within two full years.’” Then the prophet Jeremiah went his way.}
\VersePair{35:12}{And the word of the Lord came to Jeremias, after that Ananias had broken the yokes off his neck, saying,}{28:12}{Then Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah, after Hananiah the prophet had broken the bar from off the neck of the prophet Jeremiah, saying,}
\VersePair{35:13}{Go and speak to Ananias, saying, Thus saith the Lord; Thou hast broken the yokes of wood; but I will make instead of them yokes of iron.}{28:13}{“Go, and tell Hananiah, saying, ‘Yahweh says, “You have broken the bars of wood, but you have made in their place bars of iron.”}
\VersePair{35:14}{For thus said the Lord, I have put a yoke of iron on the neck of all the nations, that they may serve the king of Babylon.}{28:14}{For Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says, “I have put a yoke of iron on the neck of all these nations, that they may serve Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon; and they will serve him. I have also given him the animals of the field.”’”}
\VersePair{35:15}{And Jeremias said to Ananias, The Lord has not sent thee; and thou hast caused this people to trust in unrighteousness.}{28:15}{Then the prophet Jeremiah said to Hananiah the prophet, “Listen, Hananiah! Yahweh has not sent you, but you make this people trust in a lie.}
\VersePair{35:16}{Therefore thus said the Lord: Behold, I will cast thee off from the face of the earth: this year thou shalt die.}{28:16}{Therefore Yahweh says, ‘Behold, I will send you away from off the surface of the earth. This year you will die, because you have spoken rebellion against Yahweh.’”}
\VersePair{35:17}{So he died in the seventh month.}{28:17}{So Hananiah the prophet died the same year in the seventh month.}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{36}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{36:1}{And these are the words of the book which Jeremias sent from Jerusalem to the elders of the captivity, and to the priests, and to the false prophets, even an epistle to Babylon for the captivity, and to all the people;}{29:1}{Now these are the words of the letter that Jeremiah the prophet sent from Jerusalem to the residue of the elders of the captivity, and to the priests, to the prophets, and to all the people whom Nebuchadnezzar had carried away captive from Jerusalem to Babylon,}
\VersePair{36:2}{(after the departure of Jechonias the king and the queen, and the eunuchs, and every freeman, and bondman, and artificer, out of Jerusalem;)}{29:2}{( after Jeconiah the king, the queen mother, the eunuchs, the princes of Judah and Jerusalem, the craftsmen, and the smiths had departed from Jerusalem ),}
\VersePair{36:3}{by the hand of Eleasan son of Saphan, and Gamarias son of Chelcias, (whom Sedekias king of Juda sent to the king of Babylon to Babylon) saying,}{29:3}{by the hand of Elasah the son of Shaphan and Gemariah the son of Hilkiah, (whom Zedekiah king of Judah sent to Babylon to Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon). It said:}
\VersePair{36:4}{Thus said the Lord God of Israel concerning the captivity which I caused to be carried away from Jerusalem;}{29:4}{Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says to all the captives whom I have caused to be carried away captive from Jerusalem to Babylon:}
\VersePair{36:5}{Build ye houses, and inhabit them; and plant gardens, and eat the fruits thereof;}{29:5}{“Build houses and dwell in them. Plant gardens and eat their fruit.}
\VersePair{36:6}{and take ye wives, and beget sons and daughters; and take wives for your sons, and give your daughters to husbands, and be multiplied, and be not diminished.}{29:6}{Take wives and father sons and daughters. Take wives for your sons, and give your daughters to husbands, that they may bear sons and daughters. Multiply there, and don’t be diminished.}
\VersePair{36:7}{And seek the peace of the land into which I have carried you captive, and ye shall pray to the Lord for the people: for in its peace ye shall have peace.}{29:7}{Seek the peace of the city where I have caused you to be carried away captive, and pray to Yahweh for it; for in its peace you will have peace.”}
\VersePair{36:8}{For thus saith the Lord; Let not the false prophets that are among you persuade you, and let not your diviners persuade you, and hearken not to your dreams which ye dream.}{29:8}{For Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says: “Don’t let your prophets who are among you and your diviners deceive you. Don’t listen to your dreams which you cause to be dreamed.}
\VersePair{36:9}{For they prophesy to you unrighteous words in my name; and I sent them not.}{29:9}{For they prophesy falsely to you in my name. I have not sent them,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{36:10}{For thus said the Lord; When seventy years shall be on the point of being accomplished at Babylon, I will visit you, and will confirm my words to you, to bring back your people to this place.}{29:10}{For Yahweh says, “After seventy years are accomplished for Babylon, I will visit you and perform my good word toward you, in causing you to return to this place.}
\VersePair{36:11}{And I will devise for you a device of peace, and not evil, to bestow upon you these good things.}{29:11}{For I know the thoughts that I think toward you,” says Yahweh, “thoughts of peace, and not of evil, to give you hope and a future.}
\VersePair{36:12}{And do ye pray to me, and I will hearken to you: and do ye earnestly seek me, and ye shall find me;}{29:12}{You shall call on me, and you shall go and pray to me, and I will listen to you.}
\VersePair{36:13}{for ye shall seek me with your whole heart.}{29:13}{You shall seek me and find me, when you search for me with all your heart.}
\VersePair{36:14}{And I will appear to you:}{29:14}{I will be found by you,” says Yahweh, “and I will turn again your captivity, and I will gather you from all the nations, and from all the places where I have driven you,” says Yahweh. “I will bring you again to the place from where I caused you to be carried away captive.”}
\VersePair{36:15}{whereas ye said, The Lord has appointed for us prophets in Babylon:}{29:15}{Because you have said, “Yahweh has raised us up prophets in Babylon,”}
\VersePair{36:16}{}{29:16}{Yahweh says concerning the king who sits on David’s throne, and concerning all the people who dwell in this city, your brothers who haven’t gone with you into captivity,}
\VersePair{36:17}{}{29:17}{Yahweh of Armies says: “Behold, I will send on them the sword, the famine, and the pestilence, and will make them like rotten figs that can’t be eaten, they are so bad.}
\VersePair{36:18}{}{29:18}{I will pursue after them with the sword, with the famine, and with the pestilence, and will deliver them to be tossed back and forth among all the kingdoms of the earth, to be an object of horror, an astonishment, a hissing, and a reproach among all the nations where I have driven them,}
\VersePair{36:19}{}{29:19}{because they have not listened to my words,” says Yahweh, “with which I sent to them my servants the prophets, rising up early and sending them; but you would not hear,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{36:20}{}{29:20}{Hear therefore Yahweh’s word, all you captives whom I have sent away from Jerusalem to Babylon.}
\VersePair{36:21}{Thus saith the Lord concerning Achiab, and concerning Sedekias; Behold, I will deliver them into the hands of the king of Babylon; and he shall smite them in your sight.}{29:21}{Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says concerning Ahab the son of Kolaiah, and concerning Zedekiah the son of Maaseiah, who prophesy a lie to you in my name: “Behold, I will deliver them into the hand of Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon; and he will kill them before your eyes.}
\VersePair{36:22}{And they shall make of them a curse in all the captivity of Juda in Babylon, saying, The Lord do to thee as he did to Sedekias, and as he did to Achiab, whom the king of Babylon fried in the fire;}{29:22}{A curse will be taken up about them by all the captives of Judah who are in Babylon, saying, ‘Yahweh make you like Zedekiah and like Ahab, whom the king of Babylon roasted in the fire;’}
\VersePair{36:23}{because of the iniquity which they wrought in Israel, and because they committed adultery with the wives of their fellow-citizens, and spoke a word in my name, which I did not command them to speak, and I am witness, saith the Lord.}{29:23}{because they have done foolish things in Israel, and have committed adultery with their neighbors’wives, and have spoken words in my name falsely, which I didn’t command them. I am he who knows, and am witness,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{36:24}{And to Samæas the Ælamite thou shalt say,}{29:24}{Concerning Shemaiah the Nehelamite you shall speak, saying,}
\VersePair{36:25}{I sent thee not in my name: and to Sophonias the priest the son of Maasæas say thou,}{29:25}{“Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says, ‘Because you have sent letters in your own name to all the people who are at Jerusalem, and to Zephaniah the son of Maaseiah, the priest, and to all the priests, saying,}
\VersePair{36:26}{The Lord has made thee priest in the place of Jodae the priest, to be ruler in the house of the Lord over every prophet, and to every madman, and thou shalt put them in prison, and into the dungeon.}{29:26}{“Yahweh has made you priest in the place of Jehoiada the priest, that there may be officers in Yahweh’s house, for every man who is crazy and makes himself a prophet, that you should put him in the stocks and in shackles.}
\VersePair{36:27}{And now wherefore have ye reviled together Jeremias of Anathoth, who prophesied to you?}{29:27}{Now therefore, why have you not rebuked Jeremiah of Anathoth, who makes himself a prophet to you,}
\VersePair{36:28}{Did he not send for this purpose? for in the course of this month he sent to you to Babylon, saying, It is far off: build ye houses, and inhabit them; and plant gardens, and eat the fruit of them.}{29:28}{because he has sent to us in Babylon, saying, The captivity is long. Build houses, and dwell in them. Plant gardens, and eat their fruit?”’”}
\VersePair{36:29}{And Sophonias read the book in the ears of Jeremias.}{29:29}{Zephaniah the priest read this letter in the hearing of Jeremiah the prophet.}
\VersePair{36:30}{Then the word of the Lord came to Jeremias, saying,}{29:30}{Then Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah, saying,}
\VersePair{36:31}{Send to the captivity, saying, Thus saith the Lord concerning Samæas the Ælamite, Since Samæas has prophesied to you, and I sent him not, and he has made you to trust in iniquity,}{29:31}{“Send to all of the captives, saying, ‘Yahweh says concerning Shemaiah the Nehelamite: “Because Shemaiah has prophesied to you, and I didn’t send him, and he has caused you to trust in a lie,”}
\VersePair{36:32}{therefore thus saith the Lord; Behold, I will visit Samæas, and his family: and there shall not be a man of them in the midst of you to see the good which I will do to you: they shall not see it.}{29:32}{therefore Yahweh says, “Behold, I will punish Shemaiah the Nehelamite and his offspring. He will not have a man to dwell among this people. He won’t see the good that I will do to my people,” says Yahweh, “because he has spoken rebellion against Yahweh.”’”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{37}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{37:1}{The Word that came to Jeremias from the Lord, saying,}{30:1}{The word that came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, saying,}
\VersePair{37:2}{Thus speaks the Lord God of Israel, saying, Write all the words which I have spoken to thee in a book.}{30:2}{“Yahweh, the God of Israel, says, ‘Write all the words that I have spoken to you in a book.}
\VersePair{37:3}{For, behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when I will bring back the captivity of my people Israel and Juda, said the Lord: and I will bring them back to the land which I gave to their fathers, and they shall be lords of it.}{30:3}{For, behold, the days come,’ says Yahweh, ‘that I will reverse the captivity of my people Israel and Judah,’ says Yahweh. ‘I will cause them to return to the land that I gave to their fathers, and they will possess it.’”}
\VersePair{37:4}{And these are the Words which the Lord spoke concerning Israel and Juda:}{30:4}{These are the words that Yahweh spoke concerning Israel and concerning Judah.}
\VersePair{37:5}{Thus said the Lord: Ye shall hear a sound of fear, there is fear, and there is not peace.}{30:5}{{\raggedright For Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“We have heard a voice of trembling;}\poemline{2}{a voice of fear, and not of peace.}}}
\VersePair{37:6}{Enquire, and see if a male has born a child? and ask concerning the fear, wherein they shall hold their loins, and look for safety: for I have seen every man, and his hands are on his loins; their faces are turned to paleness.}{30:6}{{\raggedright Ask now, and see whether a man travails with child. \poemline{2}{Why do I see every man with his hands on his waist, as a woman in travail,}\poemline{2}{and all faces are turned pale?}}}
\VersePair{37:7}{For that day is great, and there is not such another; and it is a time of straitness to Jacob; but he shall be saved out of it.}{30:7}{{\raggedright Alas, for that day is great, so that none is like it! \poemline{2}{It is even the time of Jacob’s trouble;}\poemline{2}{but he will be saved out of it.}}}
\VersePair{37:8}{In that day, said the Lord, I will break the yoke off their neck, and will burst their bonds, and they shall no longer serve strangers:}{30:8}{{\raggedright It will come to pass in that day, says Yahweh of Armies, that I will break his yoke from off your neck, \poemline{2}{and will burst your bonds.}\poemline{2}{Strangers will no more make them their bondservants;}}}
\VersePair{37:9}{but they shall serve the Lord their God; and I will raise up to them David their king.}{30:9}{{\raggedright but they will serve Yahweh their God, \poemline{2}{and David their king,}\poemline{2}{whom I will raise up to them.}}}
\VersePair{37:10}{}{30:10}{{\raggedright Therefore don’t be afraid, O Jacob my servant, says Yahweh. \poemline{2}{Don’t be dismayed, Israel.}\poemline{1}{For, behold, I will save you from afar,}\poemline{2}{and save your offspring from the land of their captivity.}\poemline{1}{Jacob will return,}\poemline{2}{and will be quiet and at ease.}\poemline{2}{No one will make him afraid.}}}
\VersePair{37:11}{}{30:11}{{\raggedright For I am with you, says Yahweh, to save you; \poemline{2}{for I will make a full end of all the nations where I have scattered you,}\poemline{2}{but I will not make a full end of you;}\poemline{1}{but I will correct you in measure,}\poemline{2}{and will in no way leave you unpunished.”}}}
\VersePair{37:12}{Thus saith the Lord; I have brought on thee destruction; thy stroke is painful.}{30:12}{{\raggedright For Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“Your hurt is incurable.}\poemline{2}{Your wound is grievous.}}}
\VersePair{37:13}{There is none to judge thy cause: thou hast been painfully treated for healing, there is no help for thee.}{30:13}{{\raggedright There is no one to plead your cause, \poemline{2}{that you may be bound up.}\poemline{2}{You have no healing medicines.}}}
\VersePair{37:14}{All thy friends have forgotten thee; they shall not ask about thee at all, for I have smitten thee with the stroke of an enemy, even severe correction: thy sins have abounded above all thine iniquity.}{30:14}{{\raggedright All your lovers have forgotten you. \poemline{2}{They don’t seek you.}\poemline{1}{For I have wounded you with the wound of an enemy,}\poemline{2}{with the chastisement of a cruel one,}\poemline{1}{for the greatness of your iniquity,}\poemline{2}{because your sins were increased.}}}
\VersePair{37:16}{Therefore all that devour thee shall be eaten, and all thine enemies shall eat all their own flesh. Thy sins have abounded beyond the multitude of thine iniquities, therefore they have done these things to thee. And they that spoil thee shall become a spoil, and I will give up to be plundered all that have plundered thee.}{30:16}{{\raggedright Therefore all those who devour you will be devoured. \poemline{2}{All your adversaries, everyone of them, will go into captivity.}\poemline{1}{Those who plunder you will be plunder.}\poemline{2}{I will make all who prey on you become prey.}}}
\VersePair{37:17}{For I will bring about thy healing, I will heal thee of thy grievous wound, saith the Lord; for thou art called Dispersed: she is your prey, for no one seeks after her.}{30:17}{{\raggedright For I will restore health to you, \poemline{2}{and I will heal you of your wounds,” says Yahweh,}\poemline{1}{“because they have called you an outcast,}\poemline{2}{saying, ‘It is Zion, whom no man seeks after.’”}}}
\VersePair{37:18}{Thus said the Lord; Behold, I will turn the captivity of Jacob, and will have pity upon his prisoners; and the city shall be built upon her hill, and the people shall settle after their manner.}{30:18}{{\raggedright Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Behold, I will reverse the captivity of Jacob’s tents,}\poemline{2}{and have compassion on his dwelling places.}\poemline{1}{The city will be built on its own hill,}\poemline{2}{and the palace will be inhabited in its own place.}}}
\VersePair{37:19}{And there shall go forth from them singers, even the sound of men making merry: and I will multiply them, and they shall not at all be diminished.}{30:19}{{\raggedright Thanksgiving will proceed out of them \poemline{2}{with the voice of those who make merry.}\poemline{1}{I will multiply them,}\poemline{2}{and they will not be few;}\poemline{1}{I will also glorify them,}\poemline{2}{and they will not be small.}}}
\VersePair{37:20}{And their sons shall go in as before, and their testimonies shall be established before me, and I will visit them that afflict them.}{30:20}{{\raggedright Their children also will be as before, \poemline{2}{and their congregation will be established before me.}\poemline{2}{I will punish all who oppress them.}}}
\VersePair{37:21}{And their mighty ones shall be over them, and their prince shall proceed of themselves; and I will gather them, and they shall return to me: for who is this that has set his heart to return to me? saith the Lord.}{30:21}{{\raggedright Their prince will be one of them, \poemline{2}{and their ruler will proceed from among them.}\poemline{1}{I will cause him to draw near,}\poemline{2}{and he will approach me;}\poemline{2}{for who is he who has had boldness to approach me?” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{37:23}{For the wrathful anger of the Lord has gone forth, even a whirlwind of anger has gone forth: it shall come upon the ungodly.}{30:23}{{\raggedright Behold, Yahweh’s storm, his wrath, has gone out, \poemline{2}{a sweeping storm;}\poemline{2}{it will burst on the head of the wicked.}}}
\VersePair{37:24}{The fierce anger of the Lord shall not return, until he shall execute it, and until he shall establish the purpose of his heart: in the latter days ye shall know these things.}{30:24}{{\raggedright The fierce anger of Yahweh will not return until he has accomplished, \poemline{2}{and until he has performed the intentions of his heart.}\poemline{2}{In the latter days you will understand it.”}}}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{38}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{38:1}{At that time, saith the Lord, I will be a God to the family of Israel, and they shall be to me a people.}{31:1}{“At that time,” says Yahweh, “I will be the God of all the families of Israel, and they will be my people.”}
\VersePair{38:2}{Thus saith the Lord, I found him warm in the wilderness with them that were slain with the sword: go ye and destroy not Israel.}{31:2}{Yahweh says, “The people who survive the sword found favor in the wilderness; even Israel, when I went to cause him to rest.”}
\VersePair{38:3}{The Lord appeared to him from afar, saying, I have loved thee with an everlasting love: therefore have I drawn thee in compassion.}{31:3}{{\raggedright Yahweh appeared of old to me, saying, \poemline{1}{“Yes, I have loved you with an everlasting love.}\poemline{2}{Therefore I have drawn you with loving kindness.}}}
\VersePair{38:4}{For I will build thee, and thou shalt be built, O virgin of Israel: thou shalt yet take thy timbrel, and go forth with the party of them that make merry.}{31:4}{{\raggedright I will build you again, \poemline{2}{and you will be built, O virgin of Israel.}\poemline{1}{You will again be adorned with your tambourines,}\poemline{2}{and will go out in the dances of those who make merry.}}}
\VersePair{38:5}{For ye have planted vineyards on the mountains of Samaria: plant ye, and praise.}{31:5}{{\raggedright Again you will plant vineyards on the mountains of Samaria. \poemline{2}{The planters will plant,}\poemline{2}{and will enjoy its fruit.}}}
\VersePair{38:6}{For it is a day when those that plead on the mountains of Ephraim shall call, saying, Arise ye, and go up to Sion to the Lord your God.}{31:6}{{\raggedright For there will be a day that the watchmen on the hills of Ephraim cry, \poemline{2}{‘Arise! Let’s go up to Zion to Yahweh our God.’”}}}
\VersePair{38:7}{For thus saith the Lord to Jacob; Rejoice ye, and exult over the head of the nations: make proclamation, and praise ye: say, The Lord has delivered his people, the remnant of Israel.}{31:7}{{\raggedright For Yahweh says, \poemline{1}{“Sing with gladness for Jacob,}\poemline{2}{and shout for the chief of the nations.}\poemline{1}{Publish, praise, and say,}\poemline{2}{‘Yahweh, save your people,}\poemline{2}{the remnant of Israel!’}}}
\VersePair{38:8}{Behold, I bring them from the north, and will gather them from the end of the earth to the feast of the passover: and the people shall beget a great multitude, and they shall return hither.}{31:8}{{\raggedright Behold, I will bring them from the north country, \poemline{2}{and gather them from the uttermost parts of the earth,}\poemline{1}{along with the blind and the lame,}\poemline{2}{the woman with child and her who travails with child together.}\poemline{2}{They will return as a great company.}}}
\VersePair{38:9}{They went forth with weeping, and I will bring them back with consolation, causing them to lodge by the channels of waters in a straight way, and they shall not err in it: for I am become a father to Israel, and Ephraim is my first-born.}{31:9}{{\raggedright They will come with weeping. \poemline{2}{I will lead them with petitions.}\poemline{1}{I will cause them to walk by rivers of waters,}\poemline{2}{in a straight way in which they won’t stumble;}\poemline{1}{for I am a father to Israel.}\poemline{2}{Ephraim is my firstborn.}}}
\VersePair{38:10}{Hear the words of the Lord, ye nations, and proclaim them to the islands afar off; say, He that scattered Israel will also gather him, and keep him as one that feeds his flock.}{31:10}{{\raggedright “Hear Yahweh’s word, you nations, \poemline{2}{and declare it in the distant islands. Say,}\poemline{1}{‘He who scattered Israel will gather him,}\poemline{2}{and keep him, as a shepherd does his flock.’}}}
\VersePair{38:11}{For the Lord has ransomed Jacob, he has rescued him out of the hand of them that were stronger than he.}{31:11}{{\raggedright For Yahweh has ransomed Jacob, \poemline{2}{and redeemed him from the hand of him who was stronger than he.}}}
\VersePair{38:12}{And they shall come, and shall rejoice in the mount of Sion, and shall come to the good things of the Lord, even to a land of corn, and wine, and fruits, and cattle, and sheep: and their soul shall be as a fruitful tree; and they shall hunger no more.}{31:12}{{\raggedright They will come and sing in the height of Zion, \poemline{2}{and will flow to the goodness of Yahweh,}\poemline{1}{to the grain, to the new wine, to the oil,}\poemline{2}{and to the young of the flock and of the herd.}\poemline{1}{Their soul will be as a watered garden.}\poemline{2}{They will not sorrow any more at all.}}}
\VersePair{38:13}{Then shall the virgins rejoice in the assembly of youth, and the old men shall rejoice; and I will turn their mourning into joy, and will make them merry.}{31:13}{{\raggedright Then the virgin will rejoice in the dance, \poemline{2}{the young men and the old together;}\poemline{1}{for I will turn their mourning into joy,}\poemline{2}{and will comfort them, and make them rejoice from their sorrow.}}}
\VersePair{38:14}{I will expand and cheer with wine the soul of the priests the sons of Levi, and my people shall be satisfied with my good things: thus saith the Lord.}{31:14}{{\raggedright I will satiate the soul of the priests with fatness, \poemline{2}{and my people will be satisfied with my goodness,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{38:15}{A voice was heard in Rama, of lamentation, and of weeping, and wailing; Rachel would not cease weeping for her children, because they are not.}{31:15}{{\raggedright Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“A voice is heard in Ramah,}\poemline{2}{lamentation and bitter weeping,}\poemline{1}{Rachel weeping for her children.}\poemline{2}{She refuses to be comforted for her children,}\poemline{2}{because they are no more.”}}}
\VersePair{38:16}{Thus saith the Lord; Let thy voice cease from weeping, and thine eyes from thy tears: for there is a reward for thy works; and they shall return from the land of thine enemies.}{31:16}{{\raggedright Yahweh says: \poemline{1}{“Refrain your voice from weeping,}\poemline{2}{and your eyes from tears,}\poemline{2}{for your work will be rewarded,” says Yahweh.}\poemline{2}{“They will come again from the land of the enemy.}}}
\VersePair{38:17}{There shall be an abiding home for thy children.}{31:17}{{\raggedright There is hope for your latter end,” says Yahweh. \poemline{2}{“Your children will come again to their own territory.}}}
\VersePair{38:18}{I have heard the sound of Ephraim lamenting, and saying, Thou hast chastened me, and I was chastened; I as a calf was not willingly taught: turn thou me, and I shall turn; for thou art the Lord my God.}{31:18}{{\raggedright “I have surely heard Ephraim grieving thus, \poemline{2}{‘You have chastised me,}\poemline{2}{and I was chastised, as an untrained calf.}\poemline{1}{Turn me, and I will be turned,}\poemline{2}{for you are Yahweh my God.}}}
\VersePair{38:19}{For after my captivity I repented; and after I knew, I groaned for the day of shame, and shewed thee that I bore reproach from my youth.}{31:19}{{\raggedright Surely after that I was turned. \poemline{2}{I repented.}\poemline{1}{After that I was instructed.}\poemline{2}{I struck my thigh.}\poemline{1}{I was ashamed, yes, even confounded,}\poemline{2}{because I bore the reproach of my youth.’}}}
\VersePair{38:20}{Ephraim is a beloved son, a pleasing child to me: for because my words are in him, I will surely remember him: therefore I made haste to help him; I will surely have mercy upon him, saith the Lord.}{31:20}{{\raggedright Is Ephraim my dear son? \poemline{2}{Is he a darling child?}\poemline{1}{For as often as I speak against him,}\poemline{2}{I still earnestly remember him.}\poemline{1}{Therefore my heart yearns for him.}\poemline{2}{I will surely have mercy on him,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{38:21}{Prepare thyself, O Sion; execute vengeance; look to thy ways: return, O virgin of Israel, by the way by which thou wentest, return mourning to thy cities.}{31:21}{{\raggedright “Set up road signs. \poemline{2}{Make guideposts.}\poemline{1}{Set your heart toward the highway,}\poemline{2}{even the way by which you went.}\poemline{1}{Turn again, virgin of Israel.}\poemline{2}{Turn again to these your cities.}}}
\VersePair{38:22}{How long, O disgraced daughter, wilt thou turn away? for the Lord has created safety for a new plantation: men shall go about in safety.}{31:22}{{\raggedright How long will you go here and there, \poemline{2}{you backsliding daughter?}\poemline{1}{For Yahweh has created a new thing in the earth:}\poemline{2}{a woman will encompass a man.”}}}
\VersePair{38:23}{For thus saith the Lord; They shall yet speak this word in the land of Juda, and in the cities thereof, when I shall turn his captivity; blessed be the Lord on his righteous holy mountain!}{31:23}{Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says: “Yet again they will use this speech in the land of Judah and in its cities, when I reverse their captivity: ‘Yahweh bless you, habitation of righteousness, mountain of holiness.’}
\VersePair{38:24}{And there shall be dwellers in the cities of Juda, and in all his land, together with the husbandman, and the shepherd shall go forth with the flock.}{31:24}{Judah and all its cities will dwell therein together, the farmers, and those who go about with flocks.}
\VersePair{38:25}{For I have saturated every thirsting soul, and filled every hungry soul.}{31:25}{For I have satiated the weary soul, and I have replenished every sorrowful soul.”}
\VersePair{38:26}{Therefore I awaked, and beheld; and my sleep was sweet to me.}{31:26}{On this I awakened, and saw; and my sleep was sweet to me.}
\VersePair{38:27}{Therefore, behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when I will sow the house of Israel and the house of Juda with the seed of man, and the seed of beast.}{31:27}{“Behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, “that I will sow the house of Israel and the house of Judah with the seed of man and with the seed of animal.}
\VersePair{38:28}{And it shall come to pass, that as I watched over them, to pull down, and to afflict, so will I watch over them, to build, and to plant, saith the Lord.}{31:28}{It will happen that, like as I have watched over them to pluck up and to break down and to overthrow and to destroy and to afflict, so I will watch over them to build and to plant,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{38:29}{In those days they shall certainly not say, The fathers ate a sour grape, and the children's teeth were set on edge.}{31:29}{{\raggedright “In those days they will say no more, \poemline{1}{“‘The fathers have eaten sour grapes,}\poemline{2}{and the children’s teeth are set on edge.’}}}
\VersePair{38:30}{But every one shall die in his own sin; and the teeth of him that eats the sour grape shall be set on edge.}{31:30}{But everyone will die for his own iniquity. Every man who eats the sour grapes, his teeth will be set on edge.}
\VersePair{38:31}{Behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when I will make a new covenant with the house of Israel, and with the house of Juda:}{31:31}{“Behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, “that I will make a new covenant with the house of Israel, and with the house of Judah,}
\VersePair{38:32}{not according to the covenant which I made with their fathers in the day when I took hold of their hand to bring them out of the land of Egypt; for they abode not in my covenant, and I disregarded them, saith the Lord.}{31:32}{not according to the covenant that I made with their fathers in the day that I took them by the hand to bring them out of the land of Egypt, which covenant of mine they broke, although I was a husband to them,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{38:33}{For this is my covenant which I will make with the house of Israel; after those days, saith the Lord, I will surely put my laws into their mind, and write them on their hearts; and I will be to them a God, and they shall be to me a people.}{31:33}{{\raggedright “But this is the covenant that I will make with the house of Israel after those days,” says Yahweh: \poemline{1}{“I will put my law in their inward parts,}\poemline{2}{and I will write it in their heart.}\poemline{1}{I will be their God,}\poemline{2}{and they shall be my people.}}}
\VersePair{38:34}{And they shall not at all teach every one his fellow citizen, and every one his brother, saying, Know the Lord: for all shall know me, from the least of them to the greatest of them: for I will be merciful to their iniquities, and their sins I will remember no more.}{31:34}{{\raggedright They will no longer each teach his neighbor, \poemline{2}{and every man teach his brother, saying, ‘Know Yahweh;’}\poemline{1}{for they will all know me,}\poemline{2}{from their least to their greatest,” says Yahweh,}\poemline{1}{“for I will forgive their iniquity,}\poemline{2}{and I will remember their sin no more.”}}}
\VersePair{38:35}{Though the sky should be raised to a greater height, saith the Lord, and though the ground of the earth should be sunk lower beneath, yet I will not cast off the family of Israel, saith the Lord, for all that they have done.}{31:37}{{\raggedright Yahweh says: “If heaven above can be measured, \poemline{2}{and the foundations of the earth searched out beneath,}\poemline{2}{then I will also cast off all the offspring of Israel for all that they have done,” says Yahweh.}}}
\VersePair{38:36}{Thus saith the Lord, who gives the sun for a light by day, the moon and the stars for a light by night, and makes a roaring in the sea, so that the waves thereof roar; the Lord Almighty is his name:}{31:35}{{\raggedright Yahweh, who gives the sun for a light by day, \poemline{2}{and the ordinances of the moon and of the stars for a light by night,}\poemline{1}{who stirs up the sea, so that its waves roar —}\poemline{2}{Yahweh of Armies is his name, says:}}}
\VersePair{38:37}{if these ordinances cease from before me, saith the Lord, then shall the family of Israel cease to be a nation before me for ever.}{31:36}{{\raggedright “If these ordinances depart from before me,” says Yahweh, \poemline{2}{“then the offspring of Israel also will cease from being a nation before me forever.”}}}
\VersePair{38:38}{Behold, the days come, saith the Lord, when the city shall be built to the Lord from the tower of Anameel to the gate of the corner.}{31:38}{“Behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, “that the city will be built to Yahweh from the tower of Hananel to the gate of the corner.}
\VersePair{38:39}{And the measurement of it shall proceed in front of them as far as the hills of Gareb, and it shall be compassed with a circular wall of choice stones.}{31:39}{The measuring line will go out further straight onward to the hill Gareb, and will turn toward Goah.}
\VersePair{38:40}{And all the Asaremoth even to Nachal Kedron, as far as the corner of the horse-gate eastward, shall be holiness to the Lord; and it shall not fail any more, and shall not be destroyed for ever.}{31:40}{The whole valley of the dead bodies and of the ashes, and all the fields to the brook Kidron, to the corner of the horse gate toward the east, will be holy to Yahweh. It will not be plucked up or thrown down any more forever.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{39}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{39:1}{The word that came from the Lord to Jeremias in the tenth year of king Sedekias, this is the eighteenth year of king Nabuchodonosor king of Babylon.}{32:1}{This is the word that came to Jeremiah from Yahweh in the tenth year of Zedekiah king of Judah, which was the eighteenth year of Nebuchadnezzar.}
\VersePair{39:2}{And the host of the king of Babylon had made a rampart against Jerusalem: and Jeremias was kept in the court of the prison, which is in the king's house;}{32:2}{Now at that time the king of Babylon’s army was besieging Jerusalem. Jeremiah the prophet was shut up in the court of the guard, which was in the king of Judah’s house.}
\VersePair{39:3}{in which king Sedekias had shut him up, saying, Wherefore dost thou prophesy, saying, Thus saith the Lord, Behold, I will give this city into the hands of the king of Babylon, and he shall take it;}{32:3}{For Zedekiah king of Judah had shut him up, saying, “Why do you prophesy, and say, ‘Yahweh says, “Behold, I will give this city into the hand of the king of Babylon, and he will take it;}
\VersePair{39:4}{and Sedekias shall by no means be delivered out of the hand of the Chaldeans, for he shall certainly be given up into the hands of the king of Babylon, and his mouth shall speak to his mouth, and his eyes shall look upon his eyes;}{32:4}{and Zedekiah king of Judah won’t escape out of the hand of the Chaldeans, but will surely be delivered into the hand of the king of Babylon, and will speak with him mouth to mouth, and his eyes will see his eyes;}
\VersePair{39:5}{and Sedekias shall go into Babylon, and dwell there?}{32:5}{and he will bring Zedekiah to Babylon, and he will be there until I visit him,” says Yahweh, “though you fight with the Chaldeans, you will not prosper ”’?”}
\VersePair{39:6}{And the Word of the Lord came to Jeremias, saying,}{32:6}{Jeremiah said, “Yahweh’s word came to me, saying,}
\VersePair{39:7}{Behold, Anameel the son of Salom thy father's brother is coming to thee, saying, Buy thee my field that is in Anathoth: for thou hast the right to take it as a purchase.}{32:7}{‘Behold, Hanamel the son of Shallum your uncle will come to you, saying, “Buy my field that is in Anathoth; for the right of redemption is yours to buy it.”’”}
\VersePair{39:8}{So Anameel the son of Salom my father's brother came to me into the court of the prison, and said, Buy thee my field that is in the land of Benjamin, in Anathoth: for thou hast a right to buy it, and thou art the elder. So I knew that it was the word of the Lord.}{32:8}{“So Hanamel my uncle’s son came to me in the court of the guard according to Yahweh’s word, and said to me, ‘Please buy my field that is in Anathoth, which is in the land of Benjamin; for the right of inheritance is yours, and the redemption is yours. Buy it for yourself.’ “Then I knew that this was Yahweh’s word.}
\VersePair{39:9}{And I bought the field of Anameel the son of my father's brother, and I weighed him seventeen shekels of silver.}{32:9}{I bought the field that was in Anathoth of Hanamel my uncle’s son, and weighed him the money, even seventeen shekels of silver. \footnote{32:9: A shekel is about 10 grams or about 0.35 ounces.}}
\VersePair{39:10}{And I wrote it in a book, and sealed it, and took the testimony of witnesses, and weighed the money in the balance.}{32:10}{I signed the deed, sealed it, called witnesses, and weighed the money in the balances to him.}
\VersePair{39:11}{And I took the book of the purchase that was sealed;}{32:11}{So I took the deed of the purchase, both that which was sealed, containing the terms and conditions, and that which was open;}
\VersePair{39:12}{and I gave it to Baruch son of Nerias, son of Maasæas, in the sight of Anameel my father's brother's son, and in the sight of the men that stood by and wrote in the book of the purchase, and in the sight of the Jews that were in the court of the prison.}{32:12}{and I delivered the deed of the purchase to Baruch the son of Neriah, the son of Mahseiah, in the presence of Hanamel my uncle’s son, and in the presence of the witnesses who signed the deed of the purchase, before all the Jews who sat in the court of the guard.}
\VersePair{39:13}{And I charged Baruch in their presence, saying, Thus saith the Lord Almighty;}{32:13}{“I commanded Baruch before them, saying,}
\VersePair{39:14}{Take this book of the purchase, and the book that has been read; and thou shalt put it into an earthen vessel, that it may remain many days.}{32:14}{Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says: ‘Take these deeds, this deed of the purchase which is sealed, and this deed which is open, and put them in an earthen vessel, that they may last many days.’}
\VersePair{39:15}{For thus saith the Lord; There shall yet be bought fields and houses and vineyards in this land.}{32:15}{For Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel says: ‘Houses and fields and vineyards will yet again be bought in this land.’}
\VersePair{39:16}{And I prayed to the Lord after I had given the book of the purchase to Baruch the son of Nerias, saying,}{32:16}{Now after I had delivered the deed of the purchase to Baruch the son of Neriah, I prayed to Yahweh, saying,}
\VersePair{39:17}{O ever living Lord! thou hast made the heaven and the earth by thy great power, and with thy high and lofty arm: nothing can be hidden from thee.}{32:17}{“Ah Lord Yahweh! Behold, you have made the heavens and the earth by your great power and by your outstretched arm. There is nothing too hard for you.}
\VersePair{39:18}{Granting mercy to thousands, and recompensing the sins of the fathers into the bosoms of their children after them: the great, the strong God;}{32:18}{You show loving kindness to thousands, and repay the iniquity of the fathers into the bosom of their children after them. The great, the mighty God, Yahweh of Armies is your name:}
\VersePair{39:19}{the Lord of great counsel, and mighty in deeds, the great Almighty God, and Lord of great name: thine eyes are upon the ways of the children of men, to give to every one according to his way:}{32:19}{great in counsel, and mighty in work; whose eyes are open to all the ways of the children of men, to give everyone according to his ways, and according to the fruit of his doings;}
\VersePair{39:20}{who hast wrought signs and wonders in the land of Egypt even to this day, and in Israel, and among the inhabitants of the earth; and thou didst make for thyself a name, as at this day;}{32:20}{who performed signs and wonders in the land of Egypt, even to this day, both in Israel and among other men; and made yourself a name, as it is today;}
\VersePair{39:21}{and thou didst bring out thy people Israel out of the land of Egypt with signs, and with wonders, with a mighty hand, and with a high arm, and with great sights;}{32:21}{and brought your people Israel out of the land of Egypt with signs, with wonders, with a strong hand, with an outstretched arm, and with great terror;}
\VersePair{39:22}{and thou gavest them this land, which thou didst swear to give to their fathers, a land flowing with milk and honey;}{32:22}{and gave them this land, which you swore to their fathers to give them, a land flowing with milk and honey.}
\VersePair{39:23}{and they went in, and took it; but they hearkened not to thy voice, and walked not in thine ordinances; they did none of the things which thou didst command them, and they caused all these calamities to happen to them.}{32:23}{They came in and possessed it, but they didn’t obey your voice and didn’t walk in your law. They have done nothing of all that you commanded them to do. Therefore you have caused all this evil to come upon them.}
\VersePair{39:24}{Behold, a multitude is come against the city to take it; and the city is given into the hands of the Chaldeans that fight against it, by the power of the sword, and the famine: as thou hast spoken, so has it happened.}{32:24}{“Behold, siege ramps have been built against the city to take it. The city is given into the hand of the Chaldeans who fight against it, because of the sword, of the famine, and of the pestilence. What you have spoken has happened. Behold, you see it.}
\VersePair{39:25}{And thou sayest to me, Buy thee the field for money; and I wrote a book, and sealed it, and took the testimony of witnesses: and the city is given into the hands of the Chaldeans.}{32:25}{You have said to me, Lord Yahweh, ‘Buy the field for money, and call witnesses;’ whereas the city is given into the hand of the Chaldeans.”}
\VersePair{39:26}{And the word of the Lord came to me, saying,}{32:26}{Then Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah, saying,}
\VersePair{39:27}{I am the Lord, the God of all flesh: shall anything be hidden from me!}{32:27}{“Behold, I am Yahweh, the God of all flesh. Is there anything too hard for me?}
\VersePair{39:28}{Therefore thus saith the Lord God of Israel; This city shall certainly be delivered into the hands of the king of Babylon, and he shall take it:}{32:28}{Therefore Yahweh says: Behold, I will give this city into the hand of the Chaldeans, and into the hand of Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon, and he will take it.}
\VersePair{39:29}{and the Chaldeans shall come to war against this city, and they shall burn this city with fire, and shall burn down the houses wherein they burnt incense on the roofs thereof to Baal, and poured drink-offerings to other gods, to provoke me.}{32:29}{The Chaldeans, who fight against this city, will come and set this city on fire, and burn it with the houses on whose roofs they have offered incense to Baal, and poured out drink offerings to other gods, to provoke me to anger.}
\VersePair{39:30}{For the children of Israel and the children of Juda alone did evil in my sight from their youth.}{32:30}{“For the children of Israel and the children of Judah have done only that which was evil in my sight from their youth; for the children of Israel have only provoked me to anger with the work of their hands, says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{39:31}{For this city was obnoxious to my anger and my wrath, from the day that they built it even to this day; that I should remove it from my presence,}{32:31}{For this city has been to me a provocation of my anger and of my wrath from the day that they built it even to this day, so that I should remove it from before my face,}
\VersePair{39:32}{because of all the wickedness of the children of Israel and Juda, which they wrought to provoke me, they and their kings, and their princes, and their priests, and their prophets, the men of Juda, and the dwellers in Jerusalem.}{32:32}{because of all the evil of the children of Israel and of the children of Judah, which they have done to provoke me to anger — they, their kings, their princes, their priests, their prophets, the men of Judah, and the inhabitants of Jerusalem.}
\VersePair{39:33}{And they turned the back to me, and not the face: whereas I taught them early in the morning, but they hearkened no more to receive instruction.}{32:33}{They have turned their backs to me, and not their faces. Although I taught them, rising up early and teaching them, yet they have not listened to receive instruction.}
\VersePair{39:34}{And they set their pollutions in the house, on which my name was called, by their uncleannesses.}{32:34}{But they set their abominations in the house which is called by my name, to defile it.}
\VersePair{39:35}{And they built to Baal the altars that are in the valley of the son of Ennom, to offer their sons and their daughters to king Moloch; which things I commanded them not, neither came it into my mind that they should do this abomination, to cause Juda to sin.}{32:35}{They built the high places of Baal, which are in the valley of the son of Hinnom, to cause their sons and their daughters to pass through fire to Molech, which I didn’t command them. It didn’t even come into my mind, that they should do this abomination, to cause Judah to sin.”}
\VersePair{39:36}{And now thus has the Lord God of Israel said concerning this city, of which thou sayest, It shall be delivered into the hands of the king of Babylon by the sword, and by famine, and banishment.}{32:36}{Now therefore Yahweh, the God of Israel, says concerning this city, about which you say, “It is given into the hand of the king of Babylon by the sword, by the famine, and by the pestilence:”}
\VersePair{39:37}{Behold, I will gather them out of every land, where I have scattered them in my anger, and my wrath, and great fury; and I will bring them back into this place, and will cause them to dwell safely:}{32:37}{“Behold, I will gather them out of all the countries where I have driven them in my anger, and in my wrath, and in great indignation; and I will bring them again to this place. I will cause them to dwell safely.}
\VersePair{39:38}{and they shall be to me a people, and I will be to them a God.}{32:38}{Then they will be my people, and I will be their God.}
\VersePair{39:39}{And I will give them another way, and another heart, to fear me continually, and that for good to them and their children after them.}{32:39}{I will give them one heart and one way, that they may fear me forever, for their good and the good of their children after them.}
\VersePair{39:40}{And I will make with them an everlasting covenant, which I will by no means turn away from them, and I will put my fear into their heart, that they may not depart from me.}{32:40}{I will make an everlasting covenant with them, that I will not turn away from following them, to do them good. I will put my fear in their hearts, that they may not depart from me.}
\VersePair{39:41}{And I will visit them to do them good, and I will plant them in this land in faithfulness, and with all my heart, and with all my soul.}{32:41}{Yes, I will rejoice over them to do them good, and I will plant them in this land assuredly with my whole heart and with my whole soul.”}
\VersePair{39:42}{For thus saith the Lord; As I have brought upon this people all these great evils, so will I bring upon them all the good things which I pronounced upon them.}{32:42}{For Yahweh says: “Just as I have brought all this great evil on this people, so I will bring on them all the good that I have promised them.}
\VersePair{39:43}{And there shall yet be fields bought in the land, of which thou sayest, It shall be destitute of man and beast; and they are delivered into the hands of the Chaldeans.}{32:43}{Fields will be bought in this land, about which you say, ‘It is desolate, without man or animal. It is given into the hand of the Chaldeans.’}
\VersePair{39:44}{And they shall buy fields for money, and thou shalt write a book, and seal it, and shalt take the testimony of witnesses in the land of Benjamin, and round about Jerusalem, and in the cities of Juda, and in the cities of the mountain, and in the cities of the plain, and in the cities of the south: for I will turn their captivity.}{32:44}{Men will buy fields for money, sign the deeds, seal them, and call witnesses, in the land of Benjamin, and in the places around Jerusalem, in the cities of Judah, in the cities of the hill country, in the cities of the lowland, and in the cities of the South; for I will cause their captivity to be reversed,” says Yahweh.}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{40}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{40:1}{And the word of the Lord came to Jeremias the second time, when he was yet bound in the court of the prison, saying,}{33:1}{Moreover Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah the second time, while he was still locked up in the court of the guard, saying,}
\VersePair{40:2}{Thus saith the Lord, who made the earth and formed it, to establish it; the Lord is his name;}{33:2}{“Yahweh who does it, Yahweh who forms it to establish it — Yahweh is his name, says:}
\VersePair{40:3}{Cry to me, and I will answer thee, and I will declare to thee great and mighty things, which thou knowest not.}{33:3}{‘Call to me, and I will answer you, and will show you great and difficult things, which you don’t know.’}
\VersePair{40:4}{For thus saith the Lord concerning the houses of this city, and concerning the houses of the king of Juda, which have been pulled down for mounds and fortifications,}{33:4}{For Yahweh, the God of Israel, says concerning the houses of this city and concerning the houses of the kings of Judah, which are broken down to make a defense against the mounds and against the sword:}
\VersePair{40:5}{to fight against the Chaldeans, and to fill it with the corpses of men, whom I smote in mine anger and my wrath, and turned away my face from them, for all their wickedness:}{33:5}{‘While men come to fight with the Chaldeans, and to fill them with the dead bodies of men, whom I have killed in my anger and in my wrath, and for all whose wickedness I have hidden my face from this city,}
\VersePair{40:6}{Behold, I bring upon her healing and cure, and I will show myself to them, and will heal her, and make both peace and security.}{33:6}{behold, I will bring it health and healing, and I will cure them; and I will reveal to them abundance of peace and truth.}
\VersePair{40:7}{And I will turn the captivity of Juda, and the captivity of Israel, and will build them, even as before.}{33:7}{I will restore the fortunes of Judah and Israel, and will build them as at the first.}
\VersePair{40:8}{And I will cleanse them from all their iniquities, whereby they have sinned against me, and will not remember their sins, whereby they have sinned against me, and revolted from me.}{33:8}{I will cleanse them from all their iniquity by which they have sinned against me. I will pardon all their iniquities by which they have sinned against me and by which they have transgressed against me.}
\VersePair{40:9}{And it shall be for joy and praise, and for glory to all the people of the earth, who shall hear all the good that I will do: and they shall fear and be provoked for all the good things and for all the peace which I will bring upon them.}{33:9}{This city will be to me for a name of joy, for praise, and for glory, before all the nations of the earth, which will hear all the good that I do to them, and will fear and tremble for all the good and for all the peace that I provide to it.’”}
\VersePair{40:10}{Thus saith the Lord; There shall yet be heard in this place, of which ye say, It is destitute of men and cattle, in the cities of Juda, and in the streets of Jerusalem, the places that have been made desolate for want of men and cattle,}{33:10}{Yahweh says: “Yet again there will be heard in this place, about which you say, ‘It is waste, without man and without animal, even in the cities of Judah, and in the streets of Jerusalem, that are desolate, without man and without inhabitant and without animal,’}
\VersePair{40:11}{the voice of gladness, and the voice of joy, the voice of the bridegroom, and the voice of the bride, the voice of men saying, Give thanks to the Lord Almighty: for the Lord is good; for his mercy endures for ever: and they shall bring gifts into the house of the Lord; for I will turn all the captivity of that land as before, said the Lord.}{33:11}{the voice of joy and the voice of gladness, the voice of the bridegroom and the voice of the bride, the voice of those who say, ‘Give thanks to Yahweh of Armies, for Yahweh is good, for his loving kindness endures forever;’ who bring thanksgiving into Yahweh’s house. For I will cause the captivity of the land to be reversed as at the first,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{40:12}{Thus saith the Lord of hosts; There shall yet be in this place, that is desert for want of man and beast, in all the cities thereof, resting-places for shepherds causing their flocks to lie down.}{33:12}{Yahweh of Armies says: “Yet again there will be in this place, which is waste, without man and without animal, and in all its cities, a habitation of shepherds causing their flocks to lie down.}
\VersePair{40:13}{In the cities of the hill country, and in the cities of the valley, and in the cities of the south, and in the land of Benjamin, and in the cities round about Jerusalem, and in the cities of Juda, flocks shall yet pass under the hand of him that numbers them, saith the Lord.}{33:13}{In the cities of the hill country, in the cities of the lowland, in the cities of the South, in the land of Benjamin, in the places around Jerusalem, and in the cities of Judah, the flocks will again pass under the hands of him who counts them,” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{40:14}{}{33:14}{“Behold, the days come,” says Yahweh, “that I will perform that good word which I have spoken concerning the house of Israel and concerning the house of Judah.}
\VersePair{40:15}{}{33:15}{{\raggedright “In those days and at that time, \poemline{2}{I will cause a Branch of righteousness to grow up to David.}\poemline{2}{He will execute justice and righteousness in the land.}}}
\VersePair{40:16}{}{33:16}{{\raggedright In those days Judah will be saved, \poemline{2}{and Jerusalem will dwell safely.}\poemline{1}{This is the name by which she will be called:}\poemline{2}{Yahweh our righteousness.”}}}
\VersePair{40:17}{}{33:17}{For Yahweh says: “David will never lack a man to sit on the throne of the house of Israel.}
\VersePair{40:18}{}{33:18}{The Levitical priests won’t lack a man before me to offer burnt offerings, to burn meal offerings, and to do sacrifice continually.”}
\VersePair{40:19}{}{33:19}{Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah, saying,}
\VersePair{40:20}{}{33:20}{“Yahweh says: ‘If you can break my covenant of the day and my covenant of the night, so that there will not be day and night in their time,}
\VersePair{40:21}{}{33:21}{then my covenant could also be broken with David my servant, that he won’t have a son to reign on his throne; and with the Levitical priests, my ministers.}
\VersePair{40:22}{}{33:22}{As the army of the sky can’t be counted, and the sand of the sea can’t be measured, so I will multiply the offspring of David my servant and the Levites who minister to me.’”}
\VersePair{40:23}{}{33:23}{Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah, saying,}
\VersePair{40:24}{}{33:24}{“Don’t consider what this people has spoken, saying, ‘Has Yahweh cast off the two families which he chose?’ Thus they despise my people, that they should be no more a nation before them.”}
\VersePair{40:25}{}{33:25}{Yahweh says: “If my covenant of day and night fails, if I have not appointed the ordinances of heaven and earth,}
\VersePair{40:26}{}{33:26}{then I will also cast away the offspring of Jacob, and of David my servant, so that I will not take of his offspring to be rulers over the offspring of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob; for I will cause their captivity to be reversed and will have mercy on them.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{41}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{41:1}{The word that came to Jeremias from the Lord (now Nabuchodonosor king of Babylon, and all his army, and all the country of his dominion, were warring against Jerusalem, and against all the cities of Juda,) saying,}{34:1}{The word which came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, when Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon, with all his army, all the kingdoms of the earth that were under his dominion, and all the peoples, were fighting against Jerusalem and against all its cities, saying:}
\VersePair{41:2}{Thus has the Lord said; Go to Sedekias king of Juda, and thou shalt say to him, Thus has the Lord said, This city shall certainly be delivered into the hands of the king of Babylon, and he shall take it, and shall burn it with fire:}{34:2}{“Yahweh, the God of Israel, says, ‘Go, and speak to Zedekiah king of Judah, and tell him, Yahweh says, “Behold, I will give this city into the hand of the king of Babylon and he will burn it with fire.}
\VersePair{41:3}{and thou shalt not escape out of his hand, but shalt certainly be taken, and shalt be given into his hands; and thine eyes shall see his eyes, and thou shalt enter into Babylon.}{34:3}{You won’t escape out of his hand, but will surely be taken and delivered into his hand. Your eyes will see the eyes of the king of Babylon, and he will speak with you mouth to mouth. You will go to Babylon.”’}
\VersePair{41:4}{But hear the word of the Lord, O Sedekias king of Juda; Thus saith the Lord,}{34:4}{“Yet hear Yahweh’s word, O Zedekiah king of Judah. Yahweh says concerning you, ‘You won’t die by the sword.}
\VersePair{41:5}{Thou shalt die in peace: and as they wept for thy fathers that reigned before thee, they shall weep also for thee, saying, Ah lord! and they shall lament for thee down to the grave: for I have spoken the word, said the Lord.}{34:5}{You will die in peace; and with the burnings of your fathers, the former kings who were before you, so they will make a burning for you. They will lament you, saying, “Ah Lord!” for I have spoken the word,’ says Yahweh.”}
\VersePair{41:6}{And Jeremias spoke to king Sedekias all these words in Jerusalem.}{34:6}{Then Jeremiah the prophet spoke all these words to Zedekiah king of Judah in Jerusalem,}
\VersePair{41:7}{And the host of the king of Babylon warred against Jerusalem, and against the cities of Juda, and against Lachis, and against Azeca: for these strong cities were left among the cities of Juda.}{34:7}{when the king of Babylon’s army was fighting against Jerusalem and against all the cities of Judah that were left, against Lachish and against Azekah; for these alone remained of the cities of Judah as fortified cities.}
\VersePair{41:8}{The word that came from the Lord to Jeremias, after king Sedekias had concluded a covenant with the people, to proclaim a release;}{34:8}{The word came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, after King Zedekiah had made a covenant with all the people who were at Jerusalem, to proclaim liberty to them,}
\VersePair{41:9}{that every one should set at liberty his servant, and every one his handmaid, the Hebrew man and Hebrew woman, that no man of Juda should be a bondman.}{34:9}{that every man should let his male servant, and every man his female servant, who is a Hebrew or a Hebrewess, go free, that no one should make bondservants of them, of a Jew his brother.}
\VersePair{41:10}{Then all the nobles, and all the people who had entered into the covenant, engaging to set free every one his man-servant, and every one his maid, turned,}{34:10}{All the princes and all the people obeyed who had entered into the covenant, that everyone should let his male servant and everyone his female servant go free, that no one should make bondservants of them any more. They obeyed and let them go,}
\VersePair{41:11}{and gave them over to be men-servants and maid-servants.}{34:11}{but afterwards they turned, and caused the servants and the handmaids whom they had let go free to return, and brought them into subjection for servants and for handmaids.}
\VersePair{41:12}{And the word of the Lord came to Jeremias, saying,}{34:12}{Therefore Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, saying,}
\VersePair{41:13}{Thus saith the Lord; I made a covenant with your fathers in the day wherein I took them out of the land of Egypt, out of the house of bondage, saying,}{34:13}{“Yahweh, the God of Israel, says: ‘I made a covenant with your fathers in the day that I brought them out of the land of Egypt, out of the house of bondage, saying:}
\VersePair{41:14}{When six years are accomplished, thou shalt set free thy brother the Hebrew, who shall be sold to thee: for he shall serve thee six years, and then thou shalt let him go free: but they hearkened not to me, and inclined not their ear.}{34:14}{At the end of seven years, every man of you shall release his brother who is a Hebrew, who has been sold to you, and has served you six years. You shall let him go free from you. But your fathers didn’t listen to me, and didn’t incline their ear.}
\VersePair{41:15}{And this day they turned to do that which was right in my sight, to proclaim every one the release of his neighbour; and they had concluded a covenant before me, in the house whereon my name is called.}{34:15}{You had now turned, and had done that which is right in my eyes, in every man proclaiming liberty to his neighbor. You had made a covenant before me in the house which is called by my name;}
\VersePair{41:16}{But ye turned and profaned my name, to bring back every one his servant, and every one his handmaid, whom ye had sent forth free and at their own disposal, to be to you men-servants and maid-servants.}{34:16}{but you turned and profaned my name, and every man caused his servant and every man his handmaid, whom you had let go free at their pleasure, to return. You brought them into subjection, to be to you for servants and for handmaids.’”}
\VersePair{41:17}{Therefore thus said the Lord; Ye have not hearkened to me, to proclaim a release every one to his neighbour: behold, I proclaim a release to you, to the sword, and to the pestilence, and to the famine; and I will give you up to dispersion among all the kingdoms of the earth.}{34:17}{Therefore Yahweh says: “You have not listened to me, to proclaim liberty, every man to his brother, and every man to his neighbor. Behold, I proclaim to you a liberty,” says Yahweh, “to the sword, to the pestilence, and to the famine. I will make you be tossed back and forth among all the kingdoms of the earth.}
\VersePair{41:18}{And I will give the men that have transgressed my covenant, who have not kept my covenant, which they made before me, the calf which they prepared to sacrifice with it,}{34:18}{I will give the men who have transgressed my covenant, who have not performed the words of the covenant which they made before me when they cut the calf in two and passed between its parts:}
\VersePair{41:19}{the princes of Juda, and the men in power, and the priests, and the people;}{34:19}{the princes of Judah, the princes of Jerusalem, the eunuchs, the priests, and all the people of the land, who passed between the parts of the calf.}
\VersePair{41:20}{I will even give them to their enemies, and their carcases shall be food for the birds of the sky and for the wild beasts of the earth.}{34:20}{I will even give them into the hand of their enemies and into the hand of those who seek their life. Their dead bodies will be food for the birds of the sky and for the animals of the earth.}
\VersePair{41:21}{And I will give Sedekias king of Judea, and their princes, into the hands of their enemies, and the host of the king of Babylon shall come upon them that run away from them.}{34:21}{“I will give Zedekiah king of Judah and his princes into the hands of their enemies, into the hands of those who seek their life and into the hands of the king of Babylon’s army, who has gone away from you.}
\VersePair{41:22}{Behold, I will give command, saith the Lord, and will bring them back to this land; and they shall fight against it, and take it, and burn it with fire, and the cities of Juda; and I will make them desolate without inhabitants.}{34:22}{Behold, I will command,” says Yahweh, “and cause them to return to this city. They will fight against it, take it, and burn it with fire. I will make the cities of Judah a desolation, without inhabitant.”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{42}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{42:1}{The Word that came to Jeremias from the Lord in the days of Joakim, king of Juda, saying,}{35:1}{The word which came to Jeremiah from Yahweh in the days of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, king of Judah, saying,}
\VersePair{42:2}{Go to the house of the Archabin, and thou shalt bring them to the house of the Lord, into one of the courts, and give them wine to drink.}{35:2}{“Go to the house of the Rechabites, and speak to them, and bring them into Yahweh’s house, into one of the rooms, and give them wine to drink.”}
\VersePair{42:3}{So I brought forth Jechonias the son of Jeremin the son of Chabasin, and his brethren, and his sons, and all the family of the Archabin;}{35:3}{Then I took Jaazaniah the son of Jeremiah, the son of Habazziniah, with his brothers, all his sons, and the whole house of the Rechabites;}
\VersePair{42:4}{and I brought them into the house of the Lord, into the chamber of the sons of Joanan, the son of Ananias, the son of Godolias, a man of God, who dwells near the house of the princes that are over the house of Maasæas the son of Selom, who kept the court.}{35:4}{and I brought them into Yahweh’s house, into the room of the sons of Hanan the son of Igdaliah, the man of God, which was by the room of the princes, which was above the room of Maaseiah the son of Shallum, the keeper of the threshold.}
\VersePair{42:5}{And I set before them a jar of wine, and cups, and I said, Drink ye wine.}{35:5}{I set before the sons of the house of the Rechabites bowls full of wine, and cups; and I said to them, “Drink wine!”}
\VersePair{42:6}{But they said, We will on no account drink wine, for our father Jonadab the son of Rechab commanded us, saying, Ye shall on no account drink wine, neither ye, nor your sons for ever:}{35:6}{But they said, “We will drink no wine; for Jonadab the son of Rechab, our father, commanded us, saying, ‘You shall drink no wine, neither you nor your children, forever.}
\VersePair{42:7}{nor shall ye at all build houses, nor sow any seed, nor shall ye have a vineyard: for ye shall dwell in tents all your days; that ye may live many days upon the land, in which ye sojourn.}{35:7}{You shall not build a house, sow seed, plant a vineyard, or have any; but all your days you shall dwell in tents, that you may live many days in the land in which you live as nomads.’}
\VersePair{42:8}{And we hearkened to the voice of Jonadab our father, so as to drink no wine all our days, we, and our wives, and our sons, and our daughters;}{35:8}{We have obeyed the voice of Jonadab the son of Rechab, our father, in all that he commanded us, to drink no wine all our days, we, our wives, our sons, or our daughters;}
\VersePair{42:9}{and so as to build no houses to dwell in: and we have had no vineyard, nor field, nor seed:}{35:9}{and not to build houses for ourselves to dwell in. We have no vineyard, field, or seed;}
\VersePair{42:10}{but we have dwelt in tents, and have hearkened, and done according to all that Jonadab our father commanded us.}{35:10}{but we have lived in tents, and have obeyed, and done according to all that Jonadab our father commanded us.}
\VersePair{42:11}{And it came to pass, when Nabuchodonosor came up against the land, that we said we would come in; and we entered into Jerusalem, for fear of the host of the Chaldeans, and for fear of the host of the Assyrians: and we dwelt there.}{35:11}{But when Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon came up into the land, we said, ‘Come! Let’s go to Jerusalem for fear of the army of the Chaldeans, and for fear of the army of the Syrians; so we will dwell at Jerusalem.’”}
\VersePair{42:12}{And the word of the Lord came to me, saying,}{35:12}{Then Yahweh’s word came to Jeremiah, saying,}
\VersePair{42:13}{Thus saith the Lord, Go, and say to the men of Juda, and to them that dwell in Jerusalem, Will ye not receive correction to hearken to my words?}{35:13}{“Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says: ‘Go and tell the men of Judah and the inhabitants of Jerusalem, “Will you not receive instruction to listen to my words?” says Yahweh.}
\VersePair{42:14}{The sons of Jonadab the son of Rechab have kept the word which he commanded his children, that they should drink no wine; and they have not drunk it: but I spoke to you early, and ye hearkened not.}{35:14}{“The words of Jonadab the son of Rechab that he commanded his sons, not to drink wine, are performed; and to this day they drink none, for they obey their father’s commandment; but I have spoken to you, rising up early and speaking, and you have not listened to me.}
\VersePair{42:15}{And I sent to you my servants the prophets, saying, Turn ye every one from his evil way, and amend your practices, and go not after other gods to serve them, and ye shall dwell upon the land which I gave to you and to your fathers: but ye inclined not your ears, and hearkened not.}{35:15}{I have sent also to you all my servants the prophets, rising up early and sending them, saying, ‘Every one of you must return now from his evil way, amend your doings, and don’t go after other gods to serve them. Then you will dwell in the land which I have given to you and to your fathers;’ but you have not inclined your ear, nor listened to me.}
\VersePair{42:16}{But the sons of Jonadab the son of Rechab have kept the command of their father; but this people has not hearkened to me.}{35:16}{The sons of Jonadab the son of Rechab have performed the commandment of their father which he commanded them, but this people has not listened to me.”’}
\VersePair{42:17}{Therefore thus saith the Lord; Behold, I will bring upon Juda and upon the inhabitants of Jerusalem all the evils which I pronounced against them.}{35:17}{“Therefore Yahweh, the God of Armies, the God of Israel, says: ‘Behold, I will bring on Judah and on all the inhabitants of Jerusalem all the evil that I have pronounced against them, because I have spoken to them, but they have not heard; and I have called to them, but they have not answered.’”}
\VersePair{42:18}{Therefore thus saith the Lord; Since the sons of Jonadab the son of Rechab have hearkened to the command of their father, to do as their father commanded them:}{35:18}{Jeremiah said to the house of the Rechabites, “Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says: ‘Because you have obeyed the commandment of Jonadab your father, and kept all his precepts, and done according to all that he commanded you,’}
\VersePair{42:19}{there shall never be wanting a man of the sons of Jonadab the son of Rechab to stand before my face while the earth remains.}{35:19}{therefore Yahweh of Armies, the God of Israel, says: ‘Jonadab the son of Rechab will not lack a man to stand before me forever.’”}
\end{paracol}
\ChapterHeading{43}
\begin{paracol}{2}
\VersePair{43:1}{In the fourth Year of Joakim son of Josias king of Juda, the word of the Lord came to me, saying,}{36:1}{In the fourth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, king of Judah, this word came to Jeremiah from Yahweh, saying,}
\VersePair{43:2}{Take thee a roll of a book, and write upon it all the words which I spoke to thee against Jerusalem, and against Juda, and against all the nations, from the day when I spoke to thee, from the days of Josias king of Juda, even to this day.}{36:2}{“Take a scroll of a book, and write in it all the words that I have spoken to you against Israel, against Judah, and against all the nations, from the day I spoke to you, from the days of Josiah even to this day.}
\VersePair{43:3}{Perhaps the house of Juda will hear all the evils which I purpose to do to them; that they may turn from their evil way; and so I will be merciful to their iniquities and their sins.}{36:3}{It may be that the house of Judah will hear all the evil which I intend to do to them, that they may each return from his evil way; that I may forgive their iniquity and their sin.”}
\VersePair{43:4}{So Jeremias called Baruch the son of Nerias: and he wrote from the mouth of Jeremias all the words of the Lord, which he had spoken to him, on a roll of a book.}{36:4}{Then Jeremiah called Baruch the son of Neriah; and Baruch wrote from the mouth of Jeremiah all Yahweh’s words, which he had spoken to him, on a scroll of a book.}
\VersePair{43:5}{And Jeremias commanded Baruch, saying, I am in prison; I cannot enter into the house of the Lord:}{36:5}{Jeremiah commanded Baruch, saying, “I am restricted. I can’t go into Yahweh’s house.}
\VersePair{43:6}{so thou shalt read in this roll in the ears of the people in the house of the Lord, on the fast day; and in the ears of all Juda that come out of their cities, thou shalt read to them.}{36:6}{Therefore you go, and read from the scroll which you have written from my mouth, Yahweh’s words, in the ears of the people in Yahweh’s house on the fast day. Also you shall read them in the ears of all Judah who come out of their cities.}
\VersePair{43:7}{Peradventure their supplication will come before the Lord, and they will turn from their evil way: for great is the wrath and the anger of the Lord, which he has pronounced against this people.}{36:7}{It may be they will present their supplication before Yahweh, and will each return from his evil way; for Yahweh has pronounced great anger and wrath against this people.”}
\VersePair{43:8}{And Baruch did according to all that Jeremias commanded him—reading in the book the words of the Lord in the Lord's house.}{36:8}{Baruch the son of Neriah did according to all that Jeremiah the prophet commanded him, reading in the book Yahweh’s words in Yahweh’s house.}
\VersePair{43:9}{And it came to pass in the eighth year of king Joakim, in the ninth month, all the people in Jerusalem, and the house of Juda, proclaimed a fast before the Lord.}{36:9}{Now in the fifth year of Jehoiakim the son of Josiah, king of Judah, in the ninth month, all the people in Jerusalem and all the people who came from the cities of Judah to Jerusalem, proclaimed a fast before Yahweh.}
\VersePair{43:10}{And Baruch read in the book the words of Jeremias in the house of the Lord, in the house of Gamarias son of Saphan the scribe, in the upper court, in the entrance of the new gate of the house of the Lord, and in the ears of all the people.}{36:10}{Then Baruch read the words of Jeremiah from the book in Yahweh’s house, in the room of Gemariah the son of Shaphan the scribe, in the upper court, at the entry of the new gate of Yahweh’s house, in the ears of all the people.}
\VersePair{43:11}{And Michæas the son of Gamarias the son of Saphan heard all the words of the Lord, out of the book.}{36:11}{When Micaiah the son of Gemariah, the son of Shaphan, had heard out of the book all Yahweh’s words,}
\VersePair{43:12}{And he went down to the king's house, into the house of the scribe: and, behold, there were sitting there all the princes, Elisama the scribe, and Dalæas the son of Selemias, and Jonathan the son of Acchobor, and Gamarias the son of Saphan, and Sedekias the son of Ananias, and all the princes.}{36:12}{he went down into the king’s house, into the scribe’s room; and behold, all the princes were sitting there, Elishama the scribe, Delaiah the son of Shemaiah, Elnathan the son of Achbor, Gemariah the son of Shaphan, Zedekiah the son of Hananiah, and all the princes.}
\VersePair{43:13}{And Michæas reported to them all the words which he had heard Baruch reading in the ears of the people.}{36:13}{Then Micaiah declared to them all the words that he had heard, when Baruch read the book in the ears of the people.}
\VersePair{43:14}{And all the princes sent to Baruch son of Nerias Judin the son of Nathanias, the son of Selemias, the son of Chusi, saying, Take in thine hand the roll in which thou readest in the ears of the people, and come. So Baruch took the roll, and went down to them.}{36:14}{Therefore all the princes sent Jehudi the son of Nethaniah, the son of Shelemiah, the son of Cushi, to Baruch, saying, “Take in your hand the scroll in which you have read in the ears of the people, and come.” So Baruch the son of Neriah took the scroll in his hand, and came to them.}
\VersePair{43:15}{And they said to him, Read it again in our ears. And Baruch read it.}{36:15}{They said to him, “Sit down now, and read it in our hearing.” So Baruch read it in their hearing.}
\VersePair{43:16}{And it came to pass, when they had heard all the words, that they took counsel each with his neighbour, and said, Let us by all means tell the king all these words.}{36:16}{Now when they had heard all the words, they turned in fear one toward another, and said to Baruch, “We will surely tell the king of all these words.”}
\VersePair{43:17}{And they asked Baruch, saying, Where didst thou write all these words?}{36:17}{They asked Baruch, saying, “Tell us now, how did you write all these words at his mouth?”}
\VersePair{43:18}{And Baruch said, Jeremias told me from his own mouth all these words, and I wrote them in a book.}{36:18}{Then Baruch answered them, “He dictated all these words to me with his mouth, and I wrote them with ink in the book.”}
\VersePair{43:19}{And they said to Baruch, Go, and hide, thou and Jeremias; let no man know where ye are.}{36:19}{Then the princes said to Baruch, “You and Jeremiah go hide. Don’t let anyone know where you are.”}
\VersePair{43:20}{And they went in to the king into the court, and gave the roll to one to keep in the house of Elisama; and they told the king all these words.}{36:20}{They went in to the king into the court, but they had laid up the scroll in the room of Elishama the scribe. Then they told all the words in the hearing of the king.}
\VersePair{43:21}{And the king sent Judin to fetch the roll: and he took it out of the house of Elisama: and Judin read in the ears of the king, and in the ears of all the princes who stood round the king.}{36:21}{So the king sent Jehudi to get the scroll, and he took it out of the room of Elishama the scribe. Jehudi read it in the hearing of the king, and in the hearing of all the princes who stood beside the king.}
